guzashta roz pemra ki taraf se aik press release mein TV channels ke liye hadaayat nama jari kya gaya hai. jis mein ghair ikhlaqi programon ganoon had se tajawaz ishtiharaat aur ghair mulki mawaad se momanat aur nashriyat ka aaghaz qaumi tarane se karne ki hadaayat ki gayi hai .
mukammal press release ka matan darj zail hai
پیمرانے senate committee baraye it-tila-aat nashriyat virsa ke jari hadaayat nama morkh_h July  ke paish e nazar tamam private TV channels ko hadaayat nama jari kya hai jis mein ghair ikhlaqi programon ganoon aur muqarara hdse zayed asht_hart wagher mulki mawaad korokne ke liye ehkamaat sadir kiye gaye hain .

authority ke jari kardah hadaayat ke mutabiq mandarja zail tarz ke programme Nashar  karne ki sakhti se momanat hogi .

waqai is haadsay ki tehqiqaat honi chahiye. insani pehlu se dekhen to yeh bara ghair mamooli haadsa hai. tehqiqaat ke nateejay mein jo anasir is ke zimma daar nikleen un ki girift honi chahiye aur jo asbaab is haadsay ki bunyaad qarar payen un ka sdِ baab hona chahiye magar is ke sath sath aik aur pehlu se bhi is haadsay ki tehqiqaat honi chahiye. aur is pehlu se jo anasir is ke zimma daar nikleen un ki bhi girift honi chahiye aur jo asbaab is ki bunyaad qarar payen un ka bhi sad baab hona chahiye .

Khurshid  husn ne ibtidayi taleem Gilgit  mein haasil ki. metric mein sri پاتاپ high shool sringr se kya aur shool mein awwal rahay. ghar ka mahol Ilmi  tha aur deen ki taleem bhi barabar ki ahmiyat rakhti thi. mein riyasat mein aik hi siyasi tanzeem national conference thi. qarardad Pakistan  ko awam se muta-arif karanay wali koi tanzeem nah thi. unhon ne kuch aur talib ilmon se jo mutalba Pakistan  ke haami thi se mil kar muslim stodnts union ke naam se مسلما noon tlba ki tanzeem qaim ki. is tanzeem ke aur bhi bohat se baani log shaamil thay .
yeh nisf sadi pehlay ki baat hai behar haal nojawan tlba ki is tanzeem ne waadi Kashmir  mein national conference ki ghunda gardi ke bawajood mutalba Pakistan  ko muta-arif karanay mein bara ahem kirdaar ada kya. Meer  waiz molana Mohammad  Yousuf  Shah  national conference mein shaamil nahi thay. un ki aur un ke aqeedat mandoon ki hamdardian is tanzeem ko haasil theen. Khurshid  husn Khurshid  tanzeem ke baani secretary thay. yahin se un ki siyasi sar garmion ka aaghaz sun-hwa. ba-hasiat taalib ilm aik taraf woh siyasat mein dilchaspi rakhtay thay doosri taraf taleem ke sath ghair nasabi sar garmion mein paish paish thay. aap bachpan se hi mulki mamlaat aur siyasi nasheeb o frazz se aagah rehtay thay .
ﮐﮩﻼﺋﯿﮟ mein aap ne douran taleem hi riyasat ki wahid siyasi jamaat national conference ke matawazi muslim tlba ki p_hnchan ke liye deegar hum khayaal taalib ilmoon ke sath mil kar muslim stodnts union ke naam se aik mo-asar siyasi aawaz uthai. aap hamesha aik numaya taalib ilm rahay aap ke usaatzaa aur khandan hamesha aap ki salahiyaton par Nazaan  raha. zamana taalib Ilmi  mein hi bar e sagheer ke mumtaz siyasi وعلمی shaksiaat se aap ki shanasaai aur qurbat ho chuki thi mumtaz ahal ilm o Danish  dr taseer jaisi barri shaksiaat college ke zamane mein aap ke ustaad aur aap ki salahiyaton ke mutarrif thay. douran taleem hi aap baani Pakistan  hazrat quied Azam  Mohammad  Ali  jinah aur un ki be misaal hamsheerah madar millat mohtarma fatima jinah se shanasaai haasil kar chuke thay .
aap ki salahiyaton aur –apne kaam aur cause se lagan hi wahid wajah thi ke quied Azam  Mohammad  Ali  jinah ki nigah gohar shanaas ne –apne intehai ahem siyasi o niji mamlaat ki zaati tor par dekh bhaal ke liye janab خورشد ko –apne private secretary honay ka aizaz bakhsha is se barh kar aap ki zaat ke liye quied Azam  ke yeh alfaaz ke aaj bhala aur kon sa aisa khush naseeb hai jis ke baais baani Pakistan  hazrat quied Azam  jaisay azeem shakhs ke aisay tareefi alfaaz hon. quied Azam  ki qurbat ke baais muslim league ke tamam rahnma aap ki shakhsiyat aur martabay se aagah thay aur aap ka baja tor par ehtram bhi karte thay is haqeeqat ke bawajood ke qiyam Pakistan  aur Kashmir  ki dharti ki taqseem ke baais aap mohajir honay ke استقاق ke bawajood matdd hukoomaton aur muslim leaguei راہنماؤں ki khwahish ke bawajood kisi qisam ki jaedad allot nah karwai .
baani Pakistan  ki wafaat ke baad madar millat mohtarma fatima jinah ki khwahish numa hukum ki tameel par aap mazeed aala taleem ke liye Bartania  gaye aur numaya kamyabi ke sath barrister ka imthehaan paas kya yun aap ka shumaar Pakistan  aur Azad Kashmir  ke naamwar wukla ki fehrist mein darakhshan hai. janab Khurshid  aik baasol siyasi Mudabbir  aur aala paye ke Danishwer  aur qanoon daan thay masla Kashmir  ki باریکوں aur siyasat ki pchidgyon se bakhoobi waaqif thay aur masla Kashmir  ko jis زوایہ nazar se aap ne dekha guzarte waqt ne hamesha is ki sadaqaton aur zaroraton ko saabit kar diya hai .
ﮐﮩﻼﺋﯿﮟ mein aap ko Kashmir  ki sadarat ki peshkash ki gayi jisay aap ne madar millat mohtarma fatima jinah ke hukum par is mansab ke liye amaada ho gaye aur yun May  ﮐﮩﻼﺋﯿﮟ mein aap azad hukoomat ke saddar banay. aap ki sadarat Kashmir  ki siyasi tareekh mein is lehaaz se ahem maqam rakhti hai ke aap kabhi bhi –apne faraiz mein kisi ki mudakhlat qubool nah karte thay Pakistan  ke aala hakkaam bhi aap se waqt liye baghair mulaqaat nah kar satke thay. aap ki sab se barri khwahish aur siyasi jad-o-jehad ka محورو markaz kasmiri awam ki azadi aur riyasat جموںو Kashmir  ke tashkees ki bahaali tha kash ke Pakistan  ke hukmaran un ki baton par ghhor karte to Shahid  kasmiri qoum is sadme aur jabar se bach nikalti jis ke baais aaj aik laakh se zayed shohada Kashmir  ne apni qeemti jaanun ke نذارنے paish kiye aur aik crore se zayed kasmiri laakh se ziyada Bharti  afwaj ke jabar o tashadud ka nishana banay hue hain .
janab Khurshid  husn Khurshid  ne jo nazriya diya woh tamam aaeni aur bain al aqwami qanoon ki roshni mein yaqeenan aik dors nataij ka haamil falsafah hai magar Pakistan  ki wizarat umoor Kashmir  ke نابالغوںنے usay samajhney mein bohat takheer kar di aur yahi se ikhtilafat shuru ho gaye. janab Khurshid  millat ne kaha tha ke azad hukoomat ko mahraja hari singh ki janasheen hukoomat tasleem karte hue Pakistan  deegar mumalik se bhi is ki hesiyat ko منوانتے hue aqwam mutahidda ka mumbar bnwaye taakay aik azad hukoomat –apne maqboza ilaqa jaat aur –apne hum vtnon ki azadi ke liye mo-asar kirdaar ada kar sakay magar afsos ke aisa nah ho saka اوراختلافات bad گمانیوں mein badal gaye aur yun ئمیں aap ko sadarat se mustafi hona para
Kashmir  mein un ke hum khayaal danishwaron qanoon daano aur siyasi kaarkunon ne un ke afkaar ki roshni mein jammu o Kashmir  lbrishn league ki bunyaad rakhi. janab ke each Khurshid  anthak mehnati insaan thay agar yeh kaha jaye to ghalat nah ho ga ke aap kasmiri awam ke darwaish rahnma thay aap ne kabhi bhi Jah  jalal ki tamanna nah ki nah aap ki barri baradri ke naam Nihaad  rehnuma thay aur nah hi aap ke paas haraam ki doulat ki farawani thi magar is ke bawajood aap ne hamesha khud daari ka be misaal muzahira kiya aap shayar Farzand  Kashmir  allama Iqbal ? ke is shair ki amli tabeer thay .

janab ke. each Khurshid  Kashmir  ke un chand ناموردانشوروں aur siyasi راہنماؤں mein shaamil hain ke jin ki qurbat par insaan hamesha Nazaan  rehta hai. Kashmir  aur Pakistan  mein aik bara tabqa aap ke halqa doastaan mein shaamil hai. aap ki baatein ahal ilm o siyasat ki rahnumaiye ka baais hoten theen aap har dil-azaiz shakhsiyat ke maalik thay barray barray ohdon par Faiz  rehne ke bawajood aap mein taqqabur naam ki cheez nah thi saari zindagi aap ne aam andaaz mein busr ki aur protocol ki bila waja sakhtiyan aur pabandiyan aap ko قطا gawara nah theen. aap ne saari zindagi karaye ke makanon mein guzaraa di halaank aap ke aik isharay par Karachi  Lahore  aur Islamabad mein kayi barri barri aliiiii shaan kothyan aap ke mohajir honay ke istehqaq ke naam par allot ho sakti theen aap ne –apne peechay koi bank balance nahi chorra sala kamyaab qabil fakhr aur rashk zindagi guzaarne ke baad jab March  ko aik aam musafir ko chay mein safar ke douran alamnaak haadsay mein jaan bahaq ho gaye to aap ki jaib se kal rupay ka asasa Bar  aamad sun-hwa aap ke jsd khaki ko intehai ehtram aur shaan o Shaukat  se darlhkomt muzaffarabad laya gaya .

بجرنگی bhai jaan Pakistan  mein dhoom mcharhe hain .
film بجرنگی bhai jaan Pakistani  cinema gharon ki zeenat ban chuki hai .
film ki kahani hindu dharam ke maan-ne walay aik aisay saada looh shakhs pawan ki hai jo –apne aap ko bjrng billi ka maan-ne wala kehta hai .
dil ka itna saaf aur sacha hai ke پرہمن honay ke bawajood zaat paat ka koi khayaal nahi rakhta .
itna reham dil hai ke aik cheh sala Pakistani  musalman bachi ko is ke ghar tak pohanchanay jane ki thaan laita hai jo Bharat  mein apni maa se bhichar jati hai .
kya بجرنگی is bachi ko le kar Pakistan  pohanchana hai ha nahi yahi film ki kahani hai .
Salman  Khan  ne aik seedhay sadhay barhaman ka kirdaar bakhoobi nibhaya hai aur apni pichli tamam filmon se mukhtalif adakari ki hai .
film mein karina Kapoor  ka kirdaar go ke kam hai magar apni bharpoor adakari se unhon ne aik gehra ta-assur چھورا hai .
chay sala bachi Shahida  urf money ka kirdaar ada karne wali child star ہرشالی mlhotrh ki be sakhta aur adakari agay chal kar un ke bara adakar ban'nay ki taraf ishara karti hai .
film mein aik ahem kirdaar Pakistani  reporter chaand nawab ka hai jo kuch saal pehlay apni aik video social media har vayrl honay ke wajah kaafi mashhoor hogaye thay .
yeh kirdaar ubhartay hue kirdaar نوازالدین Siddiqui  ne bohat jandaar tareeqay se nibhaya hai .
chaand nawab Pakistan  mein بجرنگی bhai jaan ki money ko is ke ghar tak pehchane mein madad karta hai .
film go k aik sanjeeda mauzo hai magar is mein dayilag aur adakari ne kahin kahin mazah bhi dala hai .
film ke barjasta jumlay be sakhta adakari khaas tor har بجرنگی bhai jaan ke masomana andaaz mein kahe gaye jumlay film ki jaan hain .
film ki moseeqi mozoon hai. adnan Sami  Khan  ki aawaz mashhoor qawali بھردے jholi ne film
mein aik jazbati rang بھردیا hai .
yeh baat qabil zikar hai ke سلماں Khan  ki is film mein koi item نمبرنہیں hai .
release se pehlay is film ka Pakistan  mein snsr aik bara aysho tha .
magar Pakistani  snsr board ne Kashmir  ke mutaliq chand jumlay hazf karne ke baad is film ko release ki ijazat day di .
film ki khaas baat yeh hai ke film ke jitne manazair Bharat  mein dukhaay gaye hain itnay hi Pakistan  mein bhi dukhaay gaye hain .
dono mumalik ke logon ko watan parast dekhaya gaya hai magar sath hi aik dosray ke liye insaaniyat hamdardi aur dosti ka jazba bhi numaya hai .
is film mein aik hassas mauzo honay ke bawajood Pakistan  ka misbet ta-assur paish kya gaya hai jo ke dono mumalik ke darmiyan dosti ki barhti hui umeed mein aik acha qadam hai .
Salman  Khan  products ke tehat ban'nay wali yeh film Salman  Khan  ki pichli tamam kamyaab filmon se mukhtalif hai .
umeed hai ke –apne mauzo ki wajah se yeh un ki pichli tamam filmon se ziada behtar business kere gi .
zair nazar maqalay mein hum اردوکا aik ghair Maroof  aur kam yab lughat qarar al-lugaat ka taaruf paish karen ge aur is ki ahmiyat aur qader vqimt ka andaza laganay ke ilawa مؤلف ke is daaway ko bhi parkhnay ki koshish karen ge jis mein is ne kaha hai کہقرار al-lugaat Ameer  مینائیکے Maroof  lughat Ameer  اللغاتکی takmeel hai .
qarar al-lugaat aik urdu bah urdu lughat hai. is ka poora naam qarar al-lugaat yani urdu محاوراتہے aur is ke مؤلف syed Tassadaq  Hussain  Shahjehan  poori المتخلص bah قرارؔ hain. qarar al-lugaat aik kam yab lughat hai aur kam hi log is ke baray mein jantay hain. hatta ke is ka ذکرلغات aur lughat naweesi ke mauzo par kiye gaye tehqeeqi o tanqeedi kamon mein bhi nahi milta. sirf dr abbu Salman  Shahjehan  poori aur laila عبدی Khajastah  ne is ka zikar kya hai. qarar al-lugaat ka aik matboa nuskha urdu lughat board ke kutub khanaay mein mojood hai aur راقم ko usay wahein dekhnay ka mauqa mila. nuskha yun to achi haalat میںہے lekin looh aur طباعتی tafseelaat par mabni is ke ibtidayi chand safhaat napaid ہیںچناںچہ is matboa nuskhay se salِ ashaat aur nashir ki tafseelaat ka ilm nahi hota. Albata  board ke karkunaan ne hawalay ki sahoolat ke liye is پرسال taba-at ﮐﮩﻼﺋﯿﮟ likh rakha hai. abbu Salman  sahib ne is ka salِ ashaat nahi diya lekin is ke nashir ka naam gulshane ibrahim لکھنؤ darj kya hai. unhon ne lughat ka poora naam qarar al-lugaat yani urdu mahawraat diya hai .
lughat ke aakhir mein do elanaat hain jo baaz ahem maloomat dete hain. maslan yeh ke qarar Shahjehan  poori yani is lughat ke مؤلف Maroof  shayar munshi Ameer  Ahmed  مینائی ke shagird thay. neez yeh ke qarar ke waalid ka naam syed asghar Hussain  Shah  Chishti  tha aur kitaab ki ashaat ke zamane mein qarar Shah  jahan poor se لکھنؤ aaye hue thay. un elanaat mein se پہلاگویا aik ishtihar hai jo urdu ki mustand kitaaben ke unwan se hai jis میںخواجہ عبدالرئوف Ishrat  lkhnoy ki kitabon ki fehrist hai aur المشتہر ke tehat khwaja عبدالرئوف Ishrat  ihata khansama لکھنؤ darj hai .
dosra elaan qarar al-lugaat ke uqbi sar warq prhe jis mein ittila ki surkhi ke tehat yeh ibaarat di gayi hai
mein ne is kitaab qarar al-lugaat ka haq tasneef kisi ko nahi diya ہیکوئی sahib baghair meri bazabta ijazat ke chapnay یاچھپوانے ka qasad نکریں warna naffa ke aiwz nuqsaan uthana hoga aur hasb zabita harjah o nuqsaan ke deendar hon ge .
al - abad o لمشتہر syed Tassadaq  Hussain  qarar wald syed asghar Hussain  Shah  Chishti  saakin شاہجہانپور warid haal لکھنؤ talmeez hazrat Ameer  مینائی lkhnoy
kitaab ki ibtida mein guzarish ke unwan se aik safhay mein مؤلف ne bataya hai ke koi tees saal qabal un ke ustaad Ameer  مینائی ne nawab club Ali  Khan  wali raam poor ki farmaaish par urdu mahawraat ki janib tawajah mabzol ki thi lekin un ka yeh lughat jis ka naam امیراللغات tha namukammal raha. bqolِ مؤلف Ameer  ke janshinon mein se Hafiz  jallel husn jallel aur phir hakeem Mohammad  zameer husn Khan  dil Shah  jahan poori se umeeden theen ke woh Ameer  ke is kaam ko takmeel tak pouncha kar malik par ahsaan karen ge lekin unhon ne Ameer  al-lugaat ko tamam karne ki himmat nah ki. is ke baad مؤلف ne bakol khud un ke apni na qabliat aur Adam  waqfiyat ke bawajood is kaam ko jon ton takmeel tak pohanchaya. lekin مؤلف ke dil mein yeh khayaal tha ke Ameer  al-lugaat ke tarz par likhna to tedhi kheer hai is liye apni daidh eent ki allag masjid banana chahiye. phir –apne ustaad Ameer  مینائی ka yeh shair darj kya hai
is ke baad bataya hai ke is lughat ka deegar lughaat se kuch andaaz hi nirala hai aur is ki wazahat yun ki hai ke is mein murakkab aur mufrad mahawraat ki tafseel allag allag tehreer ki gayi hai تمامی mahawraat ke har maienay ke saboot mein usaatzaa ke ashaar likhay gaye hain aur aakhrmin مثلیں aur k_havtin bhi darj ki gayi hain .
is ke baad teen safhaat mein un shura ke naam diye hain jin ka kalaam mahawraat ke saboot میںتحریر kya. un mein kuch naam yeh hain امیرؔ مینائی Meer  انیسؔ آتشؔ انشائؔ جرأتؔ جانؔ sahib جلیلؔ mank poori حالیؔ داغؔ ذوقؔ رندؔ رشکؔ ریاضؔ kher abadi سوداؔ شیفتہؔ غالبؔ قلقؔ khud مؤلف yani qarar pandit diya Shankar  نسیمؔ میرتقی میرؔ Meer  حسنؔ مومنؔ منیرؔ shikwah abadi ناسخؔ نوحؔ ناروی waghera .
mulaf ka Ameer  al-lugaat ke baray mein yeh likhna ke takhmeenan tees saal ka zamana sun-hwa nawab club Ali  Khan  ne Ameer  مینائی ki tawajah lughat ki taleef ki janib mabzol karai thi qarar al-lugaat ke salِ taa leaf ke baray mein hamari rahnumai kar sakta hai. hum jantay hain ke alfrd layl ne nawab club Ali  Khan  se urdu ke aik jame lughat ki farmaaish ﮐﮩﻼﺋﯿﮟ mein ki thi اورنواب ne Ameer  مینائی ko lughat ki tayari ka hukum diya. ﮐﮩﻼﺋﯿﮟ mein tees saal jama kiye jayen to گویاقرار al-lugaat ki taleef ﮐﮩﻼﺋﯿﮟ ke lag bhag hui. lehaza saal ﮐﮩﻼﺋﯿﮟ mein taba-at o ashaat qrinِ qiyaas hai .
qarar al-lugaat ka ghaliban aik hi addition shaya sun-hwa. kam az kam hamari maloomat ki had tak is ka dosra addition nahi chhupa. is addition ke kُl teen so solah safhaat hain. yeh addition paanch inch zarb aath inch ke mistar par chhupa hai. har safhay par do column hain aur har column dhai dhai inch chaura aur aath aath inch lamba hai. har column mein tayees strin hain. jaisa ke arz kya gaya safha aik par guzarish aur aglay teen safhaat par shura ke naam hain. panchwin safhay par jahan se lughat shuru hota hai murakkab mahawraat jo Fasih  honay ki wajah se umooman nazam mein istemaal kiye jatay hain ka unwan qaim kya gaya hai. is pehlay safhay par pehla indraaj aabb aabb karna ka hai. maienay diye hain sharminda karna. is ke baad jallel ؔکا yeh shair sanad mein diya hai
is ibtidayi unwan ke tehat mndrj mahawraat safha do so unhatar tak chalay gaye hain aur is hissay mein aakhri indraaj یوہیں hona ka hai aur is ke maienay diye hain isi terhan hona aur sanad mein امیرؔ ka yeh shair hai
safha do so sattar se dosra hissa shuru hota hai jis ka unwan hai tafseel اسمائ Fasih  jo umooman nazam mein istemaal hotay hain. is safhay par alif ke tehat پہلااندراج aasteen ka saanp ka hai aur yeh maienay darj hain khufia dushman. is ke baad bator sanad بحرؔ ka yeh shair diya hai
yeh hissa safha دوسوبیاسی par ekhtataam Pazeer  hota hai jis par aakhri indraaj Yaar ghaar ka hai. maienay yun likhay hain dili dost sacha gham khawar. sanad mein do shair hain. pehlay صفدرؔکا yeh shair diya hai
phir shaad ؔکا yeh shair darj kya hai
safha do so tarasi se teesra hissa shuru hota hai jis ka unwan hai مثلیں aur کہاوتیںجو umooman nasr mein masalaa boli jati hain aur baaz jagah nazam mein bhi istemaal ki jati hain. is mein pehla indraaj aap doobe jug dooba ka hai aur yeh maienay diye hain jab Hamein nah hon ge to kisi se kya gharz. yeh hissa safha teen so das tak jata hai jis par aakhri indraaj yeh mnh aur masoor ki daal ka hai jis ke maienay یوںدیے hain tum is kaam ke Laiq  nahi ho .
چوتھااور aakhri hissa safha teen so gayarah se shuru ہوکرلغت ke aakhri safhay yani safha teen so solah tak jata hai. is hissay ka unwan hai farsi ke jumlay jo مثلوں ki jagah istemaal kiye jatay hain. safha پرپہلا indraaj aabb aamad tayamum barkhast ka hai aur is ke yeh maienay darj hain barron ke agay choton ki nahi chalti. is hissay ka aakhri indraaj jo lughat ka bhi aakhri indraaj hai yak nah shud do shud ka hai aur maienay likhay hain aik bulaa thi doosri aur nazil hui .
is taaruf ke baad hum qarar al-lugaat ke andrajaat par aik nazar daaltay hain ke un ki noiyat avrmayar kya hai
agar qarar al-lugaat ke andrajaat ki tadaad ko dekha jaye to itni kam zakhamat ke lughat mein andrajaat ki tadaad bohat ziyada honay ki tawaqqa ki bhi nahi ja sakti thi neez choti تقطیعکی is lughat mein aik column mein ausatan saat ya aath andrajaat hain jo fi safha اوسطاپندرہ bantay hain aur is ke safhaat ki tadadke paish e nazar is ke andrajaat ki kُl tadaad hamaray mohtaat andazay ke mutabiq saarhay chaar hazaar ke lag bhag ho gi. is mein mufrad alfaaz ko bator bunyadi مفرداندراج jis ko angrezi lughat naweesi ki istilaah mein
maienay mein ziyada wazahat aur tafseel se kaam nahi liya gaya hai aur bil umoom woh maienay hi diye gaye hain jo majazan ya مرادا ya کنایتہ atay hain. lekin is mein bhi nihayat ikhtisaar aur kifayat se kaam liya gaya hai lehaza aksar maqamat par tashnagi ka ehsas hota hai. maslan lafz uuullllu ke sirf aik maienay be waqoof diye hain jo muradi maienay hain lughwi maienay nahi diye. jabkay Ameer  مینائی ka lughat jis ki takmeel ka مؤلف ne iradah zahir kya hai mein allo ke dono maienay yani lughwi aur majazi baqaida allag allag shaqon mein diye gaye hain. Ameer  ne aisay mawaqay par mukhtalif maienay ki shaqon ko number diye hain. Ameer  al-lugaat ki teesri jald mein un nambaron ka bator khaas ihtimaam hai. jabkay qarar al-lugaat ke mulaf ne is taraf tawajah nahi ki. balkay agar kahin aik se ziyada majazi maienay diye bhi hain to unhein aik sath likh diya hai maslan dam dena ke maienay fraib karna jaan dena mohabbat karna kisi shaqq ki nishaan dahi ke baghair aik sath likh diye ہیںاورمعنی ke baad teen Asnad  bhi aik sath likh di hain. ghanemat yeh hai ke yeh teen Asnad  isi tarteeb se darj hain jis tarteeb se maienay likhay hain yani pehlay darj kya گیاداغ ka shair
pehlay maienay ki sanad mein hai dosra shair bhi daagh ka hai jo yeh hai
yeh dosray maienay ki sanad hai. teesra shair Anees  ka hai jo teesray maienay ki sanad mein hai yeh hai
goya yeh tarteeb durust hai lekin asolan maienay shaqq واردینے chahiye اورسند maienay ke foran baad aani chahiye .
qarar al-lugaat ke baaz indraaj maienay ke lehaaz se bohat Tishna  maloom hotay hain. neez jab مؤلف ne lughwi ya haqeeqi maienay ki bjae muradi ya majazi maienay par zor diya hai to usay tamam majazi maienay shaqq waar bayan karne chahiye thay maslan Yaar ghaar ke maienay mein dili dost sacha gham khawar likha hai lekin is ke aik aur muradi maienay yani hazrat abubaker Seddiq  razi Allah  taala anho nahi diye. isi terhan یارغار ke aik aur majazi ya muradi maienay Ashaab kahaf bhi hain aur yeh farhang Asfia  mein bhi darj hain .
baaz maqamat par andrajaat ki Tasweed  mein tarteeb hrofِ tahajji ka khayaal nahi kya misaal ke tor par jhutay mnh nah poochna ke baad jhooti sachhi اوڑانا ka indraaj hai jabkay tarteeb mein jhooti se shuru honay walay murakabat ka indraaj jhutay se shuru honay walay andrajaat se pehlay hona chahiye kyunkay jhooti mein ‫ae Maroof  hai jo lughat mein tarteeb ke lehaaz se pehlay aani chahiye. agar yeh farz kya jaye ke ‫ae Maroof  aur mj_hol ke farq کوبعض qadeem lughaat ke ttba mein is lughat mein nazar andaaz kya gaya hai to phir bhi baat nahi banti kyunkay agla indraaj jhutay ko had tak پہونچانا ka hai aur is mein phir ‫ae Maroof  ki bjae mj_hol hai .
mandarja baala misalon se yeh bhi wazeh hota hai ke مؤلف ka imla –apne daur ke lehaaz se bhi khasay qadeem andaaz ka hai jabkay is muamlay mein امیرؔ bohat mohtaat thay aur un ka imla un ke daur ki had tak jadeed hai. balkay امیرؔ ne imla aur shtِ zabaan ka khaas khayaal rakha hai aur kahin kahin tarjeeh ki wazahat bhi ki hai. qarar ka oodati ko اوڑتی aur be raah qadam uthna ko بیراہ qadam اوٹھنا likhna is ke imla ke usoolon se be nayazi ke saboot hain. مؤلف ke imla ka yeh aalam hai ke woh urdu imla ke is Musalmah  usool ke masdar mein anay wali noon ki مشدد aawaz ko tashdid se zahir nahi kya jata balkay is harf ko do baar likha jata hai ko kahin کہیںنظر andaaz kar deta hai aur maslan kaan dhar ke sunna mein sunna ko suna likhta hai. .
baaz maqamat par Asnad  paish karne mein ahthyat nahi ki gayi jaisay din manana bemani umeedwari karna ki sanad mein safha par aashiq? ka jo shair diya hai woh yeh hai
halaank yeh din manana ki nahi balkay din ko manana ki sanad hai. jabkay mohawra din manana hai nah ke din ko manana aur noor al-lugaat mein isi sanad ke sath mojood hai. نوراللغات ke mutabiq is ke maienay hain din ki tamanna karna. گویامحاورے ke asal alfaaz mein bhi aur mafhuum mein bhi kuch kami reh gayi hai. بظاہرذرا sa farq hai lekin lughat naweesi ke usoolon mein is terhan ke farq ko barri ahmiyat haasil hoti hai. aur waisay bhi mahawray ke alfaaz mein tabdeeli jaaiz nahi samjhi jati .
baaz andrajaat ke maienay mashkook balkay ghalat hain. misaal ke tor par daur ki soojhna ke maienay likhay hain teh کوپہونچنا. lekin Farhang  Asfia  aur نوراللغات میںدور ki soojhna ke jo maienay darj hain un ka khulasa yeh hai ke is ke maienay hain gehra khayaal aana bareek aur nadir baat khayaal mein aana neez daur andesh hona. urdu lughat board ke tareekhi usoolon par martaba lughat mein bhi yahi maienay diye gaye hain. sahib qarar al-lugaat ne sanad mein Ameer  مینائی ka jo shair diya hai is se bhi teh ko pohanchna ke maienay nahi nikaltay balkay Asfia  نوراور board ke lughat mein diye gaye maienay ki tasdeeq hoti hai mulahiza ho
isi terhan qarar ne bazaar ki mithai ke maienay likhay hain aasaan. jabkay is ke maienay Farhang  Asfia  ke mutabiq yeh hain woh cheez jo har 1 shakhs –apne istemaal mein laske kasbi. sahib noor al-lugaat ne Asfia  ke alfaaz ko d_hradya hai. lughat board ne bazaar ki mithai ke maienay yun diye hain woh cheez jo har shakhs ko aasani se mil sakay kasbi tawaif randi. is indraaj yani bazaar ki mithai ki sanad mein مؤلف qarar al-lugaat ne khud apna jo shair diya hai is se bhi aasaan ki bjae jisay har koi haasil kar sakay ke muradi maienay nikaltay hain mulahiza ho
Ameer  al-lugaat mein bhi bazaar ki mithai ke maienay woh cheez jo Ali  al amoom sab ko mil sakay darj hain lekin Ameer  ne is se agla indraaj bazaar ki mithai jis ne payi is ne khayi ka kya hai aur maienay likhay hain mazaaq se کسبیوں ki nisbat kehte hain. goya مؤلف ke nazdeek aasaan aur jisay har koi aasani se haasil kar sakay ke maienay mein koi farq nahi. is se un ki lughat naweesi ki mahaarat ka andaza kya ja sakta hai .
مؤلف ne baaz alfaaz ya murakabat ke maienay yeh dekhe baghair likh diye hain ke aaya sanad se woh maienay bar aamad ho bhi rahay hain ya nahi. misaal ke tor par lafz bazari ke maienay darj hain mamooli. asolan yeh maienay durust hain lekin bazari ke kayi اورمعنی bhi hain. sar-e dast bazari ke deegar maienay ko nazar andaaz karte hue woh sanad dekhte hain jo مؤلف ne apni Danist  mein bazari ke maienay ke liye di hai. سندرندؔ ke shair se hai jis ka dosra misraa hai
halaank yeh misraa bazari aurat tawaif randi kasbi ke maienay mein hai nah ke mamooli ke maienay mein. bazari ke aik maienay kasbi pesha karne wali aurat bhi hain aur urdu lughat board ke lughat mein is ki Asnad  bhi mojood hain. رندؔ ke misrey mein yahi maienay morad hain. darasal رندؔ ne twayfon ki do qasmon yani bazari aur khangi ka mawazna kya hai. khangi ke deegar maienay se qtaِ nazar khangi woh tawaif hoti hai jo parda nasheen ho aur choup kar pesha karti ho. khangi ke yeh maienay Asfia  aur noor dono ne diye hain aur sanad mein dono ne آتشؔ ka yeh shair diya hai
bordne bhi yeh maienay diye hain aur do nasri Asnad  bhi di hain .
phir –apne lughat ko mukhtalif hisson mein mukhtalif anwanat ke tehat taqseem karne ka koi جوازقرار al-lugaat ke مؤلف nahi paish kar sakay hain aur nah hi تمامی mahawraat ki koi wazahat unhon ne ki hai. mojooda soorat میںلغت mein kisi khaas indraaj ko talaash karne mein diqat hoti hai kyunkay baari baari tamam hissay dekhnay parte hain. un marozat ki roshni mein majaburan hamein yeh raye qaim karni padtee hai ke qarar al-lugaat koi bohat mayaari lughat nahi hai. mahawraat ke kuch lughaat is se pehlay mojood thay. مؤلف ko chahiye tha ke un mein kuch izafah karte ya un se kuch ikhtilaaf karte. un ke is kaam se urdu mahawraat ya alfaaz ke zimn میںیا lughat naweesi ke baab mein bohat kam izafah sun-hwa .
Albata  aik maidan aisa hai jis ki wajah se qarar al-lugaat ki kuch ahmiyat samnay aati hai aur woh hai alfaaz ke maeno ke sath shair y mton se استناد .
sheri mton se lughat میںاسناد paish karne ke zimn mein راقم alhrof zaroori samjhta hai ke urdu lughat naweesi ke mauzo par kiye gaye aik ghair matboa lekin bohat vqia aur ahem kaam ka zikar kere. yeh aik maqalah hai jo aik irani Taliba  laila عبدی Khajastah  ne professor dr tehseen فراقی sahib ki nigrani mein urdu lughat naweesi mein adbi zouq ke shawahid ke unwan se tehreer kya tha. maqalay mein unhon ne is amar ka bator khaas jaiza liya hai ke urdu ke kin kin lughaat mein kon kon se shura ke ashaar darj kiye gaye hain aur kin shura ke ashaar ziyada tadaad mein بطورسند aaye hain .
is zimn mein Khajastah  sahibaa ne qarar al-lugaat ka bhi jaiza liya aur is mein di gayi sheri Asnad  ka tajzia bhi kya. unhon ne قراراللغات mein mukhtalif shura ki paish ki gayi sheri Asnad  ko baqaida shumaar kar ke un ki jo tafseelaat di hain woh yahan darj ki ja rahi hain
is fehrist mein jahan baaz barray aur ahem naamon maslan غالبؔ ki Adam  mojoodgi khatakti hai wahan yeh bhi ghhor talabb hai ke baaz shura ki misalein bohat ziyada aur baaz ki bohat kam hain. is ki wajohaat par behas fi al haal hamaray mauzo se bohat daur hai. lekin hum yeh zaroor kahin ge ke مؤلف ne خوداپنے ashaar bator sanad achi khasi tadaad mein paish kar diye hain .
behar haal is lughat mein shaamil baaz Asnad  ahem hain aur kuch to aisi hain ke nisbatan kam Maroof  shura ke kalaam se li gayi hain aur un mein se kuch ka kalaam ab aasani se dastyab bhi nahi. بظاہرایسا lagta hai ke is ke baad taleef honay walay lughaat ke مؤلفین ko bilkhushoos Asnad  ke zail mein is se kuch nah kuch madad zaroor mili hogi lekin tehqeeq aur ameeq mutalay ke baghair is amar ko yakeeni nahi kaha ja sakta. yeh zaroor hai ke urdu lughat naweesi mein istifaday ki riwayat bhi kisi dilchasp tehqeeqi mutalay ka mauzo ho sakti hai .
un Asnad  ki ahmiyat apni jagah hai lekin qarar al-lugaat ki ahmiyat ziyada ترتاریخی hai. usay urdu lughat naweesi ki tareekh mein koi ahem sang e mil qarar nahi diya ja sakta aur is ki janib tawajah bhi is liye mabzol hoti hai ke مؤلف ke bakol yeh Ameer  al-lugaat ki takmeel hai .
مؤلف ka yeh kehna ke unhon ne is lughat ki soorat mein Ameer  ke kaam ko takmeel tak pohanchaya hai kayi wajoh ki bana par durust nahi .
jahan tak امیرؔ مینائی ke naqash-e qadam par chalne ka sawal hai to امیرؔ ka ttba agar مؤلف sahih maienay mein karte to sanad mein apna koi shair nah dete jaisa ke امیراللغات mein امیرؔ ne kya hai. go امیرؔ ki Qadir  alklami se yeh tawaqqa be ja nahi ke woh jis lafz ki sanad chahtay isi waqt aik shair keh kar usay bandh letay. lekin امیرؔ ne bojoh aisa nahi kya .
phir امیرؔ ne lughat naweesi ka kaam jitne barray pemanay par shuru kya tha aur jis terhan is ke liye baqaida daftar aur amlah faraham kya tha is ka ashr Ashir  bhi qarar ke haan nazar nahi aata. امیرؔ ke lughat ki zakhamat ka andaza yun lagaya ja sakta hai ke alif ممدودہ aur alif مقصورہ ke alfaaz Ameer  al-lugaat ki do jldon mein samaaye aur teesri jald sirf bay se shuru honay walay alfaaz par mabni hai. zakhamat aur andrajaat ki tadaad ke lehaaz se kُl safhaat par mushtamil lughat ko Ameer  al-lugaat ka takmala qarar dena ajeeb si baat maloom hoti hai. Ameer  al-lugaat agar mukammal hota to is ki kayi jldin hoten kam az kam aath jldon tak ka mansoobah to Ameer  ke zehen mein tha .
تعداداور مقدارسے qata nazar agar usool lughat naweesi ke lehaaz se dekha jaye tab bhi qarar al-lugaat Ameer  al-lugaat ke معیارسے bohat peechay hai jaisa ke stor baala mein mazkoor sun-hwa. lekin aik achi baat is daaway ke sath yeh hai ke khud مؤلف ko bhi ehsas hai ke yeh Ameer  al-lugaat ki takmeel nahi hai aur woh aik terhan se تکملے ke daaway se yeh keh kar ibtida hi mein dast bardaar ho gaya hai ke Ameer  al-lugaat ke andaaz mein likhna to tedhi kheer hai avrapni daidh eent ki allag masjid banani chahiye neez yeh ke kaha lo phool ki ja pankhari hai .
is terhan hum is nateejay par pahunchte hain ke qarar al-lugaat Ameer  al-lugaat ka takmala to nahi hai aur yeh miqdaar aur miyaar dono lehaaz se Ameer  al-lugaat ko nahi pohanchana lekin is ki baaz Asnad  ahem aur dilchasp hain aur yeh lughat urdu lughat naweesi ke taweel safar mein koi ahem sang e mil nah sahi behar haal aik sang e mil zaroor hai jis ke mutalay se kuch nah kuch akhaz kya ja sakta hai .
kya waqai Iran  Israel  dushman hain ya duniya ki aankhon mein dhool jhonk rahay hain. .

Israel  ke senior tehqiqati sahafi aur musannif
Pakistan  rangers aur Bharti  security force ke darmiyan
Bharti  media ke mutabiq  DG Rangers Punjab  major general Umar  Farooq  ki sarbarahi mein rukni wafad nai dili mein mojood hai jahan Punjab  rangers aur Bharti  security forces ke hakkaam ke darmiyan mazakraat hue jis mein says fire ki khilaaf warzi roknay ke liye nai hikmat e amli tarteeb di gayi jab ke mazeed tafseelaat tay karne ke liye mzakrt mein aik din ki tosee kar di gayi hai. Bharti  media ke mutabiq hakoomati zaraye ka kehna hai ke mazakraat mein dono fariqain ne sarhad par aman qaim rakhnay par aisi hikmat e amli par zor diya jo qabil amal ho .
mazakraat ke agenday ke mutabiq inhen jummay ko mukammal hona tha jis ke baad Pakistan  rangers ko Bharti  wazeer e dakhla se mulaqaat karna thi taham mazakraat mein aik din ki tosee kar di gayi hai jis douran aik khusoosi session jummay ke roz munaqqid kya jaye ga jis mein says fire ki khilaaf warzi ke khatmay aur aman ke qiyam ke liye protocol tay kya jaye ga. Bharti  border security force ke cheif d ke pathk ne aik taqreeb se khitaab mein kehna tha ke baat cheet intehai Khushgawar  mahol mein agay barh rahi hai اورمذاکرات ke pehlay din ki baat cheet par Bharat  mutmaen hain .
doosri janib zaraye ka kehna hai ke Punjab  rangers aur bi s f hakkaam ke darmiyan pak Bharat  border smuggling se mutaliq baat cheet ki gayi jab ke is mauqa par Punjab  rangers hakkaam ne bi s f ki janib se rangers ke jawanoo ki lashain nah uthany dainay par sakht muzammat ki aur ghalti se sarhad paar karne walon ka maamla bhi uthaya. zaraye ke mutabiq rangers hakkaam ne guzashta dinon flag staff meeting mein rangers ke jawanoo ki shahadat aur working baondri par bulaa ishtial Bharti  firing par shadeed ehtijaj kya .
urdu adab ki tareekh mein mashhoor shura ke naam aur un ka kaam is qader ziyada hai ke agar har aik ka naam aur mukhtasir taaruf bhi likhnay betha jaye to hayaat mustaar kam par jaye gi. aur is se bhi mushkil marhala un mein se yeh intikhab karna hai ke kis ko liya jaye aur kis ko chorra jaye kyun ke har naam apni jagah nah sirf yeh ke intehai ahem hai balkay apni zaat mein anjuman hai. is mushkil se niklny ki aik hi soorat hai ke aik khaas daur ka intikhab kar ke is mein paye jane walay shura ka mukhtasir taaruf aur un ke kalaam ke chand namoonay paish kiye jayen. yeh allag baat hai ke kisi khaas daur ka intikhab bhi itna hi mushkil hai jitna ke shura mein se chand ka intikhab mushkil hai .
urdu likhnay bolnay aur is mein nasr o nazam ke maidan mein mashq sukhan karne walay yun to har malik mein kuch nah kuch paye jatay hain lekin is zabaan ka asal watan aur maskan Bar  Saghir  pak o hind hai. aur duniya mein jahan kahin is zabaan ke jan-nay walay aur chahanay walay paye jatay hain un ka khameer bhi isi matti se utha sun-hwa hai un ke islaaf yahin se hijrat kar ke deyaar ghair mein ja basey aur phir wahein ke ho kar reh gaye aur un ki do do aur teen teen naslen wahein jnmin wahein peli barheen aur isi rang mein rangi gayeen .
pak o hind mein se hum taqseem Bar  Saghir  ke baad Pakistan  mein maidan shair mein naam peda kar ke aasman sukhan ke darakhshan sitaron ki hesiyat ikhtiyar karne walay chand shura ke tabsaray par iktifa karen ge .
hamein har gaz yeh nahi bhoolna chahiye ke shayar bhi isi muashray ka hissa hota hai aur is ki رذہنی o fikri rujhan saazi aur rawaiyon ki tashkeel mein muashra is ke halaat aur is ki riwayaat barri had tak assar andaaz hoti hain. aur shayar chunkay muashray ka chasham o dil hota hai aur is ka mushahida baqi logon se ziyada taiz hota hai is liye muashray ke asraat par is ki nazar bhi baqi logon se gehri hoti hai aur phir yeh mushahida is ke kalaam mein jhalakta nazar aata hai kahin is ka aks misbet hota hai aur kahin is masharti amal ka radd amal aur is ki muzammat o muzahmat shayar ke kalaam mein ja baja nazar aati hai .
Pakistani  muashra shuru hi se utaar charhao ka shikaar raha hai is liye is ke shura ke rujhanaat bhi bdalty rahay. ibtida mein to qabal az taqseem wali soch aur andaaz fikar hi shura mein mojo دتھی lehaza wohi klasiki aur qadeem riwayat par mabni shairi hoti rahi jis mein numaya naam shayar qaumi taranah Pakistan  Hafeez  Jullundhri  aur sufi ghulam mustafa tabassum ke hain. yeh agarchay bachon ke shayar ke tor par Maroof  hain lekin un ki ghazal aur deegar Asnaf  shairi mein klasiki rang dekha ja sakta hai .
klasiki rujhan ziyada der chal nah saka kyun ke phir Pakistan  mein taraqqi pasand soch ne zor pakarna shuru kar diya tha. shayad is ki wajah dayen aur baen baazu ki aapas mein nabard aazmai bhi ho. taraqqi pasand tehreek aik waqt mein bohat Maroof  hui thi aur urdu shairi ke barray barray naam is mein mojood thay. chand qabil zikar aur numaya naam jin ki shairi har khaas o aam ke paas yaksaa maqbool hai aur jis ka aitraaf –apne aur paraye sab karte hain un mein Faiz  Ahmed  Faiz  Ahmed  Nadim  qasmi aur Abdul  alhmid Adam  hain. taraqqi pasand rujhan mein aik Ansar  muzahmat ka bhi hai aur un ki shairi mein ja baja is ka rang nazar aata hai .

bano خثعم ke naam nabi sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ne jo khat tehreer farmaya Ibn  Saad  ne is ke alfaaz yeh naqal kiye hain
tum mein se jinhon ne islam qubool kya chahay طوعا kya ho ya karha aur un ke paas khaiti hai
hjri mein bano Tamim  ka wafad bargaah nabwi mein haazir sun-hwa to rasool Allah  sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ke hukum par saabit ban Qais  ansari ne is mauqa par un ke samnay aik taqreer ki jis mein unhon ne kaha
hum Allah  aur is ke rasool ke madadgaar hain. hum is waqt tak logon se laren ge jab tak ke woh Allah  par imaan nah le ayen. pas jo Allah  aur is ke rasool par imaan le aaye ga usay hamari taraf se jaan wa maal ki Amaan  haasil hogi. aur jo inkaar kere ga hum is ke sath Allah  ke rastay mein jehaad karen ge aur is ko qatal karne mein hamein koi taraddud nahi hoga .
رفاعہ ban Zaid  jazami ne nabi sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ki khidmat mein haazir ho kar islam qubool kya to aap ne unhein un ki qoum ke naam hasb zail khat day kar rawana kya
mein ne رفاعہ ko is ki saari qoum aur is mein shaamil honay walon ki taraf bheja hai taakay woh unhein Allah  aur is ke rasool ki taraf dawat day. to un mein se jo agay barheen ge unhein Allah  aur is ke rasool ki jamaat mein shumaar kya jaye ga aur jo log mun phair len to unhein do mahinay ki mohlat hai .
رفاعہ yeh khat le kar apni qoum ke paas gaye to unhon ne un ki dawat par islam qubool kar liya. srd ban Abdul  Allah  ازدی ne apni qoum bano ازد ke aik wafad ke hamrah bargaah risalat mein haazir ho kar islam qubool kya to aap ne unhein un ki qoum ke musalmanoon ka Ameer  muqarrar kar ke hukum diya ke woh –apne ilaqay ke mushriqeen ke sath jehaad karen
srd ban Abdul  Allah  razi Allah  anho ne rasool Allah  sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ke hukum ke mutabiq Yemen  ke ilaqa جرش mein mushriq qabail kamhasrh kya aur unhein islam ki dawat di. phir un mein se jin logon ne islam qubool kar liya unhein –apne sath shaamil kar liya jabkay inkaar karne walon ko qatal karna shuru kar diya. phir aik jungi tadbeer se mushriqeen ko qilay se nikal kar –apne taqub par amaada kya aur palat kar un par hamla kar diya. is jung mein bohat se mushriq maaray gaye chunancha ahal جرش ka aik wafad is ke baad nabi sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ki khidmat mein haazir aur islam qubool karne ka elaan kya .
hjri mein rasool Allah  sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ne Khalid  ban الولید ki qayadat mein chaar so admion par mushtamil aik sarya najran ke qabeela bano al-haris ban ka-ab ki taraf bheja aur kaha ke woh ja kar un ko islam qubool karne ki dawat den aur agar woh teen din tak is dawat ko qubool nah karen to un ke sath qataal karen. Khalid  ne wahan pahonch kar –apne sawaron ko mukhtalif atraaf mein bheja jinhon ne is baat ki munaadi ki ke ya bani al-haris اسلموا تسلموا. is ke nateejay mein bano al-haris ne qataal ki nobat anay se pehlay hi islam qubool kar liya .
is zimn mein bano Aqeef  ke qubool islam ki rudaad bhi barri ahmiyat ki haamil hai. zakheera seerat ki riwayaat se maloom hota hai ke agarchay rasool Allah  sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ne hjri mein Taif  ka muhasra karne ke baad halaat ki munasbat se fi al-waqt bano Aqeef  se jung ka faisla mokhar kar diya taham is muhasray ke douran mein bano Aqeef  par yeh baat achi terhan wazeh ho gayi ke rasool Allah  ki mukhalfat mol le kar jazeera arab mein par aman tareeqay se rehna un ke liye namumkin hai chunancha ashaat islam se khaufzadah ho kar aur –apne muashi mafadaat ke tahaffuz ke liye unhon ne طوعا وکرہا islam qubool karne ka faisla kar liya. hum is shakhs se khauf zada hain. is ne poori sarzamen arab ko roond kar maghloob kar liya hai. hum is sarzamen ke aik konay mein aik qilay mein band hain aur hamaray ird gird islam phail chuka hai. ba khuda agar woh aik mahinay tak hamaray qilay ka muhasra jari rakhtay to hum bhookhon mar jatay. mujhe islam qubool karne ke siwa koi charah nazar nahi aata. warna mujhe khadsha hai ke hamara haal bhi aik din wohi hoga jo mukkay walon ka sun-hwa .
chunancha ahal Taif  ka aik wafad rasool Allah  sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ki khidmat mein haazir sun-hwa aur is ne islam qubool karne ka elaan kya. is mauqa par unhon ne –apne buton ki hifazat aur sharaab zina aur sood ke kaarobar ko jari rakhnay ke hawalay se baaz shartain manwana chahain lekin rasool Allah  sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ne un ko yaksar mustard kar diya. yeh wafad wapas Taif  pouncha to is ke tasurat yeh thay
unhon ne kaha hum aik nihayat darasht aur tund khoo aadmi ke paas se aa rahay hain jo sirf apni mann maani karta hai. woh talwar le kar utha hai aur poooray arab ko is ne zair kar liya hai. log bhi is ke Mutee  ban chuke hain aur romeon par –apne qlaon mein is ka roab taari hai. ab do hi terhan ke log reh gaye hain kuch to apni marzi se is ke deen ki taraf Raghib  hain aur kuch mehez talwar ke dar se itaat qubool kar rahay hain .

keh do ke ae logo mein tum sab ki taraf Allah  ka paighambar hon woh ke asmano aur zameen ki badshahi isi ki hai. is ke siwa koi ala nahi. woh zindagi aur mout deta hai. is liye Allah  par aur is ke rasool par imaan le aao yani yeh nabi ammi jo Allah  aur is ke kalmaat par imaan rakhta hai aur is ki pairwi karo taakay tum hadaayat pa jao .

Allah  taala ne ibtida glandorf to ahal imaan ko un se sirf nazar karne ki hadaayat farmai taham is ke sath sath quran ne yeh bhi wazeh kiya ke islam aur ahal islam ko zuk pohanchanay ke liye yahood ki tamam sazishain aur koshishen be car rahen ge aur woh musalmanoon ke muqablay mein bhi zillat ومسکنت ke isi azaab se dochar hon ge jo Anabia  ki takzeeb ki Padaash  mein un par qayamat tak ke liye lazim kar diya gaya hai. phir aik khaas had tak Afoo  ودرگزر se kaam lainay ke baad surah Maida  ki aayat mein rasool Allah  sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ke khilaaf qataal aur محاربہ ki raah ikhtiyar karne walay tamam garohoon bilkhushoos yahood ki srkobi ke liye nihayat wazeh aur mutayyan Hadayat  day di gayeen. irshad sun-hwa hai
jo log Allah  aur is ke rasool ke khilaaf برسرجنگ ho jayen aur zameen mein fasaad phelanay ki koshish karen un ki saza bas yahi hai ke un ko Ibrat  naak tareeqay se qatal kar diya jaye ya suli charha diya jaye ya un ke haath paon be tarteeb kaat diye jayen ya is sarzamen se inhen jalaa-watan kar diya jaye. yeh ruswai to un ke liye duniya mein muqaddar ki gayi hai aur akhirat mein bhi un ke liye bohat bara azaab hai .
nabi sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ne isi hukum ke tehat bano qareeza ke baaligh mardon ko qatal ki jabkay bano قینقاع bano Nuzair  ahal Khyber  ahal فدک aur ahal najran ko mukhtalif auqaat mein jala watni ki saza di gayi. yahood ke yahi qabail thay jo amlan musalmanoon ke khilaaf محاربہ aur fasaad ka rawayya ikhtiyar kiye hue thay. hjri mein Khyber  ke fatah ho jane ke baad ba-hasiat aik qoum ke un ki qowat toot gayi aur woh fitnah وفساد ki salahiyat se barri had tak mahroom ho gaye chunancha ehad risalat mein Ghazwah  Khyber  ke baad mazkoorah garohoon mein se kisi ke khilaaf amli iqdaam ki zaroorat paish nahi aayi. Albata  surah tauba mein jab mushriqeen se elaan bura t- ke baad un ke qatal aam ka hukum diya gaya to ahal kitaab ke baray mein bhi yeh hadaayat ki gayi ke chunkay woh nabi sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ke دعواے nabuwat ki haikainat wazeh honay ke bawajood aap par imaan nahi laaye is liye un ke khilaaf qataal kar ke unhein mehkoom bana liya jaye aur zillat wa ruswai ki aik alamat ke tor par un jaziya aed kar diya jaye. quran ne wazeh kya hai ke is maqsad ke tehat ahal kitaab ke khilaaf qataal paighambar sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ke maqsad bassat yani izhaar deen hi ka aik laazmi hissa hai. irshad sun-hwa hai
un ahal kitaab ke sath jung karo jo nah Allah  aur yom akhirat par imaan rakhtay hain nah Allah  aur is ke rasool ki haraam kardah cheezon ko haraam samajte hain aur nah deen haq ki pairwi qubool karte hain. yahan tak ke yeh tumahray Mutee  ban kar zillat aur pasti ki haalat mein jaziya dainay par amaada ho jayen. yeh chahtay hain ke Allah  ka noor –apne monhon se bujha den lekin Allah  ka faisla hai ke woh –apne noor ko poora kar ke rahay ga chahay kafiroon ko yeh kitna hi nagawaar ho. Allah  hi hai jis ne –apne rasool ko hadaayat aur deen haq day kar bheja hai taakay usay saaray deeno par ghalib kar day chahay mushrikon ko yeh baat kitni hi napasand ho .
yeh quran Majeed  mein jehaad وقتال ke ehkaam ka asal tanazur hai aur is se wazeh hai ke mushriqeen aur ahal kitaab ke khilaaf qataal ke yeh ehkaam mehez musalmanoon ke difaa aur ahal kufar ke fitnah وفساد ko dafaa karne ke liye nahi balkay Allah  ke deen ki sar bulandi aur shirk ka khtama karne ke liye diye gaye thay. yeh aik muqaddas jung
tum par larna farz kar diya gaya hai halaank woh tumhen napasand hai. tawaqqa hai ke aik cheez ko tum napasand karo jabkay woh tumahray haq mein behtar hai. aur tawaqqa hai ke aik cheez ko tum pasand karo jabkay woh tumahray liye buri hai. aur Allah  jaanta hai aur tum nahi jantay .

Abdul  Allah  Ibn  abbas se riwayat hai ke jab hazrat aisha ne apni londi Bareera  ko azad kya to is ne –apne ikhtiyar ko istemaal karte hue –apne khawand Mughis  se alehadgi ka faisla kar liya jis par Mughis  nihayat ghamgeen thay. Bareera  ne poocha یارسو l- Allah  kya yeh aap ka hukum hai aap ne farmaya nahi mein bas sifarish kar raha hon. Bareera  ne kaha to phir mujhe Mughis  ki koi zaroorat nahi .
. hazrat Khalid  ban الولید se riwayat hai ke rasool Allah  sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ke dustar khawan par goah ka gosht paish kya gaya lekin aap ne usay khanay se guraiz kya. mein ne poocha ke kya yeh haraam hai aap ne farmaya nahi lekin chunkay yeh hamaray ilaqay mein nahi payi jati thi is liye is ka khana mere liye tbaan nagawaar hai. chunancha hazrat Khalid  ne rasool Allah  sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ke samnay goah ka gosht khaya .
mazkoorah dono riwayaato se wazeh hai ke rasool Allah  sale Allah  alaihi wasallam agar kisi ko zaati hesiyat mein koi mahswara den ya apni tabiyat ki bana par koi kaam karne ya nah karne ka faisla karen to ummat par is ki itebaa wajib nahi hai .
doosri yeh ke aap ne sahaba mein yeh mizaaj peda kya ke woh aap ke ehkaam ki illat aur un ka maienay وغرض samajhney ki koshish karen. chunancha aap ka tareeqa yeh tha ke koi deeni ya dunyawi hukum dete hue bil umoom is ki hikmat aur faida bhi bayan farma dete thay aur agar kisi mauqa par sahaba ki nazar hukum ki illat اورحکمت se hatt jati to aap un ki tawajah is ki taraf mabzol kara dete .
. hazrat aisha riwayat karti hain ke aik martaba eid al-adha ke mauqa par aik jamaat maheman ban kar madinah Munawwara  mein aayi. rasool Allah  sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ne logon ko hukum diya ke qurbani ka gosht sirf teen din ke liye zakheera karo baqi sab sadqa kar do. kuch waqt guzarnay ke baad logon ne rasool Allah  sale Allah  alaihi wasallam se arz ki ke ya rasool Allah  hum to apni qurbani ke janwaron se bohat se faiday uthatay thay. un ki charbi pighla kar rakh letay thay aur un ke chamray se pani peenay ke bartan bana letay thay. aap ne farmaya to ab kya sun-hwa logon ne kaha ya rasool Allah  aap ne khud hi to mana farmaya tha ke teen din se ziyada qurbani ka gosht zakheera nah karo. rasool Allah  sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ne farmaya bhae woh to mein ne is jamaat ki wajah se mana kya tha jo maheman ban kar tumhare paas aayi thi. tum qurbani ka gosht khao bhi sadqa bhi karo aur zakheera bhi karo .
. hazrat abbu Saeed  خدری se riwayat hai ke rasool Allah  sale Allah  alaihi wasallam aik mauqa par namaz ki imamat kara rahay thay ke doranِ namaz mein aap ne jootay utaar kar –apne baen taraf rakh diye. peechay namaz parhnay walay sahaba ne bhi aap ko dekh kar –apne jootay utaar diye. jab rasool Allah  sale Allah  alaihi wasallam namaz se farigh hue to logon se poocha ke tum ne kis wajah se jootay utaarey hain unhon ne kaha ke hum ne aap ki taraf dekh kar aisa kya hai. rasool Allah  sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ne farmaya ke mujhe to Jibreel  ne aakar bataya tha ke mere jooton mein gandagi lagi hui hai .
rasool Allah  sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ka sahaba se yeh sawal karna ke tum ne kyun jootay utaarey is par Dalalat  karta hai ke aap ke har har amal ki itebaa lazim nahi balkay yeh dekhna chahiye ke aap ke kisi feal ki noiyat kya hai aur is ki pairwi ummat se matloob hai ya nahi .

Salma  ban الاکوع riwayat karte hain ke Khyber  ke din rasool Allah  sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ne dekha ke aag par kuch ہانڈیاں charhi hui hain to poocha ke un mein kya hai logon ne bataya ke gharelo gadhon ka gosht hai. aap ne farmaya un ko toar do aur gosht pheink do. logon ne kaha ya rasool Allah  kya hum aisa nah kar len ke gosht to pheink den aur ہانڈیوں ko dho len aap ne farmaya chalo aisa kar lo .
. abbu Saeed  خدری riwayat karte hain ke rasool Allah  sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ne farmaya raastoon par mat betha karo. sahaba ne kaha hamaray liye to is ke siwa charah nahi kyunkay hamari guftagu ki mujlisain un raastoon hi mein jamti hain. aap ne farmaya acha to phir jab tum aisi mujlisain jamao to rastay ka haq ada kya karo. sahaba ne poocha ke woh kya hai aap ne farmaya aankh ki hifazat kisi ko takleef nah dena salam ka jawab dena naik baat ka hukum dena aur buri baat se rokna .
. hazrat abbu Huraira  se riwayat hai ke rasool Allah  sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ne aik mauqa par un se kaha ae abbu Huraira  mere yeh dono chappal gawahi ke liye sath le jao aur jo shakhs bhi aisa miley jo dil ke yaqeen se yeh gawahi deta ho ke Allah  ke siwa koi mabood nahi hai to usay jannat ki khush khaberi suna do. abbu Huraira  jab chalay to sab se pehlay hazrat Umar  se mulaqaat ho gayi. abbu Huraira  ne jab unhein yeh baat batayi to unhon ne abbu Huraira  ko zor se dhaka diya jis se woh peeth ke bil gir gaye o ray un se kaha ke wapas rasool Allah  sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ke paas chalo. jab dono huzoor sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ke paas haazir hue aur abbu Huraira  ne shikayat ki to rasool Allah  sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ne hazrat Umar  se aisa karne ki wajah poochi. hazrat Umar  ne arz kya ke ya rasool Allah  aap logon ko yeh khush khaberi nah sunaein kyunkay mujhe khadsha hai ke is se log amal ki janib se be parwa ho jayen ge. aap unhein amal karte rehne den. is par rasool Allah  sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ne farmaya acha theek hai un ko amal karte rehne do .

hazrat aisha farmaati hain ke yeh koi aam hukum nahi hai balkay rasool Allah  sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ne fatima ki majboori ki bana par usay yeh rukhsat di thi kyunkay woh aik weraan makaan mein rehti thi aur is ka wahan rehna khatray se khaali nahi tha .
Bharat  ki parliman ke ewaan zaireen ne raaij qanoon shehriat mein tarmeem ka bil paas kya hai. iss ke nateejay mein Pakistan  Bangladesh aur Afghanistan  waghera ke woh muhajreen Bharti  shehriat ke mustahiq qarar paye hain jo kam az kam paanch saal se Bharat  mein muqeem hain aur jin ka talluq hindu sukh budh jain paarsi aur isaai mazhab ke sath hai. musalman muhajreen ko yeh istehqaq haasil nahi hai kyunkay unhen Pakistan  Bangladesh aur Afghanistan  jaisay muslim aksriyati mumalik sukoonat ke liye muyassar ho satke hain. iss bil mein istehqaq ki bana chunkay mazhab ko banaya gaya hai lehaza isay Bharat  ke secular state honay ke tasawwur ke manafi qarar diya ja raha hai. aِsi terhan iss ki zad musalmanoon par pari hai iss liye unn ki janib se tanqeed aur ehtijaj ka silsila jari hai. iss tanazur mein aik sawal ke jawab mein استاذ graami janab Javed  Ahmed  ghamdi ne –apne usooli muaqqaf ko wazeh kya hai. unn ke muaqqaf ka khulasa darj zail hai .
mein reyaston ke naqal makani par pabandi ke qanoon ko usooli tor par ghalat samjhta hon. mere nazdeek yeh insanon ke bunyadi haqooq ke khilaaf hai. yeh zameen Allah  ki zameen hai aur iss mein sab insanon ko yaksaa tor par rehne ka haq haasil hai. yeh bunyadi insani haqooq mein se hai ke insaan –apne halaat aur zaroraton ke lehaaz se jis khittay mein chahain ja kar rahen avrjs ilaqay ko chahain apna watan banayen. yeh naqal makani baaz halaat mein ikhtiyaari nahi rehti balkay deen ka na guzeer mutalba ban jati hai. agar kisi ilaqay mein Allah  ki ibadat par qaim rehna mushkil ho jaye aur log poori azadi ke sath –apne mazhab par amal pera nah ho saken to imaan ka taqaza hai ke woh ussay chore kar aisi jagah muntaqil ho jayen jahan woh khullam khula –apne deen ka izhaar kar saken aur baghair kisi rukawat ke uss par amal kar saken. aِsi ko quran Majeed  ne hijrat se tabeer kya hai aur aisay halaat mein naqal makani se guraiz karne walon ko jahannum ki waeed sunai hai. irshad farmaya hai
jin logon ki jaan farishtay iss haal mein qabz karen ge ke woh apni jaan par zulm kar rahay thay unn se woh poucheen ge ke yeh tum kis haal mein parre rahay woh jawab den ge ke hum to iss malik mein bilkul be bas thay. farishtay kahin ge kya kkhuda ki zameen aisi wasee nah thi ke tum uss mein hijrat kar jatay. so yahi log hain jin ka thikana jahannum hai aur woh kya hi bُra ٹھکاناہے .
iss waqt dekhieye ke musalmanoon ki jo پرسیکیوشن
sirf iss kaayenaat ka khaaliq hai jo yeh haq rakhta hai ke kisi ilaqay ko khaali kara le ya kisi jagah koi pabandi lagaye. kisi giroh nasal ya qoum ko yeh haq haasil nahi hai. yeh zameen Allah  taala ki hai. yeh uss ne insanon ko di hai. rang nasal mazhab ke har imtiaz se balatar ho kar di hai. woh jahan chahain ja kar rahen. yeh Allah  ka vdiat kardah haq hai jisay koi nahi chean sakta .
yeh bataya jata hai ke insaaniyat ki ibtida africa se hui to iss ka matlab hai ke log hijrat kar ke hi saari duniya mein phailay hain. yeh hijrat agar daur awwal ke insaan ke liye jaaiz thi to aaj kaisay mamnoo ho sakti hai woh log jo qrnon pehlay naqal makani kar ke Australia  ya America  mein abad hue kya unn ka koi istehqaq tha kya woh koi visa ya passport le kar gaye thay jis haq ko unhon ne –apne liye baja samjha uss se woh doosron ko kaisay mahroom rakh satke hain yahi maamla duniya ke deegar ilaqon ka hai. yeh aِsi ka nateeja hai ke baaz ilaqay laq o diq sahraoon ki terhan khaali parre hain aur baaz jaghon par logon ke liye roti kamanay ke zaraye bhi nahi hain. lehaza mere nazdeek bunyadi insani haqooq mein yeh haq laziman shaamil hona chahiye ke kkhuda ki zameen mein naqal makani par koi pabandi nahi lagai ja sakti. aisi pabandi nah rang o nasal ki bunyaad par lagai ja sakti hai nah mazhab aur pidaaish ki bunyaad par aur nah iss bunyaad par ke koi kisi ilaqay mein kitney arsay se abad hai. naqal makani ke bunyadi haq par yeh pabandi zamana haazir ki qaumi reyaston ka jabar hai. daur jadeed ki har riyasat iss جبرکی murtakib hai. bunyadi insani haqooq ke khilaaf yeh qaumi reyaston ka ijtimai zulm hai jis se nijaat ke liye insaaniyat ko bharpoor jad-o-jehad karni chahiye .
iss usooli baat ke baad ab dekhieye ke jadeed qaumi riyasat ke tasawwur mein yeh usool tasleem shuda hai ke shehriat ki asaas geographiya ho ga. yani aik mutayyan khatta arz ko malik kaha jaye ga aur uss ke bashinday uss ke shehri kehlayen ge. shehriat ke haqooq sab bashindon ke liye yaksaa hon ge aur unn mein rang nasal zabaan aur mazhab ki bunyaad par koi tafreeq ya taqseem nahi ho gi. ab Bharat  agar aik jadeed qaumi riyasat hai to uss ka shehriat dainay mein mazhab ko bunyaad banana uss bunyadi usool ke khilaaf hai jis par jadeed qaumi riyasat qaim hai. yani awwal to aap ko iss jagah par kharray hona chahiye tha ke agar deegar mumalik ke log zulm پرسیکیوشن haq talfi aur shehriat ke Musalmah  haqooq ki pamali ka shikaar ho kar hamaray paas atay hain to hamaray darwazay unn ke liye khulay hon ge aur hum unhen barabar ke shehri haqooq dainay ke liye tayyar hon ge. agar aap iss jagah par kharray nahi ho sakay to kam se kam uss maqam se to nah htte jahan daur jadeed ki qaumi riyasat khari hai. agar aap ne kuch logon ko shehriat dainay ka faisla kar liya tha to phir uss ke radd o qubool ki bana mazhab ko hargiz nahi banana chahiye tha kyunkay yeh qaumi riyasat ke uss tasawwur ke manafi hai jis par Bharat  ki saltanat qaim hai .
qaumi riyasat ke tasawwur mein yeh misbet baat behar haal mojood thi ke woh rang nasal aur mazhab ke bjae jghrafie ko shehriat ki bunyaad banata tha. yeh aِsi bunyaad par qaim rehta to tab bhi duniya ke liye kisi had tak rehmat tha ke chalein kam az kam duniya mein kuch aisay khittay wujood mein aagaye hain jahan insaan rang nasal aur mazhab ki tafreeq se balatar ho kar qomiat haasil kar letay hain. ab agar yeh cheez bhi baqi nahi rehti to qaumi riyasat ki yeh mehdood ifadiyat bhi qaim nahi rahay gi jo iss ki baqa ki zamin hai .
mere nazdeek reyaston ke aisay iqdamaat zulm o adwan par mabni hain. yeh bunyadi insani haqooq ke bhi manafi hain aur jadeed qaumi riyasat ke tasawwur ke bhi khilaaf hain. hum musalmanoon ko inn par aazurda honay ke bjae aur qaumi Hamiyat  ka naara laganay ke bjae yeh usooli muaqqaf ikhtiyar karna chahiye ke duniya mein jahan bhi پرسیکیویشن ho gi woh khuwa musalmanoon ke khilaaf ho ya kisi aur qoum ke khilaaf hum uss ki muzammat karen ge aur uss ke khilaaf aawaz uthayen ge. ae kash ke hamari musalman hukoomaton ko ------ jin ke darwazay musalmanoon par bhi band hain ------ kkhuda yeh tofeq day ke woh yeh elaan kar den ke duniya mein jahan پرسیکیوشن ho jahan zulm o zayad-ti ho jahan jung o jadal ka bazaar garam ho jahan insani haqooq ko pamaal kya jaye jahan logon ko sataya jaye aur unn ki shehriat ki nifi ki jaye wahan ke logon ke liye hamaray darwazay khulay hain. woh ayen aur hamari sarzamen ko apna watan banayen. Pakistan  ko aِsi maqam par kharray hona chahiye. malaysia Saudi  arab khaleeji reyaston aur deegar musalman mumalik ko yahi position ikhtiyar karni chahiye .
