Anabia  ki zindagi husool sabr ke liye hamaray liye Uswah  hai. un ki daastaa’n ہاے hayaat –apne andar hamaray liye aisi misalein rakhti hain ke jin se hamein hosla haasil hota aur baseerat mein izafah hota hai. yahan aisa mauqa nahi ke hum un waqeat ki tafseel likhain taalib is ke liye un سیرتوں ke mutalea ko paish e nazar rakhay .
un ki taseer quran ke jaisi to nahi hai مگرہمیں yeh faida zaroor deti hai ke un se hamein insani zindagi ki misalein aur is mein sabr ke atlaqat ko samajhney mein madad miley gi. Anabia  se hamari mohabbat hamaray dilon mein chunkay aik taqaddus sa peda karti hai jis wajah se un ke waqeat agar sahih hon to woh bohat hi ziyada mo-asar ban jatay hain. magar yahan aik baat wazeh kardoon ke waqeat se deen akhaz nahi karna chahiye bas yeh cheez dekhni chahiye ke neki karne mein un ka rawayya kya tha. deen ka maakhuz quran aur sunnat hain. qissay kahaniyan nahi. is liye ke qissay kahaniyan mehfooz hathon se hum tak nahi puhanche. un mein logon ne bohat kuch apni taraf se mila diya hai. is liye ab woh haq aur baatil dono ka majmoa hain .
quran Majeed  ne nabi sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ke daur ke بدووں mein munafqat ko khatam karne ke liye unhein yeh mahswara diya ke
yahan Albata  aik imkaan is baat ka hai ke aap aisay aadmi ka intikhab kar len ke jo Sadiq  nah ho. is cheez se bachney ke liye zaroori hai ke aap pehlay quran ke sath oopar bayan kardah talluq mutalea qaim kar chuke hon. wagerna har anay wala aap ko –apne bahao mein baha le jaye ga. is liye ke pehchanta nahi hon abhi rahabar ko mein wali haalat aap ko har raah ro ke peechay laga di gi. quran ka tarjuma baar baar parhnay se woh zehen ban jaye ga ke woh aap ko is mushaqqat se bachalay ga ke aap har aadmi ki baat ke peechay lag jayen .
sabr ke hawalay se har tabqa mein mukhtalif p_hlvon se be sabri ya bardasht payi jati hai. maslan Mutwast  tabqay ki aurat ghar ke kaam kaaj nah kere to yeh na qabil bardasht hai. aur aylit class ki aurat kaam karna aar samjhti hai aur agar woh kar le to yeh bara karnaama hai. is tarbiyat se jo har tabqa –apne logon ki karta hai mukhtalif tabqaat mein mukhtalif ravayye wujood pazeer hotay hain. aik dehati ghareeb khandan ke log shayad aik roti ke tukre par لڑپڑیں. magar woh ho sakta hai ke tufaan anay par aaraam se –apne ghar ko girtay hue dekhte rahen .
is se yeh baat maloom hui ke barray pemanay par aisi tarbiyat sabr ke paida karnay ka sabab ban sakti hai. har khandan ke sarbarah ko –apne ghar mein tarbiyat ka mahol banana chahiye. jazbaat ko kaisay control kya jata hai. un ka izhaar kab hona chahiye waghera jaisi baatein har ghar ko –apne mahol mein taaza rakhni chahiye .
misaal ke tor par hamaray اکثرلوگوں ki yeh tarbiyat hi nahi ki jati ke kisi ka mazaaq ura dena is par koi tabsarah sa kar dena kitni buri baat hai. hamaray haan aam tor se yeh bemari har jagah dekhnay ko miley gi. logon ki mazoori par un ke naam tak par jayen ge. is terhan ki cheeze ہادم sabr hain. is liye ke un ka aam hona takleef ka baais hai. yeh takleef intiqam par abharti hai aur maashr y mein phir talkhiyan wujood pazeer hoti hain. yeh talkhiyan chughli gheebat waghera par abharti hain aur insaan aahista aahista haq ke jadah mustaqeem se hathta jata hai .
is maqsad ke liye hamaray paish e nazar aik tarbiyat gaah ka qiyam bhi hai. jis mein hum yeh chahtay hain ke aik barray pemanay par logon ko aisi taleem se guzaraa jaye ke un ke ghalat buut toot jayen aur sahih aqaed aur nazriaat wujood mein ayen. un ko mohazab insaan banaya jaye. un ke kirdaar o seerat ko sanvara jaye .
is baab mein hum woh ahem cheeze zair behas layein ge jo hamein sabr karne mein hamaray liye Maney  hoti hain .
tawakkal Allah  par –apne mamlaat ko daal kar is ke faislon par mutmaen rehne ka naam hai. jis aadmi mein tawakkal nahi ho ga woh sabr nahi kar sakay ga. is liye ke kkhuda par bharosa hi woh sahara hai jis se nafs mushkilaat mein mutmaen rehta hai. رضیت billah rubaa ki manzil jis ne pa li ho woh mushkilaat mein ghabrata nahi. is ne darasal aisi mazboot cheez کوتھام rakha hai ke jo usay har is waqt thaamay rakhti hai jab is ke qadam dagmaghanay lagtay hain .
Allah  hamaray baray mein faisla karte waqt kabhi hamein mushkil se do chaar karte hain aur kabhi aasani se. un dono terhan ke faislon mein –apne mamlaat ka wali vras Allah  ko samjhna aur is ki Raza  par qaim rehne ki koshish karna hi woh cheez hai jis کوہم tawakkal kehte hain. yahi cheez darasal sabr ki sab se barri مؤیدو Muawin  hai. kyunkay imaan billah mein aslan matloob yeh hai ke qul aamnt billah sm استقیم is baat ke qaail ho jao ke mein imaan laya aur phir is par qaim raho .
kkhuda ki zaat a seen duniya mein har neki ke liye aik بڑاسہارا hai. is ke inkaar aur is par be itmadi ki bana par shayad hi koi shakhs neki par qaim reh sakay. kkhuda par aetmaad darasal be aqli aur andhay aitqaad se peda nahi hota balkay is ke liye kkhuda par socha samjha imaan is ki zaat کاتعارف is ki sifaat o sunan ka ilm na guzeer hai. agar yahan par ghalti ho gayi to aadmi waqtan foqatan sabr se mahroom hota rahay ga. maslan baaz log yeh khayaal karte hain ke neki karen ge to hum par museebat nahi aaye gi. yeh kkhuda ke baray mein is ki sunan ka ghalat ilm hai. Allah  taala ne yeh duniya inaam ke liye nahi banai balkay aazmaysh ke liye banai hai. is mein kisi neki ka laziman ajar dena neki ke baray mein aisi Daleel  ban jana hai ke jis ke baad aazmaysh aazmaysh nahi rehti. kkhuda ne neki ko bas aik umomi sa ghalba day rakha hai jo is kaayenaat ke qaim بالخیر honay ki Daleel  hai magar yeh lazim nahi hai ke kisi fard ki neki ke baad is par koi aazmaysh nahi aaye gi. Anabia  ki zindagi is ki behtareen misaal hai. yeh log masoom an الخطا thay magar un par museebat ke aisay aisay pahar tootay hain ke quran ke mutabiq rasool aur is ke saathi pukaar uthte rahay ke madad kab aaye gi
woh aadmi jo neki is liye kar raha tha ke is par koi museebat nahi aaye gi. jab is par kkhuda ki koi aazmaysh aaye gi to woh aik taraf to yeh ke kkhuda se mayoos hoga aur doosri taraf nakiyon ko bhi fuzool samajte hue tark kar day ga. sabr to daur ki baat hai neki ka naam bhi shayad is ke liye fuzool hoga. is terhan ke log hamaray muashray mein bohat hain jinhon ne kaarobar ki behtari ke liye namaz roza shuru kya magar faida nah pa کردین se بددل hue .
is liye lazim hai ke quran ki roshni mein Allah  ki sifaat ko samjha jaye aur is ki roshni mein zindagi busr ki jaye. yeh lazim hai wagerna aahista aahista aap ke dil se imaan nikalta jaye ga .
un logon ko umooman be sabr aur jazbati dekha gaya hai jo kkhuda ko sahih tasawwur ke sath nahi jantay. maslan baaz kkhuda ko yun samajte hain jaisay navz billah koi rishwat lainay wala ho idhar aap ne neki ki rishwat di idhar woh raam ho gaya. halaank kkhuda be niaz aur ghair mohtaaj hai. usay agar zaroorat ho bhi to woh خودہر shai bana sakta hai. usay hamari ibadat o riyazat ki zaroorat nahi hai. hum un sha Allah  isi silsila Mualim  السبیل ke zimn mein aik kitaab Allah  kon hai ke naam se tehreer karen ge. jis mein Pakistani  musalmanoon ke kkhuda ke baray mein ghalat khayalat ki islaah ho gi aur un ko woh maloomat milein ge jo zindagi ko sahih maienay mein guzaarne ke liye zaroori hain .
kkhuda is duniya mein ijtimaiyat ko neki ka ajar laziman deta hai. maslan agar koi qoum –apne andar ijtimai satah prhq ko qaim kar layte hai to is se is mein kkhuda ki naematain waafar milnay lagen gi aur doosri aqwam mein is ka sir ouncha ho ga. lekin aik fard ke sath Allah  ka maamla yun nahi hai. is ki nakiyon ka ajar usay sirf akhirat mein miley ga. yahan bas Allah  usay itna hi den ge jitna is ne is ke liye likh rakha hai. neki karne se duniya mein ajar sirf yeh hai ke is se muashrat mein kher zindah rehta aur pnpta hai. lekin yeh lazim nahi hai ke usay duniya mein اجرملنے lagey. yeh isi soorat mein lazim hota hai jab akhirat mein is ka koi hissa nah ho .
Allah  ki Raza  ke bajaye hamara mtmh nazar agar yeh ban jaye ke hum ne duniya walon ko khush karna hai aur hum neki karen to log bhi is ke jawab mein hamaray sath neki karen yeh cheez bhi ہادم sabr hai. is liye ke aap har waqt neki par qaim nah reh saken ge jab log aap ke sath aap ki tawaqqa ke mutabiq paish nahi ayen ge. khud yeh cheez bhi koi neki nahi hai ke aap duniya mein sila o ajar ke liye neki karen. asal matloob yeh hai ke aap Allah  ki Raza  ke liye neki karen taakay aap agay ki tawaqqa mein duniya se be niaz rahen. aur yeh be nayazi یقینازیادہ baais ajar aur hosla o taqwiyat ke liye bohat mufeed hai .
quran مجیدنے hajj ko jane walay do garohoon ka zikar kya hai aik woh jo duniya ke liye hi safar karte hain aur dosray woh jo akhirat ki Falah  ke liye safar karte hain aur Allah  se duniya mein kher aur bhalai ke taalib rehtay hain. yahi dosray log hi asal mein saabit qadam log hain. unhein duniya mein ajar panay ki tawaqqa chunkay nahi ho ti woh akhirat ke liye amal kar rahay hotay hain is liye agar kahin gurbat o tang dasti satati bhi hai to un ki nakiyon mein ازدیاد hi ka baais banti hai .
sahaba ke baray mein aata hai ke jab jung ka mauqa aata to un ke imaan mein izafah hota magar munafiqeen jin ki nazar dunewi Manfiat  par lagi rehti hai woh is se ghabra te aur is zahiri imaan se bhi haath dho baithtay jis ke saharay par woh musalmanoon ki saf mein shaamil hue hotay thay. theek yahi haalat duniya mein taalib ajar ki hai jaisay hi Manfiat  khatam hoti hai to woh neki se haath dho baithtay hain. hum aap ko yeh koshish karni hai ke hamesha –apne andar is muharrak amal ko zindah rakhen ke hamein Allah  ki Raza  ke liye kaam karna hai. yahi cheez ind Allah  baais ajar hai aur isi se aima noon o amal mein sabr o istiqamat aati hai .
quran Majeed  mein be shumaar mawaqay par sabr ujlat ke متضادمعنی mein aaya hai. hum jin mawaqay par ujlat ka shikaar ho jatay hain wahan bil umoom be sabri dikhata hain. hum yeh chahtay hain ke idhar hum dua karen aur idhar poori ho jaye. isi terhan kisi se koi taqaza ho koi kaam nikalna ho jab hum jaldi mein par jayen to be sabri ki khata sarzad ho ti hai. maslan hamaray kisi bhai ne koi ghalat baat hum se mansoob kar di to hum foran is se intiqam lainay ki koshish karte hain. halaank pehlay lazim hai ke hum yeh jaanen ke baat kya hai kis ne kahi hai hamein ghalat baat to nahi pohanchi. ya isi terhan kkhuda ki taraf se jo museebat aur gham nazil sun-hwa hai woh jaldi nah talnay par hum mayoos ho jatay hain halaank ho sakta hai ke is mein hamara hi qasoor raha ho. parhaiz aur hifzaan sehat ka hum khayaal nah rakhen aur khayaal karen ke Allah  hum se naraaz ho gaya hai. is ne mujhe hi is museebat ke liye chunn liya hai. waghera .
–apne andar se aisay داعیات ko qaboo mein rakhna chahiye jo hamein ujlat mein mubtala karte hain. maslan hiras tama gussa nafrat aur ghirmtwazn mohabbat waghera un داعیات mein se hain jo insaan ko ujlat mein daal dete hain. chunancha yeh ujlat hum se aisay aqdama t- kraditi hai ke hum moaqqaf kher o haq se hatt jatay hain. kisi ko maarna zulm karna kkhuda ki hudood se متجاوز hona yeh sab phir wujood mein aata hai .
sabr ko nuqsaan pohanchanay walay umoor mein se aik cheez yeh bhi hai ke hamein har maamla ki haqeeqat ka ilm nahi hota. hum is ke bohat saaray p_hlvon se nawaqif hotay hain. is wajah se hum gussa mein asaktay hain agar hamein is ki haqeeqat ka ilm ho jaye to hamein nah itna dukh ho aur nah itni be sabri hi peda ho. yeh aam tor se dekha gaya hai ke jab koi اتنہائی takleef ke baad wafaat paata hai to log bil umoom yeh kehte hain shukar hai ke is ki takleef se ja noon chhuut gayi. halaank wohi aadmi agar haalat sehat mein duniya se rukhsat hotato unheen logon ka bain kayi din jari rehta .
wafaat panay walay bemaar ki is takleef ka hamein ilm hota hai magar aisi bohat si takaleef mushkilaat aur mamlaat hotay hain jo hamaray liye parda ghaib mein hotay hain. un ka posheeda rehna khud hamaray bhallay ke liye hota hai. jaisay waqea moose o khizar mein kuch cheeze ghaib ki aap alaihi salam par khol di gayi hain jo hum par bil umoom ghaib mein rehti hain. hamein nahi maloom hota ke marnay walay ko kis azaab se bacha liya gaya hai. woh kon si mushkil mein parney wala tha ya woh kya kar guzarnay wala tha waghera .
quran ne qissa khizar suna kar hamein yahi baat sikhayi hai ke hadsaat bhi –apne batan mein kher ke haamil hotay hain. duniya mein koi cheez bhi الل tup nahi ho rahi hoti. har cheez aik qaiday zaabtay aur hikmat Ellahi ke tehat aur isi ke azan se ho rahi hoti hai. woh jis cheez ko wujood bakhshta hai woh aazmaysh samait kayi qisam ke kher wujood pazeer karti hai .
isi ki roshni mein hamein yeh bhi maloom rehna chahiye ke kkhuda ke mamlaat ki terhan duniya mein insanon ke mamlaat mein se bhi besh tar parda ghaib mein hotay hain. kisi ke dil ke khayalat is ke muharikaat aur dabey jazbaat ka sahih idraak hamaray liye mumkin nahi hota. hum uthte hain aur naraaz ho jatay hain halaank dekhna yeh chahiye ke maamla kaisa hai kyun sun-hwa hai. mere sath aik maamla aisa sun-hwa ke jis se mujh par zindagi ki kayi ghirhein khulein. mujh se mere aik shagird ne meri aik kitaab ke baray mein poocha ke kahan se li hai. mein ne is se kaha ke yeh mujhe kisi ne tohfa diya hai. aik aur shagr daal ne isi kitaab ke baray mein poocha ke yeh kitaab kitney ki li hai. mein ne kaha paanch so rupay ki. dosray jawab se yeh ta-assur mil raha hai ke shayad yeh kitaab mein ne khud kharidi hai. un dono shagrdon se kisi mauqa par jab baat hui to unhein laga ke shayad mein ne jhoot bola hai. chunancha kuch arsa tak yeh baat un ke dilon mein chhupi rahi magar kisi mauqa par unhon ne is ki wazahat talabb karli to mein hanse baghair nah reh saka. is liye ke dono jumlay sach bhi hain aur aisay bhi hain ke mutazaad dikhayi dete hain. mein ne un se kaha ke yeh poochnay ka amal tum ne bohat acha kya hai. darasal mein aur mera aik dost bazaar mein thay ke yeh kitaab is ne mujhe khareed کرتحفہ di. ab chunkay mere samnay hi kharidi gayi thi is liye mujhe qeemat ka bhi ilm tha. is liye jis ne mujh se qeemat poochi is ko mein ne qeemat btadi. lekin qeemat bitanay se un ko yeh laga ke shayad mein ne khud kharidi hai. jabkay mein ne dosray shagird ko bataya tha ke mujhe yeh tohfa mein mili hai .
is waqea se yeh haqeeqat mujh par khuli ke duniya mein kitney hi aisay sach hon ge jin par jhoot ka gumaan sun-hwa ho ga jin se laraiyan aur ناچاقیاں wujood mein aayi hon gi. kitney hi kaam neki ki niyat se kiye gaye hon magar buray lagnay ki wajah se buraiee shumaar kar liye gaye hon ge. kitney hi mohabbat ke bol hon ge jin mein nafrat ko mehsoos kya gaya hoga kitney hi naseehat ke jumlay hon ge jin ko mehez naqad o aitraaz ke maienay mein liya gaya hoga. kitni hi imdaad ki koshishen hon gi jin ko ahsaan karne ke mafhuum mein liya gaya hoga. kitney hi munsifana faislay hon ge jin ko janib daari ke maienay mein liya gaya ho ga. gharz yeh aik haqeeqat hai ke yeh duniya ghaib ہاے gona gon ka majmoa hai. jis ki haqeeqat qayamat hi ko khulay gi. ya kuch un logon par jo quran mein surah حجرات ke hukum ke mutabiq koi iqdaam karne se pehlay tehqeeq kar liya karte hain .
is tafseel se hamein yeh baat maloom hui ke be صبرے honay ke bajaye koshish karni chahiye ke jin mamlaat se hamein ranj o takleef pohanchi hai un ki haqeeqat jan-nay ki koshish karen شایدوہ haadsa haadsa nah ho balkay aik khush gawaar amal ho jo hamaray liye bohat se kher –apne hamrah laa raha ho .
duniya mein mamlaat karte waqt hamein sabr se hataane wali aik cheez yeh bhi hai ke hum doosron ke haqooq ka sahih shaoor nahi rakhtay aur un ko ahmiyat dete hain. dosray bhi insaan hain un ke bhi ehsasat o jazbaat hain woh bhi ghalti kar satke hain. un ke sath bhi dunewi zaroriat lagi hain. un ke bhi biwi bachay aur mushkilaat hain un ke andar bhi tamannaon ke samandar hudood shikni ko be taab hain. dosray se maamla karte waqt hamesha un umoor ka khayaal rakhen ke woh bhi hamari terhan un cheezon se dochar hain .
naqad o islaah aur Tadeeb  o tanbeeh mein hamesha is baat ko khayaal mein rakhen ke hamein aik insaan se maamla hai. baaz log –apne mulazmeen aur mathton ke sath aisa sulooq karte hain ke jaisay bhallay log janwaron ke sath bhi nahi karte .
isi terhan lain deen aur dosray mamlaat mein bhi hum hamesha hudood se na aashna rehtay hain. nabi sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ka aik waqea oopar guzar chuka hai jis mein aap ne karzzzz dainay walay ka yeh haq tasleem kya ke jis ka kuch lena bantaa hai usay kuch kehnay ka haq hai. zahir hai ke yeh haq bhi haq ke dairay hi mein ho ناچاہیے. is aadmi ne hudood se tajawaz kya magar aap ne is ke bawajood yeh kaha ke aisa karne o kehnay ka usay haq tha. agar nabi sale Allah  alaihi wasallam is ki jagah par hotay to یقینامانگنے hi nah jatay lekin jo mangnay agaya hai usay mangnay ka to haq zaroor hai magar aziat dainay aur tang karne ka nahi hai. aap ne chunkay is ke paisay dainay thay is liye aap ne is ki is aziat ko bhi maaf kar diya .
tajurbah is baat par gawah hai ke jo log nakiyon ko be parwai se le letay hain woh shuru mein to choti choti nakiyon se be parwai karte hain magar aahista aahista woh barr y nakiyon se bhi be parwa ho jatay hain. chunancha un mein neki ka rujhan aur is ki taraf melaan ka khtama ghalib aata chala jata hai. phir aadmi ka zehen kuch aur terhan se sochnay lag jata hai. phir aik waqt woh bhi aa jata hai ke har neki usay is ke rastay ki rukawat dikhayi deti hai. aur har cheez ko woh haasil karne ke liye har terhan ke hthknde istemaal karne ki koshish karta hai. phir neki ki jagah badi aati chali jati hai aur har cheez ko woh ulat nigah se dekhnay lag jata hai kisi mansab par ho to firaon ban jata hai aur awam mein se ho to ghunda o badmaash ban jata hai. is sab kuch ki ibtida is waqt hui thi jab is ne pehlay pehal kisi neki ko haqeer khayaal kya tha .
darasal jab aadmi aik neki chhorta hai to khanah khaali ra dio ?me گیرد ke usool par buraiee is ki jagah layte chali jati hai. aadmi ke seenay mein Allah  ne har neki ke liye aik ghairat rakhi hai. yeh ghairat pehlay pehal bohat ziyada hoti hai. magar baar baar buraiee karne se yeh ghairat aahista aahista kam mosrhoti chali jati hai. yahan tak ke hum zameer ki sarznish ka bilkul assar qubool nahi karte. is ghairat ki be تاثیری darasal saari buraiyon ki jarr hai. isi se baad azan sabr mein kami aati hai aur aadmi ویسابن jata hai jaisa hum ne likha hai .
agar aadmi kuch nakiyon ke baray mein Ghayoor  rahay aur kuch ke baray mein ghairat mein kami aajay to is soorat mein woh aik ghair mutawazan aadmi ban kar reh jata hai. جوبعض mamlaat mein sabir nazar aaye ga aur baaz mein ghair sabir .
jab aadmi par mushkilaat ajayeen aur woh gardishon mein گھرجائے to usay sab se ziyada jis baat ka dheyaan rakhna hai woh yeh hai ke Allah  taala is museebat se یقینامیرا bhala chahtay hain. yeh baat hum oopar ki behas mein achi terhan samajh aaye hain ke mushkilaat se Allah  hamara bhala kis terhan chahtay hain. mushkilaat ayen to hamein Allah  ke aur qareeb le jayen. isi baat ko ahadees mubarikah mein رضیت billah rubaa ke alfaaz se bayan kya gaya hai .
mushkilaat se baarha yeh baat samnay ajati hai ke hamara muaqqaf kisi baat ke baray mein ghalat tha. is ki ghalti wazeh honay ke baad aadmi ka sabr yeh hai ke haq par qaim rehne ke liye ghalat raye ko tark kar day. aur yeh khayaal har gaz nah kere ke mein ne itnay logon ke samnay yeh baat kayi martaba duhrai hai to aaya ab mein is se rujoo kar lon. nah yeh kahe ke mein ne itni mehnat se yeh silsila chalaya tha kya ab usay khatam kardoon ya yeh soochey ke mein ne pichlle saloon se isi nahaj par itna bara idaara qaim kar rakha hai ya itnay logon ko is baat par jama kar liya hai to haq ka aitraaf to kar lon lekin yeh sab kuch kahin bikhar nah jaye .
yahood ka qazia quran mein barri tafseel se aaya hai. un ki mazhabi peshwai arbo mein muslim thi. unhon ne Quresh  ko ammi keh ke unhein –apne tabay bana rakha tha. taakay woh un ke zair assar rahen. nabi akram sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ki aamad ke baad yahood ke liye yahi sawal ubhar kar samnay aaya ke agar unhon ne is nabi ammi ko maan liya to un ki مشیخت o peshwai jati rahay gi. chunancha quran ne un se kaha ke haq par qaim rehna chahtay ho to sabr aur namaz se madad lo. yani مشیخت o peshwai jati hai to is par sabr karo is liye ke is ke baad tumhen haq par qiyam ki Nemat  haasil hogi .
haq par qaim rehne mein sabr ka taqaza yeh bhi hai ke hum –apne muharikaat amal ko durust rakhen. jo kaam duniya ke liye karna hai usay duniya ke liye karen aur jo kaam akhirat ya رضاے Ellahi ke liye karna hai usay isi niyat se karen. agar aap ki niyat durust nahi hai to goya aap ne sabr ka aik bara hissa haath se jane diya. aap ne mushkilaat mein صبرکیا magar mehez is liye ke aap ko duniya صابرکہے to aap darasal haq prqaym nahi rahay .
mushkilaat mein baaz auqaat aisi mushkil bhi sir par آپڑتی hai jaisi mushkil syedna Yousuf  alaihi salam ke bhaiyon par aayi jab unhein syedna Yousuf  ka saamna karna para ke woh un ke wohi bhai hain jinhon ne unhein kunvey mein phenka tha. aur khud un ke samnay un par ilzamaat lagaye thay. aisay mauqa par sabr ka taqaza yeh hai ke apni ghalti ka aitraaf mutaliqa logon ke samnay kar liya jaye .
quran Majeed  mein mayoos honay ko kufar karne walon ka amal bataya gaya hai. aur masaaib o mushkilaat mein kufar wohi shakhs karta hai jisay kkhuda ke baray mein sahih ilm nah ho. woh jazbaat mein aakar bhool jaye ke Allah  is se kya chahta hai. sabr ka taqaza yeh hai ke aadmi masaaib mein Allah  ke aglay faislay ka mayoos hue baghair intzaar kere. aaj woh jis museebat mein mubtala kya gaya hai woh kal ho sakta hai ke is ke liye aik roshan mustaqbil le kar aa rahi ho. aur agar kal roshan mustaqbil nah bhi aaye to is ka matlab yeh hai agar woh kkhuda ke imaan se mahroom nah sun-hwa aur aisi mushkil mein bhi haq par qaim raha ikhlaq aur neki ko zaya nah kya to usay phir jannat mein aisa ajar milnay wala hai ke duniya ke kayi khush haal is par rashk karen ge .
jab hamein koi takleef –apne qareeb rehne walay logon se millti hai tohm un ke baray mein terhan terhan ki baatein sochnay lagtay hain. halaank baaz auqaat dosray log hamari bhalai mein kuch karna chahtay hain magar un ki bhalai hamaray liye nuqsaan da ho jati hai. to aisay mauqa par hamein un ke baray mein buray gumaan nahi karne chahiye. sirf isi had tak hamein un ke baray mein raye banani chahiye jitni maloomat hamaray paas hon. quran Majeed  ne is baray mein hamein yeh farmaya hai
woh muaqqaf mat ikhtiyar karo jis ka tumhare paas nah ilm ho. is liye ke kaan aankh aur dil sab se bazprs ho ni hai .
dosray mauqa prqraan Majeed  ne yeh bhi farmaya hai ke raye un maloomat par mabni honi chahiye jo tehqeeq shuda hon. suni sunai baton par amal nahi hona chahiye. nah kisi par tehqeeq kiye بغیرالزام dharna chahiye aur nah is ke khilaaf koi iqdaam is amal ke baghair hona chahiye .
agar aadmi yeh yaqeen rakhta ho ke Allah  ki marzi ke baghair koi is ko zarrar nahi pouncha sakta to is aqeedah ka laazmi nateeja yeh niklana chahiye ke doosron ke hathon zuk pounchanay par aadmi ikhlaqi rawaiyon mein kamzor nah ho .
woh doosron ki Sarih  ghalti ke bawajood gham o gussa ka izhaar bhi kere to ikhlaq ke dairay mein rehtay hue kere aur woh aadaab ko malhooz rakhay deen o Shariat  ka paband rahay Adal  o insaaf ko haath se nah jane day .
ikhlaq ke taqazoon mein se aik taqaza yeh bhi hai ke aadmi doosron ko gaali nah day. surah حجرات mein hamein doosron ke buray naam rakhnay aur un par ithaam laganay se bachney ka hukum diya gaya hai. gaali unheen dono ke beech mein aati hai. kabhi gaali ki noiyat buray naam ki si hoti hai aur kabhi ilzaam o ithaam ki si. yeh wazeh rehna chahiye ke quran ke nazdeek buray naam rakhna fisq o Fajoor  ke darjay ki cheez hai. gaali bhi isi dairay mein aaye gi .
gheebat o chughli bhi aadmi ke bughz o keena aur buri raye kaahi izhaar hai. agar aadmi sabir hai to usay chahiye ke woh un se bhi guraiz kere. woh hama waqt is se bacha rahay. agar kabhi shiddat jazbaat se aisa ho jaye to talaafi ki koshish kere .
aadmi ko Allah  taala agar naematain ataa karen achi shakal o soorat usay den aala salahiyaton se usay nawaazain to woh maghrour ho jata hai. isi terhan agar woh kisi mushkil mein sahih rawayya ikhtiyar kar le aur usay mehsoos ho ke woh aazmaysh mein kamyaab sun-hwa hai. to yeh cheez bhi baais taqqabur وغرور ho sakti hai. aadmi ko chahiye ke woh aisay moqaon par hoshyari se apni hifazat kere .
ghuroor o taqqabur ka matlab sirf akarr kar chalna hi nahi hai balkay is se morad doosron ko haqeer samjhna bhi hai. maslan Allah  ki di hui nematon par aadmi is shakhs ko haqeer samjhay jis ko Allah  hi ne un nematon se mahroom rakha hai to yeh baat aisi sangeen hai ke aadmi ko dozakhi bhi bana deti hai .
sabr ka aik laazmi taqaza yeh bhi hai ke aadmi doosron ko un ki khataon par maaf kar diya kere. un se badla nah le. doosron se badla lena aik dunewi amal hai. jis ne poora poora badla liya woh aisa hi hai jaisa is ne aik soda day kar is ki qeemat wusool karli. is par woh kisi ajar ka mustahiq nahi hai .
lekin jo shakhs dosray ko maaf kar day woh aik deeni amal sar-anjaam deta hai. usay ajar azeem ataa ho ga. jitni barri khata ko is ne maaf kya hoga itna bara ajar usay haasil hoga. quran Majeed  ka mutalba yeh hai ke hum nah sirf maaf kar den balkay is ki buraiee ka badla bhalai se den. nabi akram sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ke baray mein aata hai ke aap ki aadat husna thi ke aap gaaliyan dainay walon ko duayen dete un ki Timar  daari ko jatay un ki kher khawahi karte un ke kaam atay chunancha woh log aap ke ikhlaq hi ki wajah se musalman ho jatay thay. quran Majeed  ne is baat ko yun wazeh kya hai
buraiee اوربھلائی barabar nahi ho sakteen tum buraiee ko is cheez se dafaa karo jo behtar hai to tum dekho ge ke woh jis ke aur tumhare darmiyan adawat hai goya woh aik sargaram dost ban gaya hai. aur yeh nahi millti magar unheen logon ko jo sabir hotay hain aur yeh nahi millti magar unheen ko jo barray Nasiba  war hotay hain .
un ayaat se yeh baat bilkul wazeh hai ke sabr ka taqaza yeh hai ke aadmi buraiee ka badla neki se day. baaz log is aayat se yeh samajte hain ke Nasiba  wari Allah  taala ke intikhab ka naam hai. aisa nahi hai. har woh shakhs Nasiba  war ho sakta hai ke jo akhirat ki kamyabi ke liye jeena seekh le. quran Majeed  surah asar mein yahi kehta hai ke jo imaan laya aur is ne naik aamaal kiye aur
is dar guzar aur sabr o danai ka nateeja akhirat ki Nasiba  wari hai aur duniya mein yeh ke dushman dost ban jaye ga. aur is dushman ka khauf aman mein badal jaye ga .
is dar guzar ke maienay yeh nahi hain ke hum bas maaf kar den. badla nah len magar hamesha ke liye qata talluq kar len. yeh ghalat ho ga. aap ke dil mein is ke baray mein khayalat kaisay bhi hon aap usay Khanda  peshani se paish ayen. isi ko hadees mein sadqa qarar diya gaya hai. jo aap ke sath neki karta hai aur aap is ko muskura kar mlitay hain to yeh to har koi کرلیتاہے. asal matloob yeh hai ke hum un se bhi muskura kar milein jo hamaray liye buraiee karte phirtay hain. aur doosri taraf barah e raast ya bil wasita un ki islaah ki koshish bhi jari rakhen taakay woh apni ghalti par aadi nah hon. yeh
sabr ka aik taqaza yeh bhi hai ke aadmi jab bhi kisi sadme se do chaar ho ya doston aur azeezon ki taraf se bura slow kaaf is ke sath kya jaye to usay chahiye ke woh zabt nafs se kaam letay hue apna ehatasab kere. yeh dekhe ke is prih ibtila jo aayi hai woh kyun kar aayi hai. is ki koi ghalti hai jis ki bana par kkhuda ne usay bedaar karna chaha hai. ya is se koi gunah sarzad sun-hwa hai. jis par kkhuda chahta hai ke hum tauba kar ke is ki taraf rujoo karen. ya mere doston aur azeezon ko mere kisi ravayye aur mere kisi iqdaam ya qoul se takleef pohanchi hai. agar aadmi aisa nahi kere ga to ya woh krhhne mein laga rahay gaaya doosron ke liye aisa mahol bana chhorey ga ke woh is ke hadaf naqad aur ta'an o tasnee hon ge .
woh muashray mein bhi aik takleef da shakhs ki terhan jie ga. aur akhirat mein doosron ko takleef dainay wala banay rehne ki wajah se saza ka mustahiq ho ga. doosron par zabaan kholnay se pehlay –apne daman ke daagh shumaar karne chahiye. aur doosron par naqad karne se pehlay –apne oopar tanqeed karni chahiye. is liye ke hum khud bhi khataon se pak nahi hain .
jaisay hi hamaray samnay hamari khata aaye to usay durust karen maloom ho ke hum ne gina hay kya tha to tauba karen. aur agar hamein maloom ho ke logon ne mere sath yeh bura rawayya is liye ikhtiyar kya hai ke mein ne bhi un ke sath yun aur yun kya tha to un se moazrat karen. aur agar maloom nah ho sakay ke mere bhaiyon ne mere sath jo bura sulooq kya hai woh kyun kya hai to phir un se mohabbat aur aajzi ke sath pooch len ke aap ne mere sath aisa kyun kya hai. agar un ki ghalat fehmi ho to usay daur kar den agar woh kisi ghalti ki nishaan dahi karen to usay tasleem karte hue moazrat kar len. is ravayye se aap ki zindagi mein aik sukoon aaye ga. aap logon ke liye aik Uswah  banin ge aur agar aap ki niyat durust hogi akhirat mein ajar panay ke liye yeh sab kuch karen ge to phir aap ke liye akhirat mein aik ajar azeem muntazir ho ga .
ehatasab nafs mein sabr ke taqazoon mein se yeh bhi aik taqaza hai ke agar aap ka aqeedah o amal durust hai. aur kuch log bila waja ya –apne nazriye ki bana par aap ke darpay hogaye hain to is soorat mein un ke sath ulajhney aur un ke sath lagey rehne ke bajaye lazim hai ke aap un ki sahih baat samajhney ki koshish karen un ke naqad ko achi terhan samajh len agar is mein koi jaan hai to zaroor apni islaah kar len wagerna mehez mazaaq aur tethon par nah tawajah dainay ki zaroorat hai aur nah dil jalanay ki. بہتیرے log apna waqt isi mein zaya kar dete hain ke is ne yeh kaha hai aur is ne woh. phir is ki safai dainay mein lagey rehtay hain. agar hum khud sahih chal rahay hain to is fikar mein nahi parna chahiye ke log kya kahin ge. agar kisi ko ghalat fehmi bhi ho gi to jald ya Badeer  daur ho jaye gi. agar aap ne waisa kya hai to aap ki safai aur is ke liye aap ki jaddo jehed raaygan jaye gi. is liye ke agar aap ghalti karte hain to jald ya Badeer  samnay aajay gi .
doosron ki kher khawahi hamesha –apne paish e nazar rakhna bhi sabr ka taqaza hai. bandah momin doosron ke liye be zarrar hai. usay doosron ki buraiee ke bawajood un ke liye kher khuwa rehna hai. is ke taqazay darj zail hain
. haq aur sabr ki naseehat karna waghera
nabi akram sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ka farmaan hai
yeh duniya دارالامتحان hai. hamara asli imthehaan sabr hi ka hai. jis ke maienay yeh hain ke hum har haalat mein sahih aqeedah o amal aur sahih rawayya o sulooq par qaim rahen. sabr hi ka sila jannat hai. isi sabr ka dosra pehlu shukar hai. yeh dono mil kar deeni ravayye ki takmeel karte hain. shukar bandagi par abharta hai aur sabr be bandagi se rokta hai. shukar neki karne ka naam hai aur sabr buraiee se bachney ka. shukar neki mein agay bherne ka naam hai to sabr is par qaim rehne ka .

aik din meri maa بہلاپھسلا kar mujhe wahan le gayeen. paiir sahib ne kisi tone ki alamaat meri aankhon mein forun daryaft kar len. lakri ki aik patli aur lambi salakh par roi ka golah chrhhakr is par زیرلب kuch parhte hue phuunkaa aur aik sheeshi mein se koi itar numa cheez ke qatray is پرڈال kar meri naak mein گھسادی. چھینکوں se mera براحال ho gaya. mein ne paiir sahib ke pait par laten maarna shuru kar den. un ke msahbin ne magar mujhe poori qowat se jakar kar apna amal poora kya. is operation ke ekhtataam par meri maa ne –apne dupattay ke پلوسے rupay nikaal kar paiir sahib ko ہدیے ki soorat paish kar diye jabkay mujhe aik se ziyada rupiya bhi barri minnat samajat aur zid ke baad naseeb sun-hwa karta tha. kisi aam kalaam ki tojeeh is ki khaas jahat khitaab ke aitbaar se aik mustaqil baab hai. تعیین khitaab ka ilm isi baab ka aik shoba hai. jis shakhs par kalaam ka sahih rukh wazeh nahi ho ga woh is ki sahih taweel tak hargiz nahi pahonch sakta. pas yeh baab taweel aur nazam kalaam ke feham ki kuleed hai aur is se be khaberi bohat si ghaltion aur thokaron ka sabab ho sakti hai. aik mustaqil muqadma mein hum ilm tojeeh ke aam qawaid bayan karen ge. usool bayan karne se pehlay yeh muqadma hum ne mehez is liye likh diya hai ke fi الجملہ is masla se logon ko ans ho jaye. masla khitaab un bohat si ghaltion ki islaah karta hai jin mein hamaray mfsrin mubtala hain. pas zaroori hai ke hum is par alehda behas karen .
khitaab mein jab mukhtalif pehluo ka imkaan ho to is ko lafz mushtarik ki terhan samjhna chahiye aur is mein baaz pehluo ka ikhtiyar karna aur baaz ko chhorna na guzeer ho ga. jis terhan aik lafz mushtarik ke tamam ma-ani ko hum maloom karte hain aur phir sayaq kalaam ki roshni mein kisi maienay ko ikhtiyar karte hain aur kisi ko chortay hain wohi tarz amal hamara is waqt ho ga jab koi khitaab mukhtalif pehluo ka ihtimal rakhta ho. lehaza awleen shai is silsila mein yeh hai ke hum khitaab ke mukhtalif pehlu maloom karen .

muntahi mein التباس paighambar aur momnin ke darmiyan hota hai. baaz martaba mukhatib bzahir to paighambar hota hai lekin fi al haqeeqat ravay sukhan ummat ki taraf hota hai. paighambar ummat ke wakeel honay ki hesiyat se un ki zabaan aur un ka kaan hota hai is liye mukhatib isi ko kya jata hai. torat mein is ki misalein bohat hain ke mukhatib to hazrat moose alaihi salam ko Basighah  wahid kya gaya hai lekin is se morad un ki ummat hai. quran Majeed  mein is terhan ke mawaqay mein nazam o sayaq ki rahnumai se maloom hota hai ke mukhatib kon hai surah tauba mein aik aayat hai

satrah baras pehlay decemeber ki pandrah tareekh thi jab molana amin Ahsen  islahi duniya se rukhsat hue. sahib tadabbur quran — Allah  ki aakhri kitaab ke be misl Sarah  .
quran Majeed  zabaan o bayan ka moujza hai. arab apni fasahat o balaghat pay Nazaan  thay. saari duniya un ke liye ajmi thi. woh isi zeam mein thay ke aasman se aik kalaam ka zahuur sun-hwa. is kalaam ke shikwah ne un arbo ko ajmi bana diya. Labid  jaisa be misl shayar aisa mabhoot sun-hwa ke shairi se tauba kar li. Allah  ne imaan ki doulat se nawaza. syedna Umar  Farooq  ne shair ki فرمایش ki to kaha kya baqra aur all Imran  ke baad bhi aik moujza namodaar sun-hwa. zabaan o bayan ke asaleeb badal gaye. qadeem pemanay agar matrooq nahi hue to be assar zaroor ho gaye. insani tareekh mein pehli baar aisa sun-hwa ke aik Sahifah  adab nabuwat o risalat ki Daleel  thehra. maan liya gaya ke insaan aisay kalaam par Qadir  nahi. Laraib  yeh asmano se utrney wala kalaam hai .
saddar awwal ke baad sadiiyon tak yeh baat mehez aik aqeedah thi. quran Majeed  ke eijaaz aur Ejaaz  ko bohat se ahal ilm ne numaya kya. quran Majeed  aik herat kida hai. jo bhi is mein Itra  koi ajeeb baat daryaft kar laya. Allah  ke aakhri rasool sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ne farmaya is ke ajaaeb qayamat tak khatam nahi hon ge. hamein is ke Mazahir  tareekh ke har daur mein dikhayi dete hain. is moajezae ka aik pehlu magar aisa tha jisay abhi aqeday se aik Ilmi  daryaft mein badalna tha. qudrat ne yeh kaam imam hamid Aldeen  frahi ke muqaddar mein likh diya. hamari Ilmi  tareekh mein pehli baar unhon ne kalaam Ellahi ke is pehlu ko aik Ilmi  haqeeqat mein badal dala. moajezae ka yeh pehlu kya hai
hum jantay hain ke quran Majeed  aaj is tarteeb ke sath mojood nahi hai jis mein yeh nazil sun-hwa. is ki mojooda tarteeb bhi توقیفی yani Allah  ki taraf se hai. hum yeh bhi jantay hain ke aafaqi pegham ke sath sath is kitaab mein un waqeat par tabsarah bhi kya gaya hai jo ehad risalat maab mein paish aaye. phir is mein bhi kalaam nahi ke jab koi aayat ya ayaat nazil hoten to aap sale Allah  alaihi wasallam hadaayat farmatay ke unhein falan surah mein falan aayat se pehlay ya baad likh diya jaye. sawal yeh hai ke is nai tarteeb mein hikmat kya thi mukhtalif mawaqay par nazil honay wali ayaat jab Allah  hi ke hukum se aik marboot kitaab mein dhalen to is se wajoh mein anay wala nazam kalaam kya tha baqra all Imran  se pehlay kyun baad kyun nahi inaam Maida  ke baad hi kyun bilashuba yeh zabaan o bayan ka moujza tha jisay imam frahi ne aik zindah Ilmi  haqeeqat mein badal dala is ummat ki tareekh mein pehli baar. mera taalib almanh ehsas hai ke Tafseer  quran ki riwayat mein is se barri Ilmi  daryaft koi doosri nahi .
feham kalaam ke baab mein imam frahi ne jin umoor ko –apne ghhor o fikar ka mehwar banaya un mein do baatein bunyadi hain
aik yeh ke quran Majeed  ki ayaat aur سورتوں mein rabt hai. yeh rabt usay aik aisi deedaa Zaib  imarat bana deta hai jis mein koi aik eent bhi kisi dosray jagah lagai jati to imarat ka husn majrooh hota .
dosra yeh ke quran Majeed  zabaan o bayan mein muqallad nahi Mujtahid  hai. yeh agarchay mojood asaleeb kalaam ko paish e nazar rakhta hai lekin is ka apna aik aahang bhi hai .
quran ki zabaan aur asaleeb mein jo Nudrat  hai is ki koi misaal nahi. imam ne apni un daryafton ka quran Majeed  ke feham par itlaq kya aur aik Tafseer  likhnay ka iradah kya. woh chand aakhri سورتوں ki Tafseer  hi likh paye ke Allah  ne unhein –apne paas bulaa liya. yahan se yeh silsila الذہب dosray daur mein daakhil hota hai. yeh imam islahi ka daur hai — imam frahi ke shagird rasheed .
molana amin Ahsen  islahi ne –apne ustaad se jo kuch seekha is mein nisf sadi ki riyazat aur ghhor o fikar ko shaamil kya to is ka haasil تدبرقرآن ki soorat mein samnay aaya. unhon ne –apne ustaad aur imam ki sirf taqleed nahi ki balkay usay apni daryaft bana diya. woh kayi maqamat par –apne ustaad se ikhtilaaf bhi karte hain. yun unhon ne zabaan haal se yeh pegham bhi diya ke ghair nabi ke sath aqeedat o mohabbat ko aqal aur zameer ke tabay hona chahiye. tadabbur quran mein pehli baar yeh haqeeqat aik Ilmi  daryaft ke tor par samnay aayi ke quran Majeed  ka nazam kya hai is ki سورتوں aur ayaat mein kya rabt hai asaleeb kalaam kis terhan johar kalaam tak rahnumai karte hain quran Majeed  ko samajhney ke dakhli wasail kya hain aur kyun woh –apne feham mein johri tor par kisi kharji waselay ka mohtaaj nahi hai
molana ne taham is nazam aur asaleeb kalaam ko ziyada tar apni Tafseer  tak mehdood rakha. agar hum sirf un ka tarjuma quran parheen to ayaat mein rabt ki talaash mein diqat paish aati hai. ab aik aam qaari ke liye yeh aasaan nahi hota ke woh tadabbur quran ki no jldon ki waraq gardani karta rahay. quran Majeed  ke aik sanjeeda qaari ke liye to na guzeer hai ke woh is behar mein utre aur moti talaash kere lekin aam parha likha aadmi is mushaqqat ka kam hi muthammil hota hai is liye yeh zaroorat baqi thi ke quran ka yeh nazam aur asaleeb kalaam ki qurani Nudrat  tarjumay mein samnay aaye. yeh woh marhala hai jahan al bayan ka zahuur hota hai — is silsila الذہب ki teesri kari .
yeh Javed  Ahmed  ghamdi sahib ka tarjuma quran hai. pehla tarjuma quran jo nazam kalaam ki riayat se kya gaya. aap usay parhte hain to kahin yeh gumaan nahi hota ke quran Majeed  mutafarraq ayaat ka majmoa hai. kalaam khud batata hai ke yeh aik marboot kalaam hai. yeh aik rasool ki srgzsht انذار hai jo is zameen par Allah  taala ki aakhri adalat thay. jin ki hayaat mubarikah mein logon ne apni aankhon se dekha ke kaisay arab ki sarzamen par woh qayamat barpaa hui jis ne kharay aur khote ko allag allag kar diya. jis ne Allah  taala ki ayaat ka inkaar karne walon ko azaab se dochar kya aur Allah  par imaan laane walon aur aamaal Saleh  karne walon ko ajar azeem se nawaza. aisay hi is aalam ka parvar-digaar aik din saari duniya ke logon ko jama kere ga aur isi terhan kharay aur khote ko allag allag kar day ga. yun quran Majeed  is qayamat sughra ki rudaad bayan karta aur qayamat par usay aik na qabil tardeed Daleel  bana deta hai. al bayan ko padhiye to Allah  ke aakhri rasool sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ki srgzsht انذار mashhoor ho jati hai. yeh bhi andaza hota hai ke quran Majeed  ko mutafarraq aqval ka majmoa samajhney aur aik marboot kalaam maan-ne mein kya farq hai aur kaisay yeh farq khud ayaat ki feham mein zameen aasman ka farq daal deta hai. Javed  Ahmed  ghamdi sahib ka molana islahi se wohi rishta hai jo khud molana ka –apne ustaad imam frahi se tha. mohabbat o aqeedat mein dooba sun-hwa lekin khuli aankhon ke sath. yun Javed  sahib –apne ustaad se kayi maqamat ki sharah mein ikhtilaaf bhi karte hain .
aik daidh mah pehlay al bayan ki takmeel ho gayi. is ki teen jldin shaya ho chuki hain. do jldon ki ashaat baqi hai. mein ne is Saadat  par Javed  sahib ko saraapaa shukar o jazbaat dekha. bilashuba sab kaam Allah  ki tofeq hi se hotay hain. har insani kawish ghalti ka ihtimal liye hoti hai. Allah  ko to matloob yahi hai ke koi bandah is ki raah mein Sadaq  dil se koi qadam uthaye. asal qeemat isi Sadaq  ki hai. molana islahi aaj zindah hotay to kitney khush hotay. un ke ustaad ne jo chairag jalaya jisay unhon ne nisf sadi ki riyazat ka roghan diya aaj jala watni ki aandhiyon mein bhi poori aabb o taab ke sath roshan hai. yeh kitaab Allah  ka chairag hai aur yeh phoonko se bujh nahi sakta .

afsos hai ke hamaray muashray mein depration ka marz bohat aam hota ja raha hai. tang dast khush haal un parh taleem Yafta  hatta ke deeni feham aur mizaaj rakhnay walay bhi is ka shikaar ho rahay hain. depration hi ki wajah se duniya mein rozana kayi afraad khudkushi aur khud Suzi  jaisi harkat ka irtikaab kar rahay hain. aik mutalay ke mutabiq tak depration duniya ka sab se bara masla ban jaye ga .
zindagi se be zaar rehna alehadgi pasand ho jana dekhnay mein bemaar lagna mustaqil be chain aur afsurdah rehna depration ke mareez ki alamaat hain. aisa mareez hasad khauf buzdali qanotiat sahal angraai aur be itmadi ka shikaar ho jata hai .
aam istilaah mein depration ki do kasmain hain. aik qisam keemiyai hai aur doosri samaji. keemiyai qisam mein insaan ke andar keemiyai anasir ka tawazun baggar jata hai. aisay logon ko sayikatrst ke paas le jana parta hai jo is ka ilaaj dawa se karta hai. aur samaji qisam mein insaan ke gharelo karobari aur masharti halaat mein koi kharabi waqay ho jati hai yani yeh depration kisi pareshani gham ya nakami ki wajah se la-haq hota hai. aisay logon ko sayikalojst ke paas le jaya jata hai jo is ka ilaaj guftagu se karta hai .
samaji qisam ke pehlu se yeh baat blakhof tardeed kahi ja sakti hai ke haqeeqi musalman kabhi depration ka shikaar nahi ho sakta. is liye ke musalman ka imaan hai ke is ki zindagi Allah  ki taraf se aik aazmaysh hai a seen ka maqsad hayaat Allah  ki parastish aur itaat hai aur is ki zindagi mein pareshaaniya is ki aazmaysh ke liye aati hain .
aur hum tumhen dukh aur sukh se aazma rahay hain parkhnay ke liye aur tum hamari hi taraf lout’tay jao ge .
aur yeh bhi haqeeqat hai ke Allah  taala ki taraf se anay walay masaaib ki shiddat kabhi insaan ke tahammul ki had se bahar nahi hoti. qanonِ Ellahi hai
hum kisi jaan par is ki istetat se ziyada boojh nahi daaltay .
chunancha musalman masaaib ko zindagi ka laazmi hissa samjhta hai aur masaaib se ghabra kar zindagi se bezaar honay ke bajaye un se nijaat panay ke liye poori aur musalsal koshish karta hai. musalman jaanta hai ke is ki dunewi zindagi ki pareshaaniya earzi hain agar woh nasaaz gaar halaat mein bhi –apne imaan aur Aamaal Saleha  par qaim rahay ga to marnay ke baad har gham se pak intehai pur musarrat uss abdi zindagi ka haq daar ho ga jis ki basharat aalam ke parvar-digaar ne di hai
be shak hum tumahra imthehaan karen ge kisi qader khauf bhook aur malon aur jaanun aur phalon ki kami se aur un saabit qadmon ko khush khaberi suna do jin ka haal yeh hai ke jab un ko koi museebat pahunchti hai to woh kehte hain ke be shak hum Allah  hi ke liye hain aur hum isi ki taraf lotney walay hain. yahi log hain jin par un ke rab ki inayateen hain aur Hamat  aur yahi log raah yab honay walay hain .
woh log jo imaan laaye aur unhon ne naik amal kiye is mein shuba nahi ke woh behtareen Khalaique  hain. un ka sila un ke parvar-digaar ke paas abadd ke baagh hain jin ke neechay nehrein bah rahi hon gi. woh un mein hamesha rahen ge. Allah  un se raazi sun-hwa aur woh is se raazi hue. yeh sila hai un ke liye jo –apne parvar-digaar se daray .
hazrat ayub alaihi salam maal aulaad aur Khudam  se mahroom honay ke ilawa aik bohat takleef da jismani azaar mein bhi mubtala hogaye. bible mein hai ke ayub alaihi salam ke talway se sir tak saaray jism mein jaltay hue phoray nikal aaye. woh aik ٹھیکرا le kar apna jism khujate aur raakh par baithy rehtay thay. lekin is ke bawajood aap imaan ki chattaan saabit hue. خباب ban arat razi Allah  anho ko mushriqeen mecca ne aag ke angaron par litaya yahan tak un ki charbi pighalnay se aag bujh gayi lekin woh imaan par jamay rahay. bilal razi Allah  anho ko lohay ki zarah pehna kar chilchelati dhoop mein khara kar diya gaya phir tapti rait par luta kar ghsita gaya magar woh ahad ahad hi karte rahay. nabi sale Allah  alaihi wasallam to sakhti ayyaam ko ibadat Ellahi ka zareya bana letay thay .
Sayeda  aisha razi Allah  anha farmaati hain ke rasool Allah  sale Allah  alaihi wasallam mere paas tashreef laaye aur farmaya tumhare paas khanay ki koi cheez hai mein ne kaha nahi to aap ne farmaya phir mein rozay se hon .

musalman is ramz se aashna hota hai ke is duniya mein sab kuch Allah  hi ke azan aur iraday se hota hai aur Allah  ka koi iradah kher aur hikmat se khaali nahi hota. is liye musalman har zahmat mein rehmat daikhta hai aur har zakham mein marham palita hai. agras ki kashti ka takhta toot jata hai aur woh aib daar ho jati hai to woh yeh soch kar pareshan nahi hota ke mumkin hai yeh waqea is ki poori kashti ko bachanay ke liye runuma sun-hwa ho. agar woh –apne jawan betay ki mout ke sadme se dochar hota hai to yeh soch kar aasabi tanao ka shikaar nahi hota ke mumkin hai agar yeh larka zindah rehta to is ke liye mout se shadeed tar sadmaat ka baais bantaa. agar is ke samnay ehley baatil ko koi faida pohanchana hai to woh yeh soch kar shakista dil nahi hota ke mumkin hai kal is mein ehley haq hi ka koi faida nikal aaye .

chunkay haqeeqi musalman zindagi ke falsafay se poori terhan aagah hota hai. woh aazmaysh ki khudai scheme se poori terhan waaqif hota hai. usay yeh maloom hota hai ke dukh is zindagi ka laazmi hissa hain. woh is se achi terhan bakhabar hota hai ke un earzi dukhoon par sabr o istiqamat ke nateejay mein is ke liye abdi raahat ka ihtimaam kya gaya hai. lehaza woh mushkil tareen aur hosla shikan halaat mein bhi kkhuda ki rehmat se mayoos nahi hota. is liye yeh baat poooray yaqeen ke sath kahi ja sakti hai ke agar koi musalman samaji halaat ki kharabi ke baais depration mein mubtala hai zindagi se bezaar hai mustaqil afsurdah rehta hai dekhnay mein har waqt bemaar lagta hai hasad khauf aur buzdali ka shikaar hai qanotiat sahal angraai aur be itmadi mein mubtala hai to یقینااس ki مسلمانیت mein koi khout hai warna yeh nahi ho sakta ke koi shakhs musalman ho aur depration ka shikaar ho jaye. musalman ka maamla to yeh hai ke
zaraat malik mein reerh ki si hesiyat rakhti hai. taraqqi Yafta  mumalik mein zaraat par khusoosi tawajah di jati hai lekin pakstan mein ahwaal is ke bar aks hain .
Pakistan  mein kashtkaron ko zaraat ke hawala se bohat si mushkilaat ka saamna karna parta hai. jin mein mayaari beej zarayi adwiyaat pani aur باردانہ ki Adam  dasteyabi aur faslun kaaalmi aur muqami mandiyon tak ba aasani rasai ka nah hona aur faslun ka mayaari qeemat par farokht nah hona shaamil hain. unhi masail par baat karne ke liye mukhtalif zamindaron se baat hui .
Mohammad  Shabir  ka talluq se hai aur yeh aekar zarayi zameen ke maalik hain ne bataya ke hamaray malik mein nhron ka jaal bichaa sun-hwa hai mujhe pani ke masail ka saamna nahi karna parta. salana neher ki bandish decemeber mein hoti hai lekin is waqt faslun ko pani ki itni zaroorat nahi rehti .
is waqt hamara ahem masla hai hamein hamari ijnaas ke khredar nahi mil rahay. aalo kapaas chawal aur makayi ke khredar nahi hain agar khredar mlitay hain to faslun ki qeemat bohat kam lagatay hain .
is dafaa aalo ki fasal ne zamindaron ki kamar toar di hai. is dafaa aalo ki fasal par pedawar laagat isi hazaar rupay fi aekar hai. jabkay fi aalo ki bori ki teen sad se saarhay tain sad rupay mein farokht hui. fi aekar mein so bori aalo nikaltay hain jis ki qeemat tees se pints hazaar rupay hai jabkay is par laagat isi hazaar rupay aayi hai .
gandum ki fasal bhi aa gayi hai. باردانہ ke husool ke liye zamindar dhakkay khaye ga ya mehanga khareeday ga. is par bhi zamindar ko izafi akhrajaat bardasht karna parte hain .
Pakistan  zarayi malik hai hukoomat ko is shoba par khusoosi tawajah ki zaroorat hai. hukoomat zamindaron ko behtar sahuliyaat day to malik ke sath sath kashtkaar bhi khushaal hoga is ke sath sath deegar shoba jaat bhi khushaal nazar ayen ge .

nhri pani faslun ke liye bohat mufeed hai Manzoor  shuda zameen par hafta baad nhri pani milta hai. nhri pani ki qeemat fi aekar rupay hai jis ki har chay mah baad adaigi hoti hai .
fi aekar ke liye meet diye jatay hain baaz موہگے chhootey hotay hain jin se pani ka ikhraj mushkil se hota hai. موہگہ se ziyada faasla par faslun par muqarara waqt mein pani mukammal sairaab nahi kar paata jis wajah se zamindar ko tube veil ka pani istemaal karna parta hai .
zamindar ko zaati bijli ke tube veil par fi unit gayarah rupay mein parta hai. hars power ki motor lagi ho twayk ghantay mein kunaal araazi sairaab hoti hai. tube veil ka pani is qeemat par parta hai .
apna zaati ho to rupay fi ghanta
kharidne par rupay fi ghanta
pitra نجن ka rupay fi ghanta
tracktor par chalaya gaya engine rupay se rupay tak
fasal ko poora pani nah miley to fasal ki behtar pedawar nahi hoti is liye zamindar ko tube veil ka pani bhi lagana parta hai. tube veil ka pani mehanga parta hai lekin zamindar majboor hota hai. phir jab fasal tayyar ho kar ghar ajati hai to achi qeemat par farokht nahi hoti .
gandum ka sarkari narkh rupay pay. agar hum yeh hi gandum kisi آڑھتی ke paas le kar jayen taa woh aik hazaar se gayarah so rupay qeemat lagaye ga aur phir apni آڑھت commission alehda se le ga .
makayi tamam halaat mein rupay fi mann farokht hoti hai lekin jab fasal ke baad farokht karne jayen to rupay fi mann se zayed آڑھتی nahi kharidata jabkay is se zayed zamindar kharcha kar chuka hota hai .
chand barson se zamindar musalsal khasaray mein ja raha hai. sarkari pani باردانہ ya tube veil ke pani par utney walay zayed akhrajaat hi hamaray masail nahi hain. is ke ilawa bhi hamaray beshumar masail hain jin mein srِfhrst ijnaas ke khredar nahi hain .
hakoomati naaqis policion ke tehat aalmi mandiyon tak hamari rasai na Guzir  hai. jab tak hukoomat hamaray masail par tawajah nahi day gi zamindar khushaal nahi ho ga .
chohadry Rafeeq  ki saarhay pandrah aekar zarayi zameen mein hai unhon ne zamindaron ke masail par roshni daaltay hue bataya ke jis neher se hamari zamiinon ko pani milta hai is ki tell par hamari zameen honay ki wajah se pani bohat hi kam pohanchana hai. jis neher par مؕوگہ ka size inch hai nhri pani ka waqt minute fi aekar hai jabkay inch مؕوگہ par minute fi aekar pani diya jata hai. jis ki maliyat mah baad rupay fi aekar gaon ke nambardar ko jama karwa di jati hai. har saal pani lainay ke auqaat tabdeel kar diye jatay hain. subah bujey ki baari walay ko saal baad shaam chay bujey pani lainay ki baari miley gi .
nhri pani nah milnay ki soorat mein tube veil ka pani istemaal karna parta hai jo khasa mehanga hai. bijli par chalne walay tube veil ka kharcha rupay fi unit hai. bijli par chalne wali hars power ki موٹرسے aik ghanta mein kunaal zameen sairaab hoti hai .
pehli baar makayi ki fasal ko daidh ghanta fi aekar pani lagta hai. pehli dafaa gandum ki fasal ko fi aekar ghanta mein pani lagta hai. tracktor ke zariye engine chalanay پرفی ghanta mein letter diesel kharch hota hai fi letter diesel ki qeemat rupay hai .
pehlay bijli par chalne walay hars power ki motor walay tube veil par bil hazaar rupay fix tha. jo hukoomat ne fix rupay hata kar rupay fi unit kar diya jis se zamindar mazeed izafi akhrajaat ke boojh taley dab gaya. faslun par utney walay akhrajaat ziyada hain jabkay farokht karne par asal akhrajaat ki raqam bhi nahi millti .
gandum ke liye klov gram plastic ka thela rupay mein mil raha hai. aik aekar ke liye thelay diye jatay hain. klov gram aalo ki khaali bori ki qeemat rupay rupay ka taat aur rupay mazdoori aalo بھروائی. un boryon ko khait se manndi tak pahunchana is par akhrajaat uthte hain. is baar zamindar ko aalo manndi mein teen se chaar rupay fi klov آڑھتی ko farokht karne parre. makayi se rupay fi mann farokht hui. jabkay is fasal par uthnay walay akhrajaat hazaar rupay fi aekar hain. fi aekar mein se mann makayi nikalti hai. gandum ki pedawar bhi mann fi aekar hai. is ka sarkari narkh rupay fi mann hai. fasal kal fi aekar pedawar kam ya ziyada mousmi halaat par munhasir hai .
hukoomat se guzarish karen ge ke woh dosray malik ki sabzian ya phal waghera is malik mein nah mngwayin hamaray malik ki yeh sab ashya dosray mumalik mein bhejen taa ke zamindar ko bhi achi qeemat mil sakay. mulki kisaan ki khushhali malik ki khushhali ki zamanat hai .
ikhtilaaf agar misbet ho to taraqqi ki nai rahein کھولتاہے aur agar ikhtilaaf baraye ikhtilaaf ho to muashray mein inteshaar phelanay ka baais bantaa hai. ikhtilaaf mein dono fareeqon ki nazar Daleel  par hoti hai aur mukhalfat mein dono fareeqon ki nazar dosray ko badnaam karne par hoti hai. insani fitrat hai jab hamein koi insaan bُra lagta hai to iss ki har baat burii lagti hai. hamaray haan behas baraye behas aur zaati mafadaat ke حسصول ke liye hoti hai kyunkay ikhtilaaf hi hamara bunyadi hadaf hota hai .
Pakistan  mein hakoomaten apni na ahli aur na qabliyat ki wajah se gardaab mein phansi rehti hai. corruption scandal. rimnd dews case. WikiLeaks. mimo gate. Karachi  target killing. an are o. to heen adalat. soys. rental power. ایفیڈرن scandal. nndi power project. میٹروبس. model ٹاؤن. panamh leaks. mukhtalif mamlaat ki wajah se masail aur uthte tufaan ki wajah se حکومتوںکی tawajah aur tawa naiya mulk ki taamer o taraqqi mein kam avrkhod ko sacha saabit karne sirf hoti hain aur mukhalfin bharpoor siyasi faida uthanay ki koshish karte hain. hazbay Iqtidaar  aur hazbay ikhtilaaf ki awleen tarjeeh hoti hai kisi nah kisi terhan haqayiq maskh kya jaye. arsa daraaz se Pakistan  mein ilzaam dar ilzaam ki siyasat urooj par hai. سیاستکاری ke maahir piyali mein tufaan khara karte hain lekin guzarte dِn ke sath yeh tufaan tham jata hai aur jab tak دوسراطوفان khara nahi hota media par behas o مباحشہ jari rehta hai. hukoomat ki aara se nah mukhalfin mutmaen hotay hain aur nah hi mukhalfin haar مارننے ko tayyar. terhan terhan ki صفائیاں aur تشریحاں sُnne ko millti hain. roz aik nai behas janam layte hai avrbe nateeja khatam ho jati hai aur mukhalfin ke buland o bangh daaway waday sab dharay ke dharay rahay jatay hain. baghair kisi nateejay par puhanche baghair khatam shuda .
iss baar bhi sorat e haal maazi se mukhtalif nahi. panamh leaks ke muamlay par mulk mein siyasi tamasha apni poori aabb o taab se jari hai. aik na khatam honay wali jung chhar y hui hai. electronic aur print media mein aik dosray ke khilaaf tndotiz bayanaat shaya ho rahay hain. lahasil guftagu tabsaray tajzia aur تشر یحا t- ka silsila jari hai. panamh leaks pravr ghair zama darana trzِ siyasat ne iss maslay ¾ ko mukammal tor par siyasi bana dala. aisa lagta hai ke bohraan musalsal ke bunyadi muharrak aur fitnah o fasaad ka asal maqsad corruption se نہیںبلکہ muntakhib jamhoori hukoomat se chhutkara paana hai. parlimani baladasti ke geet ganay walon ki shadeed خوائش hai ke jamhoori system jald az jald zamee bose ho jaye. waqt bara be reham hai. teen saal se muntashir hazbay ikhtilaaf yakja to ho gayi hai jamhoori hukoomat ke khilaaf jamhoori ittehaad marzِ wujood mein aachuka. ittafaq ho na sawalia nishaan hai .
karva sach hai ke chand dِn pehlay tak hazbay ikhtilaaf mein shaamil mukhtalif jamaaton ke arakeen aik dosray par tanqeed ke nishtar barastee nahi thaktay thay. aik dosray ko mukhtalif alqabaat se nawaza jata tha. aik dosray ki corruption daastaa’n cheekh cheekh kar bayan kya jata tha. jalson mein llkarh jata tha. awaami numainday TV talk shows mein ikhlaqi eqdaar ki had paar kar ke aik dosray se dast o gireybn thay. magar aaj aisa kya ho gaya ke maazi ke hareef garamjoshi ke sath bghlgir hain. ajab tamasha hai shore woh log macha rahay hain jin par sab se ziyada maali bud unwani aur اقرباپروری ke ilzamaat aur cases hain. aaj ke ittihadi –apne maazi mein jhanknay ki zahmat نہیںکرر hai. ikhlaqi juwaz ki baat par ہرزباں par hai. kash log apni naaqis yadasht ko ko phir se tawana kar len to yeh siyasi tamasha ekhtataam pazeer ho jaye. maamla itna pichid hay nahi hai magar iss khail ke –apne taqazay bhi hain. hazbay ikhtilaaf bakhobi waaqif hai ke iss mein se kuch nahi niklana .
iss baat se inkaar nahi kiya ja sakta ke hukoomat mein so خرابیا n hain. hakoomati arakeen bhi corruption mein mulawis ho satke hain. magar hazbay ikhtilaaf pehlay apni safoon se bhi bad unwaan anasir kharij kere tab hi corruption ke khilaaf muhim kamyaab ho sakti hai. agar haqeeqatan siyasi jamaten corruption ke khatmay par سنجیدہیں to siyasat baraye siyasat se guraiz aur maazi ki talkhioun ko bُhla kar sanjeedgi se vtnِ Aziz  se corruption ke naasoor khatam karne ki qanooni aur aaeni jad-o-jehad karen. iss terhan jamaten bhi bad unwaan anasir se pak aur malik bhi. kisi bhi muashray mein iss se barh kar koi nuqsaan da cheez nahi ho sakti ke jab kisi ko kisi se zaati inaad رنجشی ya ikhtilaaf ho to woh jung mein sab kuch halal hai ka ابلیسی usool ikhtiyar kar le. aik dosray par har terhan ke jhutay ilzamaat ki yalghaar kere. jaan boojh kar ghalat baatein mansoob kere iss ke nuqta nazar ko qasdan ghalat soorat mein paish kere. siyasi ikhtilaaf ho to isay ghaddar aur dushman watan ٹہرائے ba-hasiat poori qoum ka nuqsaan hai. jis se bil akhir khud woh log bhi nahi bach satke jo ikhtilaaf ke iss behooda tareeqay ko mufeed samajh kar ikhtiyar karte hain .
kuch zikre khaas media ka karte hain. afsos se kehna parta hai Pakistan  mein media ke kuch عناصرہمہ waqt aisay mauqa ki talaash mein rehtay hain jis se jamhoori hukoomat ka khtama ho jaye ya phir kamzor prhjaye. mojooda sorat e haal mein mein media ka kirdaar bhi janabdaar hai. sahafi eqdaar ko baalaye taaq rakhtay hue media ke kuch anasir ne poori taaqat ke sath hukoomat waqt par yalghaar ki hui hai. hukoomat ke achay kamon aur misbet iqdamaat ko bhi ghalat piraye par Nashar  kar ke tanqeed ke نشتربرسا ye ja rahay hain. naam Nihaad  sahafi agenday ke mutabiq tajziye tabsaray o tshrihat bayan kar rahay hain. soul aur askari ke darmiyan mhaz aarai ki kefiyat peda karne ki nakaam koshish ki ja rahi hai. pemra kuch waqt le liye محترک ho a tha magar phir se maazi ka media sir atharha hai. خاکسا ray ne kuch dِn pehlay –apne column mein tehreer kya tha ke agar pemra ne sirf notices par iktifa kya to nah hi notice کیااہمیت rahay gi aur nah idaray ki authority ki. yaqeen janye media ka yeh kirdaar duniya ke jamhoori mumalik mein nhinhoga. hakoomati ki ghalat palisz par intahaa tak tanqeed ki jati hai lekin waqt se pehlay hukoomat ko khatam karne ki misaal nahi millti .
jis par malik ke tamam mukhtalif alkhyal garohoon mazhabi o siyasi jamaten aur ashkhaas ko ittafaq karna chahiye woh hai sadaqat aur bahami insaaf. ikhtilaaf agar imandari ke sath ho dalail ke sa th ho aur aِsi had tak rahay jis had tak fi al waqea ikhtilaaf hai to aksar halaat mein yeh mufeed saabit hota hai. kyunkay is terhan mukhtalif nuqta nazar apni sihh soorat mein logon ke samnay aajate hain aur log انہیںدیکھ kar khud raye qaim kar satke hain ke woh inn mein se kis ko qubool karen. bad qismati se نارواداری aur badgumaani aur khudpasandi ka yeh marz hamaray malik mein aik وبائے aam ki soorat ikhtiyar kar chuka hai jis se bohat hi kam log bachay hue hain. hukoomat aur iss ke arbab ikhtiyar mubtala hain siyasi partiyan iss mein mubtala hain mazhabi giroh iss mein mubtala hain akhbar nawees iss mein mubtala hain hatta ke bustiyon aur mehloon aur dehaat ki choti choti tolyon tak mein iss ke zahreeley اثررات utar gaye hain. iss ka madawa sirf iss terhan ho sakta hai ke sab se pehlay woh log jo –apne –apne halqon mein assar rakhtay hain apni zehniat tabdeel karen aur khud –apne tarz amal se logon ko tahammul bardasht aur wusat zarfi ka sabaq den .
wazeer e azam Nawaz  shareef aur irani saddar husn Rohani  ke darmiyan mulaqaat shuru ho gayi. army cheif general raheel shareef bhi mulaqaat mein shareek hain .
mulaqaat ke douran Pakistani  qayadat irani saddar se Iran  Saudi  arab kasheedgi aur khittay ki soorat e haal par baat kere gi .
is se qabal t_hran mein wazeer e azam Nawaz  shareef aur army cheif general raheel shareef ne qasr sadarat mein awwal naib saddar Ishaq  j_hangiri se mulaqaat ki .
army cheif general raheel shareef ne irani wazeer difaa se bhi mulaqaat ki jis ke douran army cheif ka kehna tha ke dehshat gardi aik aalmi khatrah hai jis ka mazboot aur marboot jawab dainay ki zaroorat hai .
aayi SP are ke mutabiq army cheif general raheel shareef ne t_hran mein irani wazeer difaa Hussain  dehqaan se mulaqaat ki jis mein ilaqai salamti ke umoor par tabadlah khayaal kiya gaya .
army cheif ne kaha ke Iran  Pakistan  ka ahem hamsaaya malik hai aur Pakistani  awam –apne irani bhaiyon se bohat لگاؤ rakhtay hain dehshat gardi aik aalmi khatrah hai jo khittay ko ghair mustahkam karne ki salahiyat rakhti hai

wazeer e azam Nawaz  shareef ki kabeena ke ahem rukan aur qareebi saathi mshahdallh Khan  ne kaha hai ke pichlle saal Islamabad mein tehreek insaaf aur awaami tehreek ke dharnon ke douran Pakistani  intelli jins agency aayi s aayi ke is waqt ke sarbarah Lieutenant General Zahir  al - islam abbasi ne aik saazish tayyar ki thi jis ke zariye woh fouji aur soul qayadat ko hata kar malik par qabza karna chahtay thay .
Mushahid  Allah  Khan  ke bakol is saazish ka inkishaaf is waqt sun-hwa jab Pakistan  ke civilian intelli jins idaray intelli jins beuro ne liftint general Zahir  al - islam abbasi ki tally phonic guftagu tape ki jis mein woh mukhtalif logon ko Hadayat  day rahay thay ke dharnay ke douran kis terhan afratafri phalane hai aur wazeer e azam house par qabza karna hai .
Mushahid  Allah  Khan  ne is dharnay ke aik saal mukammal honay par bi bi si ko diye gaye aik interview mein kaha ke augst ki shaam Wazeer e Azam  Nawaz  shareef ne buri fouj ke sarbarah general raheel shareef se mulaqaat ke douran yeh audio tape unhein sunai .
wifaqi wazeer ne kaha general raheel shareef yeh tape sun kar heran reh gaye. unhon ne isi waqt general Zahir  al - islam abbasi ko isi meeting mein Wazeer e Azam  ke samnay talabb kar ke wohi tape dobarah چلوائی aur un se poocha ke kya yeh aawaz aap hi ki hai aur general abbasi ki janib se is tasdeeq ke baad ke yeh aawaz unhi ki hai general raheel ne general abbasi ko meeting se chalay jane ko kaha .
Mushahid  Allah  Khan  ne kaha ke yeh tape aur is ke ilawa bhi is waqt hukoomat ko mukhtalif zaraye se jo it-tila-aat mil rahi theen woh bohat khofnaak theen aur is waqt tayyar honay wali saazish ke nateejay mein bohat tabahi honi thi .
is tape mein khuli saazish tayyar ki ja rahi thi ke kya karna hai kaisay karna hai wazeer e azam house par qabzay ki bhi baat ki gayi thi yani is sab ke nateejay mein bohat hi ziyada bigaar tha. is waqt kuch bhi ho sakta tha .
Mushahid  Allah  ke bakol is waqt jo saazish tayyar ki ja rahi thi is ka nishana sirf soul hukoomat ya wazeer e azam Nawaz  shareef nahi thay balkay yeh saazish buri fouj ke sarbarah ke khilaaf bhi thi .
is saazish ka aik hissa yeh bhi tha ke wazeer e azam Nawaz  shareef aur general raheel shareef ke darmiyan itni khaleej aur ikhtilafat peda kar diye jayen ke Nawaz  shareef ko majboor kar diya jaye ke woh general raheel ke khilaaf koi action len aur jab woh action len to is waqt kuch log is waqt harkat mein ayen aur Iqtidaar  par qaabiz ho jayen
is sawal par ke jab Islamabad mein itni sangeen saazish tayyar ho rahi thi aur is par amal karne ki koshish ho rahi thi ain is waqt wazeer e azam Nawaz  shareef achanak wazeer e azam house chore kar –apne ahal khanah samait Lahore  kyun chalay gaye
Mushahid  Allah  ne kaha ke wazeer e azam ko ewaan wazeer e azam se bahar nikaalte ka faisla bhi aik saazish se bachney ke liye kya gaya tha .
is ki tafseel batatay hue Mushahid  Allah  ne kaha ke augst ke roz intelli jins beuro aur baaz deegar zaraye se hukoomat ko khabar mili ke aslehay se bhari do gariyaan wazeer e azam house ki taraf aa rahi hain. is waqt tak pi TV par qabza ho chuka tha aur log secreteriat aur wazeer e azam house ki taraf barh rahay thay .
aisay mein hukoomat ke paas is ke ilawa koi rasta nahi tha ke wazeer e azam ko wahan se nikaal kar mehfooz maqam par muntaqil kar diya jaye. baad mein hamein maloom sun-hwa ke fouj hi ke aik Afsar  ne do gariyon ko pakra jo wazeer e azam house jane ki koshish kar rahi theen. un gariyon mein pachees pachees kalashnikov theen
is sawal par ke yeh bndoqin kis ne aur kahan istemaal karni theen Mushahid  Allah  Khan  ne kaha jab mein ne is baray mein daryaft kya to mujhe bataya gaya ke un ke kuch log wahan pehlay hi pahonch chuke thay jinhon ne un klashnkofon ko istemaal karna tha. bas yeh asleha andar laane ki der thi .
jab un se poocha gaya ke aik taraf aap baaz fouji jrnilon par hukoomat ke khilaaf saazish ka ilzaam laga rahay hain aur doosri taraf wazeer e azam house aur deegar ahem amarat ki hifazat ki zimma daari bhi fouj hi ko day di gayi Mushahid  Allah  ne kaha ke fouj bator idaara hukoomat ke khilaaf is saazish mein shaamil nahi thi .
baaz bohat mo-asar aur senior jarnail is saazish mein mulawis thay jin mein liftint general zhiralaslam bhi shaamil hain lekin general raheel aur Pakistani  fouj aik idaray ke tor par is saazish mein shaamil nahi thi .
Mushahid  Allah  ne kaha ke agar general raheel hukoomat khatam karne ki khwahish rakhtay to phir dharnon waghera ki zaroorat hi nahi paish aani thi .
is sawal par ke hukoomat ko is dharnay ki aarr mein honay wali is mobayyana saazish ka ilm kab sun-hwa to mshahdallh Khan  ne kaha ke hukoomat ko pehlay din se is saazish ka ilm tha .
hamein pata tha ke London  mein tahir al-qadri aur Imran  Khan  ke darmiyan honay wali mulaqaat mein aayi s aayi ke kuch log bhi mojood thay. hum yeh bhi jantay thay ke is mulaqaat mein kya kuch tay sun-hwa ke kis ne Lahore  se kab chalna hai kahan pohanchna hai kya karna hai .
unhon ne kaha ke hukoomat ne pehlay din hi se yeh tahiya kar rakha tha ke kisi bhi qeemat par un logon ke khilaaf taaqat istemaal nahi karni kyunkay baaz taqaten yahi chahti theen ke hukoomat taaqat istemaal kere aur un ki saazish par amal ka rasta hamwar ho jaye .
is mobayyana saazish mein mulawis honay par aayi s aayi ke sabiq sarbarah general retired Zahir  islam abbasi ke khilaaf karwai ke imkanaat ke baray mein aik sawal par Mushahid  Allah  ne kaha ke Pakistan  mein jamhoriat abhi itni taaqatwar nahi ke is terhan ki karwai kar sakay .
go ke hamari hukoomat ne general Musharraf  ke khilaaf muqadma to darj kya lekin hum un ke khilaaf bhi is terhan ki karwai nahi kar sakay jaisa ke ki jani chahiye thi. wazeer e azam ki saari tawajah mulki istehkaam aur usay agay le jane par markooz hai. aisay mauqa par woh is qisam ki inquiry ya karwai ka faisla nahi karna chahtay .

hamesha haq par qaim rehna sabr hai balkay hum ne yeh jana ke asal sabr hi yahi hai. isi baat ki wazahat peechay se hoti chali aa rahi hai. yahan hum apni baat ko raye ki had tak mehdood karen ge. is liye ke hum zehni آزمایشوں ke pehlu se sabr ko dekh rahay hain. zehni aitbaar se yeh sab se barri aazmaysh hai ke aadmi apni raye mein haq par qaim rehta hai ya nahi .
insaan ghalti ka shikaar ho sakta hai. agar is mein haq parasti ka Wasf  nah ho to wahein chipak kar reh jata hai. sirf haq parasti hi کاوصف aisa hai ke is ki ghaltion ko daur karta aur is ki islaah karta rehta hai. jo log yeh khayaal karte hain ke hamari raye pukhta aur durust hai woh sab se barri ghalti ka shikaar hain. yahi sab se barri na-haq parasti hai. Anabia  ke baad koi shakhs aisa nahi hai jisay haq ke baray mein ghalti nah lagi ho. koi shakhs bhi سوفی sadi durust nahi hai. is liye har shakhs ko har waqt is ke liye tayyar rehna chahiye ke is ki ghalti nikal sakti hai magar hamari qoum ki tarbiyat aisi hui hai ke woh yeh samajte hain ke bas un ke paas jo kuch hai wohi mustand aur durust hai .
is ummat mein Anabia  ke baad aymh ko aik bara maqam mlahe unhein ummat ke barray barray garohoon ki taraf se qabuliat mili hai magar un ka maamla bhi yeh hai ke charon aik baat nahi kehte. yeh to kabhi bhi nahi ho sakta ke aik waqt mein teen ya chaar baatein durust hon. laazmi baat hai ke ikhtalafi aara mein charon mein se aik sahih aur baqi ghalat hon gi. is baat se hum yeh samajh satke hain ke aadmi khuwa kitna bara kyun nah ho agar woh nabi nahi hai to usay ghalti lag sakti hai. is liye ke nabi ko apni aara mein Allah  ki wahi durust karti hai .
jo log khud soch kar apni aqal o qiyaas se kaam letay hain unhein ghalti lagti hai. is liye lazim hai ke aap apni ankhen khuli rakhen. har baat ka Dayanat  daari se jaiza len. usay prkhin is ke dalail ka jaiza len aur agar is mein ghalti nikal aaye to apni raye durust kar len .
hamaray muashray mein ahal hadees dyobndi briloy tableeghi jamaat jamaat islami ahal tasawuf Shiah  aur is terhan ke kayi giroh paye jatay hain jo deen ke bunyadi mamlaat jaisay shirk o toheed se le kar fqhi o froay mamlaat tak mein aik dosray se mukhtalif hain. yeh to ho nahi سکتاکہ yeh sab durust hon ge. agar yeh sab har maslay mein durust hain to phir deen islam navz billah aik chistaan sun-hwa. aur yeh bhi kehna sahih nahi hai ke un mein se sirf aik giroh poori terhan sahih hai aur baqi teen chaar giroh mukammal tor prghlt hain. is liye ke un sab ko deen sadiiyon ke taamul se mila hai jis mein ulma ki aara bhi shaamil hui hain aymh o فقہا ke Fatawa bhi ghair muslimon ke nazriaat bhi jaisay falsafah yunan waghera aur Zanni  o qatee zaraye se milnay wala deen bhi .
ab sawal yeh hai ke aadmi kis ke sath jurey kis ki baat manay. is sawal ka jawab yeh hai ke un mein se hamein kisi giroh se nahi jurna balkay hamein haq se jurna hai. jo unheen garohoon ke paas hai magar is mein un garohoon ke –apne nazriaat shaamil ho chuke hain. kisi ne –apne nazriaat daal diye hain. kisi ne apni fiqa aur kisi ne –apne falsafay taraash liye hain. kisi ne naye Minhaj  daryaft kar ke is mein daakhil kar diye hain aur kisi ne saaray deen ki majmoi tabeer aisay kar di hai ke dekhnay mein to deen hi lagta hai magar woh deen nahi raha .
is daur mein jabkay baatein aik se ziyada ho gayi hain aur giroh be shumaar ban gaye hain to is mein Saleh  aadmi ke liye is ke siwa kuch charah nahi hai ke is deen tak puhanche jisay nabi akram sale Allah  alaihi wasallam le kar aaye thay. bilashuba woh unheen garohoon ke paas ho ga magar sara kisi aik ke paas nahi. is ka kuch hissa kisi ke paas mehfooz hai aur kuch hissa kisi avrke paas .
deen ke is daur mein hamein –apne apane hue deen ko parkhte rehna chahiye. quran aur sunnat متواترہ ko miyaar banatay hue aik aik amal ka jaiza le لیناچاہیے. aik aik nazriye aur aqeday ko parkh lena chahiye. har har giroh se raye leni chahiye un ke dalail ko janna chahiye aur jis ki baat quran o sunnat se ziyada qareeb lagey usay apnaana chahiye. jo log deen mein aisi mushaqqat nah kar satke hon unhein kam az kam aisa zaroor kar lena chahiye ke woh do teen ulma se mutaliq ho jayen jin ke baray mein un ka khayaal ho ke woh quran vasant ko samajhney walay hain aur deen ke sath mukhlis hain magar yeh faisla mehez jazbaat aur –apne kisi talluq ki bana par nahi hona chahiye balkay nihayat Dayanat  daari se achi terhan to l- parkh kar hona chahiye .
haq parasti ke liye darj zail cheeze zaroori hain
lekin agar aap naik niyati se kharray hue jitni namaz aap ko aati thi sahih parhi magar kahin ko yi ghalti ho gayi aur aap ko pata nahi chala haan agar aap ko pata chal jata to aap durust karne ke liye tayyar hotay to yeh ghalti wali namaz ka bhi aap ko sawab miley ga. is liye ke khata o nasiyan par Allah  taala ne muwakhza nahi rakha .
hum ne ikhlaq ke chay pehlu oopar bayan kiye thay
