is ke maienay yeh hain ke hum har kaam ke karte waqt apni niyat ko misbet رکھیںیعنی sabr ka taqaza yeh hai ke hum –apne iraadon aur niton mein hamesha misbet pehlu se agay barheen maslan
is ke maienay yeh hain ke –apne ird gird rehne walay logon ko dekhnay ki nazar yeh banani chahiye ke woh log insaan hain aur jis terhan hum se ghalti ho jati hai un se bhi ho sakti hai. is liye un ke har amal ko is waqt tak misbet nigah hi se dekhna chahiye jab tak un ka shar khil kar samnay aajay. agar aadmi ki yeh tarbiyat nah hui ho to usay quran o hadees bhi faida nahi day satke. is liye ke is ki aadat baton ke ghalat rukh ko dekhnay lag jati hai. chunancha jab is ka koi bhai band is ke sath neki bhi kere to is mein se bhi kisi aisay pehlu ko nikaal laita hai jo manfi ho. chunancha is ke baray mein quran ka hukum yeh hai ke logon ke baray mein badgumaani nah ki jaye .
quran Majeed  jaisi kitaab ko agar ghalat zavia nigah se dekhen ge to woh bhi hamari gumraahi ka baais ban jaye gi. jaisay quran Majeed  میںآنے wali misalon ka zkrkrte hue farmaya gaya hai
is se Allah  bahuton ko gumraah karta aur bahuton ko hadaayat deta hai. gumraah magar un فاسقین hi ko karta hai .
is aayat mein yeh baat wazeh ho rahi hai ke quran jaisi kitaab ke baray mein bhi yeh baat khud quran hi keh raha hai ke aik fasik ke liye yeh kitaab ya is mein misalein jo aslan hadaayat ke liye aayi hain woh gumraahi ka baais hain. to is ke maienay yeh hain ke agar fasik aadmi ke zavia nigah se baat ko samjha jaye to quran ke nataij aur hain aur agar مومنانہ nigah se quran ko samjha jaye to is ke smrat aur hain .
yahi sabr ki aazmaysh hai ke aap –apne zavia nigah ko hamesha durust rakhen. is maqsad ke liye zaroori hai ke aap har waqt apni ng_h daari karen .
apni ng_h daari se hamari morad yeh hai ke aap har waqt –apne af-aal o afkaar par nigah rakhen ke kahin woh jadah mustaqeem se hatnay to nahi paar hai hain. agar koi falsfiyana behas koi amli mushkil koi moima aap ko ghalat rastay par daal raha hai to is prghor karen ke yeh baat kya hai jo mere dil mein ubhar rahi hai. usay دبایے nahi balkay usay ٹٹولیں کریدیں is ko samjhain aur samajh kar mutayyan karen ke yeh kya baat hai. phir is ke sawal ka jawab talaash karen. agar khud nah dhoond saken to ulma aur samajh daar logon se madad len jo deen mein baseerat rakhtay hon .
apni ng_h daari ka dosra pehlu amal se mutaliq hai. hum jo bhi amal karte hain is ke asraat hamaray dil vdmagh par parte hain. jo hamari shakhsiyat ki taamer karte hain. agar hum achay kaam karen ge to hamari nafsiat mustahkam aur sehat mand banay gi. agar hum ghalat raahon aur amlon mein par gaye to is se hamari nafsiat par buray asraat parrin ge. yeh aamaal hamaray tajarbay ki soorat mein hamari raye par bhi assar andaaz hotay aur hamari aadaat takhleeq karte hain. aik aadmi ghar mein baith kar ghalat sochon mein para rahay to bahar nikal kar is ki nazar pak nahi ho sakti. isi terhan ghalat amal karne walay ka dimagh bhi saaf aur pak baz nahi ho sakta .
aap ko apni sohbat aur yaari dosti ke lehaaz se apni ng_h daari karni hai. achi sohbat achay zehen ko takhleeq karti hai aur buri sohbat buray zehen ko. isi liye quran mein un logon ke paas bethnay se roka gaya hai jo quran ki ayaton ka mazaaq uratay thay. is liye ke is se wohi zehen banay gajs ke asraat imaan o amal dono par parrin ge .
is zamane mein baaz deeni log bhi zehni ayashyon ke liye baaz aisay logon ke paas uthte baithy hain ke jahan woh nuqta aafrini aur Bazla  sanji ke johar dikhata aur phir aahista aahista ghalat nazriaat ke aisay aseer ho jatay hain ke phir baat samjhaye nahi banti .
isi liye ummat mein shuru se yeh nazriya mojood raha hai ke sohbat Saleh  tra Saleh  knnd ke achi sohbat tujhe acha banati hai. quran Majeed  ne jab بدووں ki taraf se imaan ki kamzoree dekhi to unhein yeh mahswara diya ke qoul o feal mein sachey logon ki sohbat uthao. chunancha farmaya
sabr ke lehaaz se aik zehni aazmaysh yeh hai ke hum har haalat mein –apne aqeedah ko durust rakhen. maslan توحیدیا kkhuda ki bandagi aur isi se isteanat talabi hamesha barqarar rahay. agar kisi ke aulaad nah ho to aam tor se dekha gaya hai ke woh kkhuda se mayoos ho kar peeron faqeero ke darwazay par jatay darbaron par nazrane charhatay un ke naam ki نیازبانٹتے aur agar un se bhi kaam nah banay to phir un ko chore کردوسروں ke darwazay par dhakkay khatay phirtay hain. yeh sab be sabr y hai. is se aap ka aqeedah kharab ho jata hai. yeh shirk hai ke aap yeh manen ke insanon mein se koi ایساہے jo kkhuda ke faislon ko tabdeel kara sakta hai. yeh kkhuda ki sifaat ka inkaar aur is ki zaat ki ihaanat hai .
isi terhan mohabbat rasool mein logon ke haan ghallo wujood mein aata hai aur woh Allah  aur nabi mein farq مٹادیتے hain. halaank yeh esaiyat ka nuqta nigah hai. islam mein nabi ko Allah  ya is ka beta nahi mana jata magar hamaray aqeday isi qader kharab ho chuke hain. hum insanon ko kkhuda ka taqaddus dete aur yun شرکاے kkhuda ki aik lambi fehrist par imaan rakhtay hain. yeh nazriaat hamaray isi terhan ki zaroraton se phootay hain jin mein aik aulaad ke nah honay ka hum ne zikar kya. isi terhan aik چیزدوزخ ka khauf aur hamari be amli hai. is ne un shrka y kkhuda ko wujood بخشاہے jo hamaray شفاعتی banin ge. chunancha jab woh akhirat mein شفاعتی banin ge to yahan is duniya mein bhi yeh tasawwur wujood mein aaya ke woh duniya mein bhi kkhuda ke faislon ko badal satke aur unhein hamaray haq mein tabdeel kraskte hain. chunancha jin logon ne –apne aap ko tasawuf mein qutub o Abdal  banaya un ke darbaron aur mazaron par tht ke tht lag gaye. woh پوجے gaye un se isteanat talabb ki gayi aur kkhuda ki raah mein anfaq ke bajaye un ke naam ke نذارنے aur نیازیں بٹیں. yeh sab istiqamat o sabr ke manafi hai .
aazmaysh khuwa kaisi bhi kyun nah hawas mein kkhuda ki rehmat se mayoos nahi hona chahiye. kkhuda se mayoos hue baghair is ki Raza  par raazi rehna is muamlay mein sabr hai .
is baab mein hum un cheezon se behas karen ge jo hamein sabr karne mein mumid o Muawin  hain
sabr ke baray mein hum oopar yeh parh aaye hain ke yeh Allah  taala ke sath hamaray talluq se peda hota hai. yeh talluq jitna sahih hoga sabr ke husool mein itna hi mumid o Muawin  hoga. sahih honay ke maienay yeh hain ke yeh talluq sahih rukh mein aur poooray shaoor ke sath ho. sahih rukh ke maienay yeh hain ke hum kkhuda ko achi terhan jaan kar is ke sath talluq banayen. jaisay duniya mein agar hum insanon ko sahih nah pehchanen to hum un se basa auqaat nuqsaan utha baithtay hain. theek aisay hi agar hum ne kkhuda ko sahih nah pehchana to hum kkhuda se aisi ghalat tawaquaat par baithy rahen ge jinhen poora karna Allah  taala ki Safa  t- aur hikmaton ke khilaaf ho. is liye hamaray kkhuda ke sath sehat mandana talluq ke liye yeh zaroori hai ke hum is ki sifaat aur sunan ko jaan kar is ke sath talluq ustuwar karen. taakay ghalat tawaquaat aur ghalat nazriaat ki bana par hamara talluq naaqis banay aur ain is waqt shakista ho jaye jis waqt hamein is talluq ki sab se ziyada zaroorat ho .
is baat ko hum aik misaal se samajte hain. aik buzurag saari zindagi Allah  taala ki ibadat karte rahay. aur –apne tasawurat ke mutabiq is zeam mein rahay ke aisi riyazat ke baad Allah  taala ki madad isi terhan aati hai jis terhan ibrahim par aag thandhi karne ke liye Allah  ki madad aayi. aur is taweel riyazat ke douran mein unhon ne kkhuda se koi cheez talabb nahi ki. taakay woh aisay kisi mauqa par Allah  taala se –apne liye madad maang saken .
chunancha aik dafaa yun sun-hwa ke bad o baran ka nihayat sakht tufaan aaya jis ke nateejay mein selaab agaya. sara gaon garqaab ho gaya. log bachney ke liye lakri shehteer aur har terhan ki cheezon se madad lainay lagey magar un buzurgon ke nazdeek yahi mauqa tha ke woh apni riyazat ka faida haasil karen. chunancha unhon ne aasman ki taraf sir uthaya aur pukare ke ae Allah  aaj to khud mujhe aakar bachaaye ga. mein kisi cheez ki madad haasil nahi karoon ga. barish hoti rahi aur woh buzurag pani mein kkhuda ke haath ka intzaar karte rahay. aik shehteer tairta sun-hwa un ke paas se guzra magar unhon ne yeh keh kar usay nah roka ke aaj Allah  mujhe bachaaye ga. mein is ki madad nahi lon ga. thori der baad aik bhens tairti hui aayi. woh is par baith kar bhi bach satke thay magar unhon ne kaha aaj Allah  mujhe bachaaye ga itnay mein pani un ki gardan tak agaya. thori der baad gaon ke kuch log kisi takhtay par tertey hue aaye unhon ne kaha baba jee aajao marjao ge magar باباجی ne muskura kar socha aaj mujhe Allah  bachaaye ga. phir unhon ne takhtay par tairnay walon ko un ki madad lainay se inkaar kar diya. itnay mein pani un ke sir tak pahonch gaya. phir fojion ki aik kashti tairti aayi unhon ne باباجی ki laash ko uthaya aur pani se bahar le aaye. is qissa se baat wazeh hui ke kkhuda ke sath talluq aisi tawaquaat par wabasta kar ke banaya gaya ke jo is ki sunnat aur sifaat ke khilaaf tha. kyunkay woh is duniya ko parda ghaib mein reh kar chala raha hai is liye woh kisi ki –apne haath zahir kar ke madad nahi karta nah kere ga. woh takhta shehteer tairti hui bhens hi Allah  ke haath thay jin ko thaam kar bahar aana chahiye tha .
is ke maienay yeh hain ke Allah  taala ke saaray kaam is ke ilm o hikmat par mabni hotay hain. woh jazbaat ke tehat nahi hotay. Allah  taala kisi ki shakal o soorat aur hasb o nasb dekh کرفیصلے nahi karte balkay woh –apne ilm aur hikmat ke paish e nazar yeh sab kar rahay hotay hain. chunancha is ke kisi rasool ki ummat mein se hona ya kisi ki aulaad hona is baat ki kisi ko mustahiq nahi banati ke woh hamaray sath un cheezon ki bana par koi maamla kere. ایساوہ –apne ilm hikmat aur danai ki bana par karta hai .
Allah  sahib ilm hai. duniya mein honay wala har waqea azal se is ke ilm mein hai. is ke liye koi cheez haadsa nahi hai. woh ghaib aur zahir dono ko jaanta hai. yahan aik baat ضمنا arz karna chahta hon ke Allah  taala ki tamam sifaat is se kisi bhi haalat mein judda nahi hoten. theek isi terhan is ki sift ilm bhi har waqt is mein mojood rehti hai. chunancha jab hum par koi museebat utri ho to yeh har gaz khayaal nahi karna chahiye ke Allah  is se be khabar ho گایایہ ke usay to is ka ilm nahi tha .
Allah  taala ke baray mein hamara yeh nazriya ke woh har waqeye ko jaanta hai hamaray liye baais tasalii o itminan aur sahara ban-na chahiye. hamari morad yeh hai ke jab hamaray oopar koi museebat o mushkil aaye to yeh khayaal nahi aana chahiye ke hamara maalik وآقا is se be khabar hai. ab hamara pursan haal koi nahi hai balkay is ke bar aks yeh khayaal karna chahiye ke duniya hamari is museebat se be khabar hai magar woh karsaaz is se waaqif hai jis ne usay is museebat se nikalna hai .
jab aadmi ko museebat ke waqt yeh yaad rahay ke is ki mushkilaat daur karne wala is ki museebat se bakhabar hai to yeh is ke liye aik bara sahara hai jo usay bila muawza aur bulaa inqita muyassar rehta hai .
phir yeh bhi dekhieye ke woh hamari salahiyaton hamari افتادطبع hamari dili khwahisaat aur hamaray halaat ka nihayat bareeqi se ilm rakhta hai. chunancha agar woh hamein kisi mushkil mein daaley ga to un tamam p_hlvon se woh mushkil aazmaysh nihayat napi tali aur mutawazan ho gi. agar hum sahih zehen ke sath is ka muqaabla karen to hum bulaa shuba aazmaysh ki is Bhatti  se kundan ban kar nikleen ge. aur sabr bhi hamaray liye aasaan tar hoga .
yeh duniya Allah  ne banai hai woh usay chala raha hai. is ki nigah musalsal is ki nigrani kar rahi hai. aisa nahi hai ke koi museebat zada ho aur Allah  is se waaqif nah ho. nah aisa ho sakta hai ke koi zulm kar raha ho aur Allah  is se be khabar ho. is liye is baat se pareshan nahi ho na chahiye ke agar hum mazloom hain to hamari daad rassi nahi ho gi ya ho gi to haakim ki be khaberi ki wajah se poori poori daad rassi nah ho sakay gi koi kami reh jaye gi. be sabr a to is ko hona chahiye jisay daad rassi ki umeed nah ho ya jo be insafi ki tawaqqa rakhta ho. maslan agar kisi ne mere bhai ko qatal kar diya hai to woh aaj to qanoon ki girift se bach sakta hai lekin kkhuda ki pakar se kaisay bach sakta hai .
quran ne kaha ke is zameen o aasman ki hudood se bhaag kar kaisay nikal jao ge. aakhir tum sab aahista aahista –apne rab ki taraf khnche ja rahay ho aur aik din is ke samnay kharray ho ge. is din kkhuda ka saamna har kisi ne karna hai. aadam o Hawa  ke zamane se le kar qayamat se pehlay peda honay walay aakhri aadmi tak ne yeh din dekhna hai aur is mein jo kuch is ne kya hai usay bhughtna hai. is duniya mein agar aap ke sath koi zulm o insafi ho khuwa is ki kamiat o ahmiyat zarra barabar ho woh bhi samnay aaye gi. aur is par aap ko poora poora badla miley ga. qayamat ke baray mein quran ki yeh tasreeh ke is din Khairoo  shar mein agar kisi ne aik zarra barabar amal bhi kya hai to usay dekhe ga. yani is se ajar o gunah paye ga. har mazloom ke liye khoo sh khaberi hai aur har zalim ke liye aik waeed o dhamki. jis mazloom par yeh haqeeqat munkashif ho woh –apne zaalmon se badla lainay ke liye kyun kar hudood se tajawaz kere ga aur usay badla lainay ki aisi jaldi bhi nahi ho gi ke ماوراے adalat intiqam laita phiray. gharz yeh ehsas ke mein Allah  ki nigahon mein hon woh har waqt meri har haalat se waaqif hai yeh cheez hamein aik noiyat ka itminan ataa karti aur hamein be sabri se rokay rakhti hai .
Allah  sahib hikmat hai. duniya mein honay wala har waqea is ki danai baseerat aur is ke hakeemana maqasid ka haamil hota hai. hamari nigah is par nahi honi chahiye ke yeh museebat kitni barri hai balkay is par honi chahiye ke yeh kyun aayi hai. is liye ke is hakeem o khaibar se yeh tawaqqa nahi ke woh bulaa wajah hamein kisi ibtila mein daal day gavh یقینادر j baala maqasid hi ke liye hamein aazmaata hai. is ke hakeem honay ka taqaza yahi hai ke is ke har kaam ko hikmat par mabni samjha ja ye is liye ke hum yeh jaan chuke hain ke is ki yeh sifaat is se kisi haalat mein bhi allag nahi hoten. is liye yeh jaan lena chahiye ke agar woh kisi ko saza bhi day raha ho to woh bhi hikmat se khaali nahi hoti .
is ko hum aik adna darjay par maa ki misaal se samajh satke hain jo –apne bachay ko badtameezi karne ya mehnat nah karne par sirf is liye saza deti hai ke is ki aadato ka bigaar is se daur ho ya is ka mustaqbil tareek nah ho. maa ke zehen ki yeh hikmat baaz auqaat betay se oojhal hoti hai aur woh maa se baaghi ho jata hai jo ke jaaiz nahi hai. agar maa –apne betay par yeh sitam is liye torti hai ke woh sudhar jaye is ka mustaqbil sanwar jaye woh anay walay dinon mein pareshan nah ho to kya kkhuda maa se ziyada hakeem nahi hai aur woh is se ziyada mustaqbil se bakhabar nahi hai yahi is ka Aleem  o hakeem hona hai jo hamaray liye baais itminan hai .
is hikmat ka aik pehlu yeh bhi wazeh rehna chahiye ke basa auqaat hum yeh khayaal kar rahay hotay hain ke hamara kaarobar chal jana chahiye hamein mulazmat mil jani chahiye hamaray aulaad honi chahiye lekin maamla is ke bar aks rehta hai. is ki wajah yeh hoti hai ke Allah  ka ilm yeh keh raha hota hai ke yeh sab kuch hamaray liye mustaqbil mein nuqsaan ka baais ho ga. woh hamein is nuqsaan se bachanay ke liye is sab kuch se mahroom rakhta hai .
mushkilaat mein hamein jo cheez ‫n sabr ke liye badarqa faraham karti hain un mein se Allah  ki do sifaat rauf o Raheem  hain .
rauf is zaat ko kehte hain jo doosron ki mushkilaat daur karne wali un ko kulfaton se nikaalte ka ihtimaam karne wali ho. jabkay Raheem  is zaat ko kehte hain jo inayat o meharbani karne wali ho logon ke liye istehqaq ya bulaa istehqaq naematain nazil karne wali ho. goya rehmat aam hai aur Rafet  khaas jo is waqt mutharrak hoti hai jab aadmi mushkil mein ghira sun-hwa ho .
is sift ke tazkeray se jo baatein mein samnay lana chahta hon un mein se aik baat yeh hai ke Allah  taala ki sift yeh to hai ke woh mushkilaat mein se nikalta hai lekin yeh nahi hai ke woh mushkilaat mein dalta hai. Albata  is ne yeh bataya hai ke woh bhook jaan jane ke khauf اورنقص amwal se hamari aazmaysh karta hai. is ka nateeja yeh nikalta hai ke hum aisi zaat ke baray mein jo rauf o Raheem  hai har gaz yeh khayaal nah karen ke woh khuwa makhuwa hamaray o par masaaib nazil karta rehta hai .
asal haqeeqat yeh hai ke woh jab bhi hamein mushkil mein dalta hai to woh mehez mushkil mein daalnay ke liye aisa nahi karta balkay is ka maqsad jaisa ke oopar wazeh ho chuka hai hamari bhalai hoti hai. dekha jaye to haqeeqat mein Rafet  ka تقاضایہی hai .
quran Majeed  میںیہ sift o allah rauf بالعباد ke alfaaz ke sath bhi aayi hai. quran Majeed  ka yeh usloob nihayat darja dil Nawaz  hai. isi terhan yeh sift un allah بالناس لرؤف uraheem ke alfaaz ke sath bhi aayi hai. surah baqra mein yeh sift jahan aayi hai woh maqam is sift ko samajhney ke liye nihayat ahem hai. is liye aik nazar is maqam par daal lena bhi faiday se khaali nah hoga .
yahan Allah  taala ne tbdily qibla ka hukum day kar is mutawaqqa radd amal ka zikar kya hai jo bilkhushoos yahood ki taraf se samnay anay wala tha. woh sadiiyon se beeet almuqaddas ko qibla banaye hue thay. ab is qibla se hatna un ke liye behar haal aik dushwaar kaam tha. is liye Allah  taala ne yeh hukum dete hi farmaya hai ke Allah  ne yeh hukum ummat Musalmah  ko کاملا deen ibraahimi par qaim karne ke liye diya hai aur is liye diya hai ke woh yeh parkhe ke kon rasool sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ki pairwi karta hai aur kon ultay paon wapas chala jata hai .
is hukum ke yeh dono maqsad bitanay ke baad farmaya ke bulaa shuba yeh kaam mushkil hai lekin hum ne yeh hukum is liye nahi diya ke hum tumahra imaan zaya kar den. Allah  to logon ke sath rauf o Raheem  hai .
yahan se hamein yeh baat maloom hui ke tbdily qibla jaisi aik barri aazmaysh mein daalnay ke baad jis ke mushkil honay kokhod rauf o Raheem  ne tasleem kya hai a lillah taala yeh farmatay hain ke mein rauf hon is liye tum par aisi aazmaysh nahi daloon ga jis ki wajah se tum imaan se haath dho betho. isi usool ko is ne aik umomi usool ke tor par bhi bayan kya gaya hai ke
doosri baat Rafet  ke pehlu se samajhney ki yeh bhi hai ke rauf o Raheem  ki nazar takhleeq aadam ke is maqsad par rehti hai ke is ne usay aazmaysh ke liye peda kya hai nah ke is duniya mein hamesha ki zindagi guzaarne ke liye jabkay hum aksar auqaat is haqeeqat ko faramosh kiye rehtay hain .
woh aik hamdard maa ki terhan jo apnay nalaiq bachay ke mustaqbil se pareshan rehti hai usay kabhi ڈانٹتی hai kabhi kostey hai kabhi pyar se behlaati پھسلاتی hai kabhi lalach deti aur kabhi saza ki waeed sonaati hai. zara is nigah se un آزمایشوں ko dekhieye aur sochiye ke woh kitna pyar karne wala kitna kher khuwa aur kis qader mushkilaat se nikaalte wala hai .
woh is nadaan maa ki terhan nahi hai jo –apne bachay ko is liye چلنانہیں sikhati ke kahin gir kar usay chout nah aajay. woh jahan jati hai usay goad liye rehti hai. bzahir woh betay ki hamdard hai lekin haqeeqat mein dekha jaye to woh –apne betay ki dushman hai. usay betay ke un dinon ki parwa nahi hai jab woh usay goad mein utha kar kahin nah le ja sakay gi. phir yahi beta usay gaaliyan day ga ke to ne mujhe chalna kyun nahi sikhaya tum ne Meer  y sath yeh dushmani kyun ki aur woh usay yeh nah keh sakay gi ke mein ne to tumhari hamdardi ki thi .
jis maa ne –apne betay ko paon prchlne ke liye mushkilaat mein nahi dala woh is waqt hamdard nazar aati thi magar woh haqeeqat mein rauf nahi thi aur jis ne –apne betay ko bachpan mein mushkil mein dala woh is waqt sakht nazar aati thi magar haqeeqat mein woh rauf o hamdard thi .
hum chunkay bachon ki terhan –apne mustaqbil ko aksar faramosh kiye rehtay hain is liye hamein woh maa achi lagti hai jo hamari aaj ki raahat ka khayaal rakhti hai jabkay door andaish aadmi ko woh maa achi lagey gi jo is ke kal ki raahat ko bhi malhooz rakhay. Allah  aisi hazaar maaon se bhi Ziyaad  hay hamdard hai. is liye mushkil se mushkil waqt mein bhi yeh khayaal rakhna chahiye ke Allah  یقیناہمیں paon پرچلنا sikha rahay hain اورسیکھنے ke douran mein thokrain to hamein lagen gi .
aik nazar ab Raheem  ki sift par bhi daal lijiye. Raheem  is zaat ko kehte hain jo inayat o meharbani karne wali ho logon ke liye istehqaq ya bulaa istehqaq naematain nazil karne wali ho. rehmat ke chand ahem pehlu samjhna hso l- sabr ke liye nihayat na guzeer hai. rehmat Allah  taala ki aisi sift hai ke is se baaz mkatb fikar ne ajeeb o ghareeb falsafay taraash rakhay hain jis ki wajah se basa auqaat Allah  taala ki zaat hi ki nifi ho jati hai ke woh koi baasol zaat hai bhi ya nahi aayye ab rehmat ke hawalay se chand baatein samajh len
rehmat ko aik aur pehlu se bhi samajh lena chahiye. aam tasawwur is ke baray mein yeh hai ke is mein sirf inayat o shafqat hi shaamil hai lekin quran Majeed  se yeh maloom hota hai ke saza bhi rehmat ka laazmi hissa hai. is ke baghair rehmat ka tasawwur takmeel nahi paata. is baat ko hum aik misaal se samajh satke hain. farz karen aik maa ke do betay hain. aik shararti hai aur dosra shareef aur seedha saadha hai. shareer bacha kisi mauqa par shareef ko tang karta hai to maa jo dono beton ki yaksaa maa hai woh is terhan ke mauqa par hamesha yeh nahi kar sakti ke –apne shareef bachay ko dilaasa day kar chup karaday balkay usay shareer bachay ko saza bhi dena padtee hai taakay shareef bachay ka dil thanda ho aur usay mehsoos ho ke jo is ki shararat se is ne takleef uthai thi is ki saza usay mil gayi. agar woh maa aisa nah kere to woh shafeeq maa nahi hai. maa ke is ravayye se maloom sun-hwa ke shafqat aik bacha ki saza ke baghair takmeel nahi paati .
theek isi usool ko malhooz rakhtay hue Allah  taala ne quran Majeed  mein farmaya hai
Allah  ne –apne oopar rehmat wajib kar rakhi hai is liye woh zaroor qayamat ke din tumhen jama kere ga .
yahan dekhieye ke Allah  taala ne qayamat ke din akthakr ke hisaab kitaab ko apni rehmat ka taqaza qarar diya hai. rehmat ka yahi woh usool hai jis se Adal  پھوٹتا hai. chunancha saari duniya is baat par mutfiq hai ke muashray mein honay walay juraim ki saza di jaye taakay mujrimeen ke liye Ibrat  ke sath sath مظلو meem ki daad rassi bhi ho. quran Majeed  ne qoum Quresh  ke injaam bad ki khabar di to farmaya
un se laro Allah  unhein tumhare hathon se saza dena chahta hai woh unhein shikast o ruswai se do چارکرے ga اورتمھیں ghalba o nusrat se aur is terhan momnin ke seenay thanday kere ga .
morad yeh hai ke saza ki takmeel sahaba ke seenon ki thandak ke baghair namukammal hai. surah inaam میںیہی wajah hai ke kufar ki jarr katne پراللہ ka shukar ada kya gaya hai
so Allah  parvar-digaar aalam ka shukar hai ke zulm karne walon ki jarr kaat di gayi .
zahir hai ke shukar ka haqeeqi mauqa rehmat o inayat hai isi liye yahan is inayat par kkhuda ka shukar kya gaya hai ke duniya un لاخیروں se pak kar di gayi .
is liye hamein chahiye ke jab hum par koi mushkil nazil ho to usay rehmat Ellahi ke khilaaf nah samjhain. is mauqa par wohi rawayya ikhtiyar karna chahiye jo nabi sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ne –apne aik sahabi ko bemari ke mauqa par tajweez farmaya tha ke is bemari ko –apne gunaaho ka kaffara samjhoo .
jaisay hum ne arz kya ke Allah  ki koi sift kisi waqt bhi is se judda nahi hoti is liye khayaal rehna chahiye ke is ki sift Rehma  is ki sift qaim بالقسط se judda ho kar amal nahi karti balkay woh jab reham karta hai to kabhi bhi insaaf aur qist ke khilaaf nahi hota .
is ko aik tamseel se samjhiye aik aadmi par Allah  ki har inayat lagta hai ke aasman se barah ast baras rahi hai. duniya ki koi Nemat  nahi jo is ke ghar mein nah ho magar is ka کرداراور is ka amal nihayat sar kashi aur nihayat deen napsndi balkay کفرکا hai to kya is par Allah  ki rehmat qareen insaaf hai
har aadmi jo is duniya mein aaya hai usay fitrat vdiat hui hai. jis mein neki ka شعوراوراس ki Halawat  is ke liye ajnabi nahi hai. is liye yeh دنیاطلب aadmi bhi neki karta hai. agarchay woh duniya mein shohrat panay ya mehez qalbi taskeen ke liye karta hai. to انما الأعمال بالنیات ke usool par usay duniya mein is ka ajar milna chahiye. agar unhein duniya mein ajar nah miley aur akhirat mein bhi un ki un nakiyon ka ajar nah miley to yeh na-insafi ho gi .
is liye usay yeh ajar mukhtalif sooraton mein day diya jata hai kisi ko muashray mein buland mansab ataa kar ke kisi ko shohrat یادولت day kar aur kisi ko guru aur peshwa bana kar kisi ko muqtadir aur firaon bana kar gharz jo soorten is duniya ke tang نائے mein mumkin hain un sab sooraton mein kisi ki neki ke mutabiq usay ajar mil jata hai. is terhan aik neki goya aik tadbeer ka darja pa kar akhirat tak jane se mahroom ho jati hai .
is liye yeh farmaya gaya hai ke jo log neki is terhan karte hain ke unhein duniya hi mein ajar mil jaye to unhein yeh ajar duniya hi mein mil jaye ga. Albata  akhirat mein un ke hissay kuch nahi aaye ga. is liye dekhieye ke aik be insafi wali rehmat kitna bara insaaf hai .
yeh duniya Allah  taala ne jis terhan banai hai woh darasal jore ke usool par banai hai. yahan har cheez naaqis hai aur usay is ka jora mukammal karta hai. maslan hum raat mein aaraam kar satke hain magar kaam poori terhan nahi kar satke. din mein kaam bharpoor tareeqay se kar satke hain magar aaraam nahi kar satke. chunancha raat din mard وعورت zameen وآسمان khushi vghm aaraam o takleef gharz har har pehlu se dekhen to kkhuda ki yeh kaari giri hamein nazar aaye gi ke is ne har cheez ka jora banaya hai jo aik dosray ke nuqs kopora karte hain. isi terhan Allah  ne kher o shar ka jora bhi banaya hai. yani neki bhi hai aur badi bhi gham bhi hai اورخوشی bhi. yeh charon cheeze hamari aazmaysh hi ke liye banai gayi hain. is duniya mein gham museebat nuqsaan mout aur deegar takaleef aisi aazmaysh hain ke hamein un par sabr karna hota hai. yeh sab cheeze bhi raahat chain naffa zindagi aur khoshion ka jora hain. jis terhan hum ne oopar jana ke har cheez –apne jore se mil kar mukammal ho ti hai isi terhan khushi aur gham bhi aik dosray ki kami ko poora karte hain .
yeh duniya chunkay aazmaysh ke liye banai hai. is liye nah akela gham is aazmaysh ko sahih maienay mein aazmaysh banata hai aur nah akeli khusihyan. yani agar yahan gham hi gham ہوتااور khushi ka tasawwur hi nah hota to insaan ke liye gham ki aazmaysh be maienay ho jati usay takleef zaroor rehti مگرراحت ke nah honay ki wajah se is aazmaysh mein aisa nuqs ajata hai ke gham ki haalat wohi ho jati hai jo is waqt hamari محدودیت ki hai. yani maslan hum urr nahi satke to is ki nah hamein koi aazmaysh mehsoos hoti hai aur nah is ka gham o qlq hamein satata hai. takleef agar laazmi hissa ho jaye raahat nah rahay to itna bara khlal waqea hota hai ke kaayenaat hi namukammal si dikhayi deti hai .
is liye hamein yeh yaad rakhna chahiye ke yeh gham ورنج ka aana shikwah o shikayat ke liye nahi hai balkay nematon ke ehsas un ki ahmiyat jatlane aur hamein azmaane ke liye hai. tamam masaaib ko isi rang mein dekhna chahiye. museebat mein gum ho jane ke bajaye usay samajh kar is mein kamyaab ho kar niklny ki koshish karni chahiye .
hum is duniya mein arsa daraaz se hain. aur hum sadiiyon ke is sfrmin yahan rehne ke aisay aadi hue hain ke usay hum ne apni manzil hi samajh liya hai. chunancha hum yahan hamesha jeena chahtay hain lekin haqeeqat yeh hai ke yeh duniya faani hai. is ki har shai ko zawaal hai aur khud un zameen o aasman ko jo mohakam o saabit nazar atay hain aik din khatam ho jana hai. is lambay arsa mein hum yeh bhool chuke hain ke hamein akhirat mein kkhuda ke huzoor mein paish hona hai .
chunancha insaan is nasiyan ki wajah se apni manzil ko bhool kar rastay hi ko manzil samajh laita hai. jabkay usay akhirat ki tayari ke liye peda kya gaya hai aur woh apni saari msaay isi duniya ko bananay mein sirf kar deta hai. is ke bar aks chunkay Allah  taala ko nasiyan la-haq nahi hota is liye woh musalsal hamari akhirat ke liye tayyar y ke asbaab peda karte rehtay hain. hum aik mushkil جوبلاشبہ sangeen ho sakti hai par rotay rehtay hain jabkay akhirat ki nakami se barri museebat koi nahi hai. hamein agar woh pareshani yaad ho to hamein duniya ki mushkilaat kabhi itna pareshan nah karen agar hum unhein apna زادسفر bana len .
is liye Allah  ke nazdeek is duniya ki barri se barri tangi bhi dozakh ki tangi se barri nahi hai. kisi aurat par zulm hona usay Talaq  ho jana kisi aurat ka be auladi ki wajah se be ghar kya jana saas aur baho ke jhagron mein is par ilzaam lagna kisi ka kaarobar thap ho jana agar kisi ko un mein se guzar kar jannat milnay wali ho to Allah  ke nazdeek yeh mamooli baatein hain .
woh jaanta hai ke aik bewa aik mutalqa ya aik ilzaam zada aurat ya zulm o sitam ka sataya ho اکوئی aadmi jo bhi un آزمایشوں mein kamyaab ho kar jannat mein aajay ga woh un mushkilaat ko –apne liye Nemat  samjhay ga kyunkay agar woh mushkilaat is par nah aatin to woh dozakh ki museebat se nijaat nah pa sakta. isi liye hadees mein aaya hai jis maa ke teen bachay mar gaye aur woh صابروشاکر rahi to yeh gham is ke jannat mein jane ka sabab ban jayen ge .
is ko bhi maa hi ki misaal se samajte hain. maa jab –apne bachay ko churee chaako se khailtay hue dekhatii hai to is se woh chaako chean layte hai. is liye ke woh yeh janti hai ke is waqt churee se mahroom hona itni barri takleef nahi hai jitni barri takleef usay is churee se haath kat jane ki wajah se ho gi. is liye woh bachay ke cheekhnay aur chalanay ke bawajood is se churee chean layte hai. aur agar woh chup nah kere to woh usay mazeed  daant bhi deti hai .
is se hamein Allah  ki pay dar pay آزمایشوں ka bhi aik sabab maloom ho jata hai ke jab hum Allah  ki kisi aazmaysh par sahih rawayya ikhtiyar nahi karte to woh hamein mazeed dantta hai taakay hum sambhal jayen .
hum bil umoom un mushkilaat par ziyada gazabb naak hotay hain jo hamaray doston ya Aziz  rishta daaron ke kisi iqdaam ki wajah se hum par aati hain. maslan hamaray muashray mein chughli gheebat taang khenchna dhoka dahi zar aur zameen ke jhagray aisay aam juraim hain ke aadmi un se pareshan ho kar doston se jhagar parta behan bhaiyon se qata talluq kar laita un ke baray mein terhan terhan ki bdgmanyon ka shikaar ho jata maa baap ko ghar se nikaal deta hatta ke baaz auqaat unhein ya –apne aap ko mout ki neend sulaa deta hai .
is ki wajah yeh hai ke woh un saaray جھگڑوںکو aazmaysh ke tor par nahi laita. woh yeh khayaal karta hai ke yeh sab kuch woh apni poori azadi se kar rahay hain is liye agar mein unhein khatam kardoon un se natha toar lon un ko gaaliyan day lon un ko maroo paiton to saaray maslay hal ho jayen ge. chunancha woh aisay iqdamaat ke baad mazeed mushkilaat ka shikaar ho jata hai .
aisa shakhs asal mein Allah  ki rabobiyat aur is ki hikmat ka inkaar karta hai. quran Majeed  ke mutalay se maloom hota hai ke duniya ka koi kaam is ki th_hrayi hui taqdeer aur is ke hakeemana faislon ke khilaaf ruba amal nahi hota. jab soorat e haal aisi hai to kya yeh rishta daar yeh gheebat o chughli karne walay jo yeh sab kuch kar rahay hain آیاخدا ki mohlat ke baghair kar rahay hain
agar hum yeh inkaar kar den ke woh Allah  ki di hui mohlat ke baghair aisa kar rahay ہیںتو yeh kkhuda ki al-wahiyat o hakeemana control ka inkaar hai aur agar hum yeh yaqeen rakhtay hain ke unhein Allah  hi ne mohlat di hai to phir yeh bhi maanna parre ga ke Allah  ki yeh mohlat bila waja nahi hogi. is ke peechay mazkoorah maqasid mein se koi nah koi maqsad zaroor paish e nazar ho ga yani hamari islaah hamaray gunaaho ko jhaarna waghera. chunancha is نقطۂ nazar se ab –apne un sathiyon ki kargzari ko dekhieye to jo gunah o khata woh kar rahay hain woh agarchay apni marzi se kar rahay. is se woh yaqeenan gunah kama rahay hain lekin mohlat chunkay Allah  ne di hai is liye woh hamari tarbiyat aur aazmaysh ka samaan bhi kar rahay hain .
woh hamaray oopar zulm dhaa ne jaisa kbirh gunah kar rahay hain magar hamaray liye sabr karne ki soorat mein jannat ki raah khol rahay hain. abbu لہب aur abbu jahel ki sazishon aur resha dwanyon ne aik taraf un ke liye dozakh taamer ki to doosri taraf sahaba rizwan Allah  allahum ke kirdaar ki taamer ki. woh jaisay jaisay yeh harkatein karte gaye sahaba ka imaan mazboot hota gaya. goya Allah  taala ne is kaayenaat ka nizaam aisi hikmat aur tadbeer se banaya hai ke aik shar bhi wujood mein aata hai to so kher –apne daman mein le kar aata hai .
is nuqta ke hal honay ke baad jab mein –apne gird o nawah mein logon ko –apne oopar ilzaam dete taanay dete terhan terhan ki sazishain karte daikhon - to yeh kaisay ho sakta hai ke mein unhein apna dushman qarar dun mere to woh mohsin hain dushman to woh –apne hain. woh meri tarbiyat ka samaan apna nuqsaan kar ke kar rahay hain. chunancha un ko taanay ka jawab dainay ke bajaye mujhe un ki islaah ka sochna chahiye. un par taras aana chahiye ke woh apni tabahi ke gharrey khoud kar mujhe un mein utarna aur utar kar niklana sikha rahay hain .
lekin mujhe yeh faida bas isi soorat mein mil sakta hai ke jab میںان ki un harkaat ko Allah  ki aazmaysh samajh kar usay apni tarbiyat o islaah ka zareya bunun. agar mein ne un ki eent ke jawab mein pathar utha ke day mara to mein bhi un jaisa hon. mein ne bhi ghalti ka irtikaab kar dala hai. is ke baad kher ka darwaaza mere liye band ho jaye ga .
hadees mein syedna abubaker razi Allah  anho ka waqea milta hai ke koi sahib un ko gaaliyan dete rahay aur kuch der tak abubaker chup rahay lekin kuch der baad unhon ne bhi jawab dena shuru kya to nabi sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ne mun phair liya. abbu baker razi Allah  anho ke poochnay par aap ne unhein bataya ke jab tak tum khamosh rahay to farishtay jawab dete rahay aur jab tum jawab dainay lagey to woh chalay gaye. aik terhan se Allah  un ki taraf se difaa karta raha. firshton ka jawab dena ghair msmoa tha. hamein nahi maloom ke woh galion ke jawab mein kya jawab dete rahay hon ge lekin woh jo kuch tha woh abubaker razi Allah  anho ke liye aik kher tha jis se woh jawab dainay ke baad mahroom ho gaye .
theek isi terhan ki mehroomi ka shikaar hum ho jatay hain jab hum buraiee ke jawab mein buraiee ka rawayya ikhtiyar karte hain. hum doosron ki buraiee ka un se badla jaaiz aur aadlanh tareeqon se le satke hain lekin unhein maaf karna
quran Majeed  yeh kehta hai ke tum kisi ki buraiee ka badla achhai se do. is ke alfaaz hain ke tum kisi ki buraiee ko neki se dhakel kar hata do. bajaye is ke ke tum badi ko dhakelnay mein badi hi ki raah ikhtiyar karo to yeh tumhen Allah  ki inayaton se mahroom kar day ga. agar tum is ki raah mein zindagi busr karo aur logon ki buraiee ka difaa neki se karo to is se nah sirf yeh ke tumahra dushman tumahra Aziz  dost ban sakta hai balkay tum bhi woh khush qismat ban jao ge jinhen kkhuda apni hikmaton se نوازتاہے. dekhieye quran Majeed  ne is rawayya ko aik barri khush bakhti qarar diya hai aur usay sabr ka Samrah  qarar diya hai
neki aur badi barabar nahi ho sakti. tum buraiee ka Ahsen  cheezon se difaa کرو- to tum dekho ge ke woh jis ke aur tumhare darmiyan adawat thi wohi tumahra garam josh dost ho ga. magar yeh woh Danish  mandi hai jo sirf sabr karne walon ko millti hai. aur yeh sirf un ko millti hai jo barray naseebay walay hotay hain .
husool sabr ke liye aik bunyadi cheez yeh bhi hai ke hum Allah  taala ke wadon par yaqeen rakhen. jis terhan hum ne sifaat Ellahi mein jana hai ke Allah  taala ki Safa  t- hamaray liye sabr ke husool ka zareya hain isi terhan Allah  ke waday bhi hamaray liye aik sahara hain. Allah  taala ne quran Majeed  mein kuch waday nabi akram sale Allah  alaihi wasallam se kiye hain kuch waday sirf sahaba rizwan Allah  allahum se kiye hain aur kuch waday bani noo aadam se kiye gaye hain. jaisay neki karne aur buraiee se bachney par jannat ka wada آزمایشوں mein saabit qadam rehne par imaan zaya honay se bachanay ka wada kisi par is ki himmat se ziyada boojh nah daalnay ka wada isi terhan buraiee karne par dozakh ki saza ka wada waghera .
وما صبرک ila billah mein Allah  ke yeh waday bhi shaamil hain jo hamein sabr ka hosla bkhshte hain. quran Majeed  jab yeh kehta hai ke tum Allah  ke baghair sabr nahi kar satke to jis terhan is ki zaat is ki sifaat jaisa ke hum oopar parh aaye hain hamaray liye aik sahara hain theek waisay hi yeh is ke waday bhi hamaray liye sahara hain .
yeh waday mushkilaat aur آزمایشوں mein hamaray liye is liye sahara hain ke jab hamein mushkil kaam karna parre to hum unheen wadon ke bil par mushkil ke bawajood neki karne aur is par saabit qadam rehne mein kamyaab ho satke hain. agar hamein kkhuda ki taraf se daad rassi aur inaam ki tawaqqa nah ho to shayad har qadam par neki se haath دھوبیٹھیں balkay agar hum yeh kahin ke agar jannat aur dozakh ka tasawwur nah ho to shayad insanon ki nihayat hi qaleel تعداددنیا mein neki par qaim rahay. is liye ke insaan apni tabiyat mein maqsad ke liye jeeney wala hai. agarchay aksar woh choti choti cheezon ko apna maqsad bana laita hai .
insaan umeed ke saharay bohat kuch kar laita hai. neki ke maidan mein yeh umeed kkhuda ke wadon se wujood Pazeer  hoti hai. un saharon se jo umeed peda hoti hai woh shab o roz ki kulfaton mein thandhi sun-hwa ke jhonkay ki terhan hamari timardari karti hai. masiihaa ban kar hamara ilaaj karti hai. kabhi kam aur kabhi ziyada itminan ataa karti hai. aur hum is itminan ke saharay raah hayaat par chaltay chalay jatay hain. jo log is imani qowat se mahroom hain woh is umeed aur un saharon se be khabar honay ki wajah se kayi bimarion ka shikaar ho jatay aur kuch log khud kashi tak kar letay hain aur kuch doosron ko qatal kar baithtay aur baaz nafsiati amraaz ka shikaar ho kar be mout mar jatay hain. yeh be umeedi zehni دباؤ gham o ghusse aur mayoosi
quran Majeed  ne آزمایشوں ke anay ke jo asbaab bayan kiye hain un ke ilm se bhi aadmi ko sabr haasil hota. is liye ke yeh ilm aadmi ko wajohaat bta kar tasalii deta hai aur tasalii ki wajah se usay sabr ajata hai. yeh ilm Allah  taala ki sunnat ibtila se mutaliq hai. aur ibtila ya aazmaysh is duniya ki haqeeqat hai. jis ke sahih tasawwur ke baghair yeh duniya nah samajh mein anay wala moima hai .
chunancha yeh ilm agar zehen se utar jaye to is ko taaza rakhna chahiye aur is maqsad se quran Majeed  ka mutalea bhi bohat mufeed hai. isi terhan is mauzo par ahal ilm ki tahreeron ka mutalea bhi aik had tak mufeed rahay ga. Albata  quran Majeed  ke mutalay se hamari morad is ki tilawat nahi hai balkay is ko samajh kar parhna matloob hai. is liye ke samjhay baghair is ki talemaat se aagahi na mumkin hai .
quran مجیدکے mukhtalif maqamat se maloom hota hai ke namaz bilkhushoos t_hjd ki namaz husool sabr ka aik nihayat mufeed zareya hai. سورۂ muzammil میںآیا hai ke t_hjd ki namaz dil jamee aur qoul ki pukhtagi ke liye bohat mufeed hai. yani t_hjd ki namaz paanch waqt ki namaz se ziyada mo-asar hai is liye ke ziyada geherai aur tawajah se parhi jati thi. aur is mein nabi sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ko hukum tha ke quran thehr thehr kar yani usay samajh samajh kar parha jaye. taakay t_hjd apna kaam apni kaamil soorat mein kar sakay .
سورۂ muzammil mein quran Majeed  ne is namaz ki haqeeqat do lafzon mein bayan ki hai
–apne rab ka zikar kar aur is ki taraf Khalq  se kat kar gosha geer ho ja .
is aayat se maloom ho taa hai ke nabi sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ko jo t_hjd ada karne ke liye farmaya gaya tha to is ke jo aadaab aap ko sikhayiye gaye thay un mein aik yeh bhi tha ke aap usay yaddehani aur zikar ka zareya banayen aur is ke zariye se kkhuda ke daman rehmat mein gosha geer ho jaya karen .
molana amin Ahsen  islahi is hukum ki تفسیرکرتے hue farmatay hain
yeh Allah  taala ne aap ko is baat ka tareeqa bataya ke jab jab logon ki dil aazari se dil aazurda ho to tum un naqdron se kat kar –apne rab ke daman rehmat mein gosha geer ho jaya karo. aur is ke liye tumhen is ke siwa kisi cheez ki zaroorat nahi ke tum is ke naam ko yaad kya karo. to woh khud tumhen apni panah mein le le ga .
yeh amar yahan malhooz rahay ke Allah  taala ke tamam naam is ki sifaat hi ki tabeer hain aur un sifaat hi par tamam deen o Shariat  aur saaray imaan o aqeedah ki bunyaad hai. un sifaat ka sahih ilm مستحضر rahay to aadmi ki pusht par aik aisa lashkar giran is ke Muhafiz  ki hesiyat se mojood rehta hai ke shetan ki saari faujein is ki nigahon mein par kah ke barabar bhi waqat nahi rakhtin. woh –apne aap ko pahoron se bhi ziyada mustahkam mehsoos karta hai .
aur agar kkhuda ki sifaat ki sahih yad dasht is ke andar baqi nah rahay ya kamzor ho jaye to phir is ka aqeedah be bunyaad ya kamzor ho jata hai jis ke sabab se is ko munafiqeen ki terhan har bijli –apne hi Khirmen  par girty nazar aati hai .
yahi woh zikar hai jis se kkhuda ke daman rehmat mein gosha Gary  ki raah khulti hai. un sifaat ki yaad aik hisaar ki terhan hamaray gird Muhafiz  ban kar mojood rehti hai. jaisay aik bacha kisi khauf naak cheez se dar kar apni maa ki goad mein panah geer ho kar saari duniya ke khauf o dehshat se be niaz ho jata hai theek waisay hi aik bandah is yaad ke taaza honay ke baad kkhuda ke daman rehmat mein choup kar saaray gham bhool jata hai. terhan terhan ke hamlon se –apne aap ko Mamoon  khayaal karta hai .
namaz ka yahi pehlu hai ke agar usay namaz mein peda nah kya jaye to namaz –apne asraat peda nahi karti. phir is ke baad aadmi terhan terhan ke masnoi saharay talaash karta hai usay un ka nasha to lag jata hai magar maslay hal aur gham daur nahi hotay .
namaz ehad abodit ki yaad hai jo sabr ko taqwiyat deti hai. quran Majeed  yeh kehta hai ke اقم الصلوہ لذکری meri yaad ke liye namaz qaim karo. خداکی yaad ehad bandagi ki yaad ko taaza karti hai. yeh aadmi ko batati hai ke woh kkhuda ka bandah hai jo آزمایشوں mein is liye dala gaya hai ke woh –apne aap ko aik Saleh  بندۂ kkhuda saabit kere. yeh cheez is ki ghaflat o nasiyan ko daur karti hai jis mein par kar woh be sabra ho raha tha. is yaad ke taaza honay se woh aik haqeeqat shanaas ban kar اٹھتاہے. haqeeqat is par roshan hoti aur is idraak haqeeqat se is par apna maqam khilta aur woh aik taaza dam sipahi ki terhan maidan amal mein dobarah kood jata hai .
qiyam ruku aur sajda batadreej aadmi ki ghaflat ko daur karte hain. qiyam mein kkhuda ka kalaam usay kuch haqeeqaton ki taraf tawajah dilaata hai. ruku isi bandagi o سرفگندگی ke jazbay ka awleen izhaar hai jis ke baad sajda is ki aakhri shakal hai. yeh tenu aamaal hum namazon mein aik se ziyada martaba karte hain. jo hamein yaad dilatey aur haqeeqat shanaas banatay hain .
oopar yeh baat wazeh ho chuki hai ke t_hjd kkhuda ki rehmat میںگوشہ Gary  ke liye raah hamwar karti hai. yeh gosha Gary  darasal kkhuda se talluq ka aik pehlu hai. namaz kkhuda ke sath taqarab ka talluq peda karti hai. سورۂ Alaq  mein Allah  taala ne farmaya hai ke واسجد واقترب sajda kar wa aur kkhuda ke qareeb ہوجاؤ. yeh qurbat agar chay ghair mehsoos hai aur hum is ki kefiyat o mahiat ko samajh nahi satke lekin yeh qurb یقیناخدا ki panah ke liye aik isteara hai. is qurb ke maienay yeh bhi hain ke namaz husool sabr mein isteanat karti hai .
quran Majeed  mein nabi sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ko mushkilaat ke waqt kayi بارحصول sabr ke liye namaz ka hukum tasbeeh o Tehmid  ke alfaaz mein diya hai. agarchay yahan namaz hi ka hukum diya gaya hai magar yeh baat wazeh hai ke nmazka yeh hukum is ki do خاصیتوں ko samnay rakh kar diya gaya hai. namaz ke yeh do pehlu aisay hain ke jo manwi ya zehni asraat rakhtay hain. agar hum namaz mein tasbeeh o Tehmid  ko soch samajh kar ikhtiyar karen to is ke kuch nataij nikaltay hain. yeh nataij hamaray liye sabr karne میںممدو Muawin  hain. un dono خاصیتوں ke maienay aur asraat ka jaiza hum agli stor mein len ge .
jis ke maienay yeh hain ke خداے wahid ki paki bayan ki jaye. paki bayan karne ke maienay yeh hain ke yeh mana jaye ke Allah  ke kisi feal aur faislay mein koi ghalti nahi hai. jab Allah  ke faislay mein koi ghalti nahi hai توپھریہ sawal peda ho ga ke hamein phir yeh takleef mein kyun dala gaya hai. hamein bhook khauf aur mout ki kisi aazmaysh mein dala hai to is ki wajah kya hai. jab is ka faisla ghalat nahi hai aur woh hamaray oopar museebat nazil kar raha hai to yeh baat wazeh hai ke phir is ke paish e nazar koi maqsad ho ga. aur woh maqsad yahi hai ke Allah  ne hamein azmaane ke liye yeh mushkil bhaije hai .
tasbeeh ka yeh tasawwur hamaray زاویۂ nigah ko بدلتاہے. hamein yeh sakata hai ke tum yahan kuch panay ke liye aaye ho. is liye Allah  hamein آزماتاہے. aur azmaane ke liye jaisi aazmaysh honi chahiye waisi woh nazil karta hai. mera aap ka har amal kkhuda ki Mansha  o azan se doosron ke liye aazmaysh bantaa hai. isi terhan doosron ka har amal hamaray liye aazmaysh bantaa hai. isi wajah se deen ka mutalba doosron ki buraiee par yahi hai ke hum sabr karen. jo aadmi aisay mawaqay par sabr nahi karta aur intiqam le laita hai to agar is ne insaaf se intiqam liya hai to Allah  taala is se muwakhza to nahi karen ge magar dar haqeeqat is ne duniya daari wala maamla kya hai. deen ka taqaza poora nahi kya. is liye woh barray kher se mahroom reh jaye ga .
hamd tasbeeh ka dosra rukh hai. tasbeeh yeh batati hai ke Allah  taala ki zaat o sifaat aur af-aal mein koi aib nahi hai aur حمدیہ batati hai ke saari achi sifaat is میںہیں. is ke tamam af-aal اوراوصاف kher hain. is se jo bhi amal cheez aur khayaal wujood mein aata hai woh kher hai. hamaray oopar anay wali aazmaysh museebat zulm sab kher hi ki aik qisam hai. is liye ke aik pehlu se woh aap ke liye aik mushkil sawal hai jis ka imthehaan mein aap ko jawab dena hai aur doosri taraf woh aik nerceri hai jis ki paneeri se khaaliq kaayenaat kher ki parwarish karta hai. مثلاجس aadmi ka beta sarkash o bad-qamash ho is ki mout maa baap ke liye museebat hai magar muashray ke liye kher hai. is usool se hum yeh baat samajh satke hain ke yeh kaayenaat jis usool par bani hai woh yeh hai ke har cheez dohray rukh ki hai is ka aik rukh acha hai aur dosra bzahir bura magar haqeeqat yeh hai ke yeh dono pehlu –apne nataij ke aitbaar se achay hain .
khaaliq kaayenaat شرکی kookh se kher peda karta hai. سورۂ kahaf mein mazkoor aik nojawan ki kashti -کا tootna bzahir aik bura haadsa hai magar haqeeqat mein woh aik kher ko wujood mein lata hai. har haadsa khuwa is ka kher hamein foran nazar aaye ya nah aaye darasal kher ko peda karne ke liye hota hai. aik aadmi ka marna kaarobar mein kasaad ka aana bemari ka la-haq hona zehni aziat se do chaar hona ghar se nikala jana gharz sab hadsaat hain un ka zahir bura hai magar un sab se kher bar aamad hota hai .
usay hum aik haqeeqi misaal se samajte hain. mere paas aik qazia aaya ke aik ghar mein chaar paanch bhai ikathay rehtay thay. un ke walidain ka intqaal ho chuka tha. aik bhai un mein se bihaya sun-hwa tha. baqi sab kunware thay. jo bihaya sun-hwa tha bas wohi kamata tha. baqi sab parhay likhay thay magar aaraam talabi ki bana par kamanay nah jatay thay. ya phir koi wajah thi. un ki bhabhee sab ke kaam bhi karti aur un ki jali kati bhi sunthee thi. koi teesray chouthay saal is ki biwi ne insaaf ka taqaza kya. dono miyan biwi ke khayaal mein masla ka hal sirf yeh tha ke woh allag ho jayen magar woh bhaiyon ko chore kar nahi ja satke thay. is liye ke aik to kamate nahi thay dosray un ke ghar sambhalay ke liye biwiyan bhi nahi theen .
kisi ke kehnay proh mere paas aaye to mein ne kaha ke bhaiyon ko bhi بلاؤ. pehlay to raazi nahi hue magar mere israar par un ko laya gaya. mein ne sab larkoon ko mukhtalif zimma dariyan sonpin aur barray bhai ko allag ho jane ka mahswara diya. yeh un larkoon ke liye aik nagehani museebat zaroor thi magar mein ne unhein bataya ke tumhare liye bil akhir baais kher ho gi. un ke liye barray bhai se aik mah ka kharcha bhi dila diya yun unhein aik mahinay ke andar –apne liye rozgaar bhi haasil karna tha aur ghrke saar y kaam bhi. chunancha woh bhai aur bhabhee jis ko unhon ne –apne ghulam bana kar rakha sun-hwa tha woh aik Nemat  gum gashta ban gaye. aik mahinay ke andar hi un bhaiyon mein se aik ko mulazmat تومل gayi magar ghar ke kaam kar ke unhein ehsas sun-hwa ke un ki bhabhee ne kya boojh utha rakha tha. gharz unhein andaza nahi tha ke kis Nemat  ko paker woh nashukray banay rahay. un ke dilon mein bhai aur bhabhee ki mohabbat jaagne lagi un ka ehtram peda sun-hwa aur saal daidh saal ke andar hi woh sab kamanay lag gaye. un ki aaraam talabi aahista aahista rukhsat ho gayi .
is misaal se yeh baat wazeh hui ke bhaiyon ke liye barray bhai ka chore kar chalay jana un ke liye islaah ka baais bana. yani aik museebat bzahir museebat thi magar un ke mustaqbil ke liye aik Naveed  thi jis ne unhein نکمے insanon ke bajaye kaam karne walay log banaya. is ke baad mujhe nahi maloom ke kya sun-hwa is liye ke unhon ne aik daidh saal hi mujh se rabita rakha. is liye ke pehlay woh mujh se shaaki thay phir mutmaen hue to zahir hai itminan ke baad log sab bhool jatay hain .
yeh misaal kkhuda ke sazawar حمدہونے ki taraf rahnumai karti hai yani Allah  taala ne is duniya mein shar ke peda honay ka jo imkaan rakha hai woh bhi is liye ke is se kher bar aamad ho. quran Majeed  mein jab Allah  taala ne insaan ko is duniya mein sahib Iqtidaar  bananay ka elaan kya to firshton ko is Iqtidaar  ka manfi rukh samnay aaya to unhon ne kkhuda se kaha ke hum to aap ko سزاوارتسبیح o taqdees samajte hain phir aap ke Shayan  shaan yeh nahi ke aap is duniya mein koi aisa kaam karen ke jo shar ko wujood bakhshay. Allah  taala ne un ko samjhaya ke mein jis sahib Iqtidaar  ko wujood bakhash raha ہوںصرف shar hi peda nahi kere ga balkay is ki nasal mein bohat ziyada Akhyar  aur صالحین bhi hon ge .
is qissay se hamein yeh baat maloom hoti hai ke kkhuda ki taqdees aur khata se is ka munazza o pak hona is se khatam nahi hota ke woh shar ko kisi kher ke liye wujood mein anay day. is liye hamein sirf is wajah se pareshan nahi ho na chahiye ke hamein museebat la-haq ho gayi hai balkay yeh dekhna chahiye ke is se hamaray liye kher bar aamad ho ga. is khayaal ke sath barri se barri museebat mein bhi umeed qaim rehti hai. aadmi ke hauslay qaim rehtay hain .
quran Majeed  ka farmaan hai ke is ne insaan ko peda kya phir is ki taqdeer th_hrayi aur phir usay is ki taqdeer ke rastay par chala diya. goya aadmi neki اوربدی jo kamata hai woh twapni azadi aur ikhtiyar se kamata hai lekin jo maqam اورمرتبہ usay haasil hota hai jo maal o doulat usay haasil hoti hai woh is ki taqdeer ka likha sun-hwa usay mila hai. is liye nah usay gurbat par karhna chahiye aur nah apni doulat o izzat par Nazaan  hona chahiye .
yeh sab kuch aisa hi hai jaisay achi aur buri soorat wala hona. nah achi soorat taqqabur o غرورکی wajah hai aur nah barri se barri mushkil mayusion ka baais. yeh sab kuch Allah  ki taqdeer hai jo is ne apni khaas hikmaton ke sath th_hrayi hai jin mein kuch hikmaton ko hum ne oopar seekha hai. aadmi ki shakal o soorat is ki salahiyaten is ka maal o doulat sab ka talluq is ki qismat se hai nah ke is ke zaati istehqaq aur is ki qabliyat ka sila اورحق. is liye un ka hona ya nah hona منشاے Ellahi hai jis ka muqaabla hosla اوردانش mandi se karna chahiye .
agar koi mushkil aadmi par aaye to aadmi ko achay dinon ko yaad karna chahiye jin mein Allah  ne is par inayateen ki hoti hain. aur yeh khayaal karna chahiye ke agar Allah  ne woh din dukhaay thay aur guzar gaye to yeh din bhi baqi nahi rahen ge yaqeenan achay halaat naseeb hon ge. is se bhi aadmi ko sabr aur tasalii haasil hoti hai. سورۂ alum nshrh mein yahi tareeqa nabi sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ki tasalii ke liye ikhtiyar kya gaya hai .
husool sabr ke oopar bayan kardah yeh tenu tareeqay asal میںخدا ke sath aadmi ke talluq ki bunyadain faraham karte hain. aadmi ka yeh shaoor jitna gehra hoga utnahi is ka kkhuda se talluq gehra aur mustahkam hoga. aur jitna is ka talluq is se gehra hoga isi qader woh mushkilaat mein sabr kar sakay ga .
lekin hum un nematon se haqeeqi maienay mein faida nahi utha satke agar hum un mushkilaat mein Allah  se taalib madad nah hon. Allah  se madad baaz tasawurat ke sahih kiye baghair talabb karna basa auqaat namumkin hota hai aur basa auqaat be maienay hai is liye munasib maloom hota hai ke un tasawurat ko sahih kar liya jaye .
akhirat aik abdi badshahi ka naam hai jis mein nematon ko zawaal nahi hai. jo mil گیاوہ hamesha ke liye mil gaya. hum aap ko isi manzil ka sacha raahi ban-na chahiye. aur jab kabhi is manzil ko bhoolnay lagen to foran yaad dehani haasil karen –apne ird gird تواصی بالحق ka mahol banayen jahan aap doosron ko aur dosray aap ko haq baat ki naseehat karen ke kal tum qayamat ke din kya karo ge. isi naseehat se sabr haasil ho ga .
quran Majeed  ne soor ۂ asar mein hamein hukum diya hai ke hum aap aik dosray ko naseehat karen haq ki aur is par qaim rehne yani sabr ki. is hukum ki wazahat karte hue ustaad graami janab Javed  Ahmed  sahib ghamdi likhte hain
yeh amal agar hamaray mahol mein aam ho jaye to hamein har waqt yaddehani karanay walay muyassar rahen ge. yaddehani darasal hamein akhirat ka bhola sun-hwa sabaq yaad dilaati hai. aakhir t- ka sabaq agar hamein har waqt yaad rahay to yeh hamaray liye husool sabr ka baais hai. isi wajah se quran Majeed  ne
nakiyon par qaim rehne mein muawnat karne wali cheez Allah  ki raah mein anfaq bhi hai. yeh anfaq zkoh aur fitraana waghera ki soorat mein to har musalman کرتاہی hai مگرکچھ is ki lazim soorten aam musalmanoon ko maloom hi nahi hain. woh yeh samajte hain ke zkoh dainay ke baad un ki asal zimma daari poori ho gayi. ab jo bhi woh kharch karen ge woh nfli hai. is par hamara muwakhza nahi ho ga .
yeh ilm ki kami hai. darasal zkoh ke ilawa bhi anfaq ki kuch shakalain aisi hain ke jo hum par lazim hain. un mein miqdaar aur waqt mutayyan nahi hai lekin yeh baat lazim hai ke is mein dena na guzeer hai .
zkoh ke ilawa anfaq ka aik saada usool hai ke hamaray maal mein Allah  taala ne mahroom aur sayel ka haq rakha hai. jo log mahroom hon un ki madad karna aur jo darwazay par ajayeen un ko dena hamaray malon mein se haq muqarrar kya gaya hai. jis se maloom hota hai ke jo rizaq Allah  taala hamein dete hain woh darasal sirf hamara nahi hai balkay is mein kuch dosray sayel o mahroom bhi hissa daar hain. is maqsad se aisay logon ke liye –apne maal mein se kuch hissa zaroor muqarrar karna chahiye .
dosra usool nusrat deen ka hai. jab deen ka wujood khatray mein ho to is ki madad karna lazim hai. is silsilay mein agar zaroorat Maqtazi  ho deen par ibtila aisi shadeed ho ke apni zaroorat se barh kar sab kuch dena parre to dena hoga. log usay nfli cheez samajte hain halaank yeh lazim hai .
isi usool par muashray malik aur qoum ki abtlamin madad karna bhi hatta almaqdoor lazim hai. aisa karne se insaan mein Awsaf  Hamida  wujood mein atay hain jin ke zariye se insaan mein sabr peda hota hai .
Allah  ki raah mein kharch aisa hi assar rakhta hai jaisay namaz. سورۂ tauba mein anfaq ko qurb Ellahi ka sabab qarar diya gaya hai isi terhan namaz کوقرب Ellahi ka sabab qarar diya hai. Allah  se yeh talluq insaan mein nakiyon ki taraf melaan aur buraiyon se ijtinab ka Wasf  peda karta hai. neki par qaim rehna aur buraiyon se مجتنب rehna hi sabr hai .
rozana quran ka aik itna hissa jis se kkhuda ka koi pegham haasil hota ho parhna –apne liye lazim kar lena chahiye. usay kisi achi Tafseer  ki roshni mein nah bhi samjha jaye to quran Majeed  ki تکرارا war tasreef ayaat se is ke mukhtalif pehlu samnay atay hain aur baat aam qaari ko bhi samajh ajati hai .
is mein baaz taalib ilmoon ko mein ne yeh mahswara diya ke woh molana amin Ahsen  islahi Rehma  Allah  ki Tafseer  tadabbur quran agar teen se paanch mah mein khatam kar saken to unhein quran ke majmoi paighamaat ka qadray behtar feham haasil hoga. jab unhon ne aisa kya to unhein mein ne bhi –apne nazriaat aur rawaiyon mein mukhtalif mehsoos kya hai is liye ke quran tarbiyat karta hai .
jo log taalib ilm nahi hain aur itni miqdaar mein nahi parh satke to agar woh koi acha tarjuma hi do teen mah mein parh liya karen to is se wohi nataij haasil ho satke hain agar chay woh aahista hon ge aur kayi dafaa ke aisay mutalea ke baad haasil hon ge. aadmi agar ترجمۂ quran ko samajh kar parhnay ka mamool bana le aur har teen chaar mah mein quran ka tarjuma khatam kar liya kere to khud usay bhi un herat angaiz asraat ka ehsas hoga .
is mein tarjuma koi bhi liya ja sakta hai magar firqa waranah tasbat ki bana par tarajum ke حواشی mein aur baaz auqaat tarajum ke wast mein aisay izafay kar diye jatay hain ke jis se tarjuma apna asal rang kho deta hai. agar yeh mumkin ho ke koi aisa tarjuma jisay likhnay walay kisi firqay ke mubalagh o nmaynd hay nah hon to woh ziyada behtar hai. mere khayaal mein مولاناامین Ahsen  sahib islahi Rehma  Allah  ka tarjuma jo allag bhi choup gaya hai woh is maqsad ke liye ziyada behtar hai .
lekin agar is raftaar se parhna mumkin nah ho to nah parhnay se behtar hai ke aadmi itna parhay jo hum ne sab se pehlay zikar kya ke jis se rozana aik pegham sa aap ko mil jaye .
logon ne quran ko jaadoyi kalmaat ki terhan samajh rakha hai yani usay samjhain ya nah samjhain woh assar zaroor karta hai. yeh nazriya ghalat hai. quran hadaayat o ضلالت ke qanoon ke mutabiq bas itna hi Faiz  yab karta hai jitni hamari aap ki sae hogi .

malbay taley dabey afraad ko mein se 2 afraad ki lashain nikaali gayi hain jabkay chaar afraad ko zakhmi haalat mein nikala gaya hai. hakkaam ka kehna hai ke afraad badastoor malbay taley dabey hue hain .

tahaffuz naswan qanoon ghair islami qarar
Islamabad islami nazriati council ne tahaffuz naswan bil mustard karne ke hawalay se hukoomat Punjab  ko tehreeri tor praagah karte hue apni tajaweez paish kar den .
Punjab  hukoomat ke naam khat mein islami nazriati council ne tahaffuz naswan mustard karne ki wajohaat bayan ki hain .
khat mein kaha gaya hai ke bohat se gharelo mamlaat mein shohar ki raye faisla kin hoti hai shohar se ikhtilaaf raye ki soorat mein biwi ko sarkari idaron se appeal ka qanoon khandani nizaam ki rooh ke khilaaf hai .
council ne qarar diya ke shohar ko ghar se bahar rehne ki saza bhi ghair sharai hai. aurat ke nan nfqe ka zimma daar shohar hai tahaffuz khawateen bil mein shaamil sazayen shohar aur biwi ke darmiyan dooria peda karne ka baais banin gi .
khat mein kaha gaya ke bil mein islam ke sulah aur maffi ki talemaat ko yaksar nazar andaz kya gaya hai .
islami nazriati council ki press release mein kaha gaya Punjab  assembly ke qanoon ka mauzo gharelo aur khandani mamlaat hain jis ke ahkam sarahatan quran o hadees mein aaye hain yani sharai ahkam se mutaliq qanoon hai. jis terhan Khyber  Pakhtunkhwa  assembly mein paish honay ke liye is mauzo par tayyar krd_h bil baqaida tay shuda aaeni tareeqay se islami nazriati konsl ke paas bheja gaya agar Punjab  assembly bhi yahi aaeni tareeqa kar ikhtiyar كرتی توبہتر hota .
konsl ne shaqq waar jaizay ke nateejay mein hasb zail daf-aat ko khilaaf islam qarar diya
qanoon كی dafaa mein Zikr  krd_h aksr تعریفات ghair sharai ghair wazeh aur ghair zaroori hain aur quran vhdis mein Tadeeb  par mushtamil islami ahkam se mutsadam hain .
dafaa sharai Tahkeem  ke khilaaf hai jis ka Zikr  quran Majeed  كی surah النسآ mein كیا gaya hai .
dafaa ghar mein rahaish ka haq dafaa haza sorة baqra aur surah Talaq  neez ahadees نبویہ mein مذكور nan ونفقہ كسوہ aur سكنی ke ahkam se mutsadam hai neez sharai haqooq ملكیت ke ahkam كی bhi manafi hai .
dafaa پروٹیكشن order qata rehmi aur mqatah كی hurmat وممانعت par Dalalat  krne wali نصوص se mutsadam hai. neez rishton ke taqaddus ke khilaaf honay ke sath sath fariqain ke darmiyan musalihat كی raah mein rkavt par mabni hai .

dafaa maali order sharai haqooq nafqa se mutsadam hai .
dafaa dakhla ka ikhtiyar surah noor aur mutadid ahadees mein مذكور sharai aadaab استیذان aur chadar chardiwari ke taqaddus ke khilaaf hai .
dafaa bra_ea_iat insaaf aur masawaat ke usoolon ke khilaaf hai. jaisa ﻛﮧ konsl apni aik Sabiqa  sifarish mein is كی wazahat كرچكی hai .
aik press release mein islami nazriati council ki janib se is silsilay mein mutadid sifarshaat bhi paish ki gayeen

pemra ke zariye tamam nashriyati idaron ko paband كرے ﻛﮧ woh khandani rishton ke taqaddus aur ahmiyat par programme كیا كریں .

panama leaks saazish nahi haqeeqat Imran
panama leaks mein bataya gaya hai ke kis terhan duniya bhar ke Ameer  aur taaqat war log apni doulat chhupanay aur tax se bachney ke liye beron malik asasay banatay hain. Islamabad mein insidadey dehshat gardi adalat mein pi TV aur parliment hamla case ke silsilay mein paishi ke mauqa par adalat ke bahar media se guftagu karte hue Imran  Khan  ne hukoomat ko aik martaba phir panama leaks par shadeed tanqeed ka nishana banaya .
Imran  Khan  ka kehna tha mein ne koi jurm nahi kya jinhon ne jurm kya hai aur bahar paisay bhijvaaye hain woh dan danatay phir rahay hain
Imran  Khan  ne qaumi ehatasab beuro se panama papers par tehqiqaat ka mutalba dohratay hue kaha ke agar neb ko apni saakh barqarar rakhni hai to fori tehqiqaat ka aaghaz kya jaye. yaad rahay ke guzashta roz bhi Imran  Khan  ne aik press conference ke douran qaumi ehatasab beuro se panama leaks par tehqiqaat ka mutalba karte hue kaha tha ke deegar mumalik ki terhan Pakistan  mein bhi is muamlay par tehqiqaat shuru ki jaye .
pi tea aayi chairman ne aik martaba phir wazeer e azam Nawaz  shareef ko tanqeed ka nishana banatay hue kaha ke Pakistan  se wafadar leaguei rehnuma Nawaz  shareef se poucheen paisa kahan se aaya. un ka kehna tha panama leaks koi saazish nahi haqeeqat hai wazeer e azam Nawaz  shareef ko batana parre ga ke paisa beron malik kaisay gaya
Imran  Khan  ne metro aur orange train project ki bhi tehqiqaat ka mutalba kya aur kaha ke maloom kya jaye ke yeh paisa kahan ja raha hai. pi tea aayi chairman ne dharnay ke shrka ke khilaaf muqadmaat ko bhi na-insafi qarar diya aur kaha ke jamhoori hukoomaton mein ehtijaj karna logon ka haq hai .
unhon ne dharnay ke shrka ke khilaaf muqadmaat khatam karne ka mutalba kya aur kaha ke agar insaaf nahi mila to woh phir sarkon par nikleen ge. yaad rahay pi tea aayi ne Imran  Khan  ki qayadat mein mein Islamabad mein din ka dharna diya tha jis ke douran unhon ne wazeer e azam Nawaz  shareef se istifa ka mutalba kya tha
is dharnay ke douran muzahireen ne Pakistan  tally vision aur parliment par hamla kar ke toar phore ki thi jis ke baad pi tea aayi ke mutadid karkunaan ke khilaaf muqadmaat darj kiye gaye thay
panama papers mein kab kya aur kaisay sun-hwa
aaj se aik saal qabal aik namaloom shakhs ne Germany  ke sab se barray akhbar زیدوئچے سائتونگ se rabita kya aur akhbar ko موساک فونسیکا ki androoni dastawizaat faraham karne ki peshkash ki .
akhbar ne is par razamandi zahir ki aur anay walay mahino mein is namaloom zariye ki janib se bhjwayi jane wali dastawizaat ki tadaad barhti chali gayi aur is saaray data ka hajam tira bayit tak pahonch gaya .
yeh sab kuch faraham karne walay zariye ne is ke badlay mein koi maali faida haasil nahi kya balkay security ke baray mein chand yaqeen d_hanyan mangeen .
زیدوئچے سائتونگ ne saaray data ka jaiza international knsorshim of انویسٹیگیٹو journalists ya
panama papers aalmi satah par is noiyat ke taawun ki aik bohat barri misaal hai .
un papers ke liye ki gayi tehqiqaat mein guzashta mahinay ke douran media tanzeemon se aur mulkon se talluq rakhnay walay ke qareeb sahafion ne hissa liya .
un mein bi bi si ki team Bartanwi  akhbar guardian francesi akhbar laa moond urgentine ke akhbar laa نیسیون shaamil hain .
is tehqeeq par kaam karne wali team ka pehla ijlaas washington myonkh London  aur للہیمر mein sun-hwa jis mein tehqeeq ke daira car ka taayun kya gaya .
panama papers ke data ke hajam ka andaza is baat se lagayen ke yeh WikiLeaks ki safarti kiblz of shore leaks lux leaks soys leaks ke saaray data se ziyada hai jis mein e mails pi d f faailan tasaveer aur موساک فونسیکا ke androoni data bees ka hissa bhi shaamil hai jo se tak phela sun-hwa hai .
do saal qabal aik aur zariye ne موساک فونسیکا ka data farokht kya tha magar woh hajam mein bohat chhota tha magar panama papers ke zariye afsha ki jane wali dastawizaat mein companiyon ke baray mein maloomat theen .
un maloomat ke nateejay mein tafteesh karon ne ke qareeb afraad ke dafatir par chaapay maaray jin mein کومرز bank bhi shaamil tha .
is ke nateejay mein کومرز bank each s each aur ہائپورنسبینک ne do crore yoroz ka jurmana ada kya .
موساک فونسیکا ne har shall company ke liye aik folder banaya sun-hwa tha jis mein company ki e mails raabtey baat cheet thekay aur un ki sakin shuda dastawizaat shaamil theen .
sab se pehlay tehqeeq karon ne saaray data ko behtareen karkardagi walay computeron par charhaya jis ke nateejay mein faailun ko parhnay mein aasani mili aur unhein tarteeb diya gaya jis ke nateejay mein sahafion ko is saaray data ko Google  ki search ki terhan khangalnay mein madad mili .
chand minton mein saaray data ko sudharnay ke baad is par tehqeeq ka kaam shuru sun-hwa jis mein har samnay anay walay naam ke baray mein sawalaat samnay laaye gaye ke un companiyon mein is fard ka kya kirdaar hai paisa kahan se aa raha hai paisa kahan ja raha hai kya strkchr kya qanooni hai
umomi tor par of shore company rakhna ghair qanooni nahi hai balkay of shore companian bananay ko barray pemanay par karobari saudey karne ki janib qadam samjha jata hai .
Ayaan  Ali  ko saza paanch crore jurmana paanch laakh dollar zabt
Pakistan  ke soobah Punjab  ke shehar Rawalpindi  ke custom collector ki adalat ne model Ayaan  Ali  ko beron malik ghair mulki currency smgl karne ka ilzaam saabit honay par paanch crore rupay jrmane ki saza sunai hai .
adalat ne Ayaan  Ali  ke qbse se bar aamad honay wali paanch laakh Amrici  dollar ki currency zabt karne ka hukum bhi diya hai .
Rawalpindi  ke custom collector Ali  Raza  ki adalat ne is muqadmay ka faisla sunaate hue istighasa ki janib se do gawahoon ke paish nah honay par unhein paanch paanch laakh rupay ki saza sunai hai .
un gawahoon mein Mohammad  owais aur mumtaz Hussain  shaamil hain. un ke baray mein bataya jata hai ke woh Ayaan  Ali  ke sahoolat car hain aur mutadid baar bulanay ke bawajood woh adalat mein paish nahi hue .
model Ayaan  Ali  ghair mulki currency beron malik smgl karne ke muqadmay mein paanch mah tak jail mein rahi hain aur is muqadmay mein un par frdِ jurm bhi aed ki ja chuki hai taham Ayaan  Ali  ke wukla ne special judge central ke is faislay ko Lahore  high court mein challenge kar rakha hai .
sabiq hkmran jamaat Pakistan  peoples party ke secretary general sardar lateef khosa is muqadmay mein Ayaan  Ali  ke wakeel ke tor par paish ho rahay hain .
mulzima ke wukla ki taraf se yeh muaqqaf samnay aaya hai ke woh custom collector ke is faislay ko adalat mein challenge karen ge .
model Ayaan  Ali  ko guzashta baras is waqt girftar kya gaya tha jab woh paanch laakh Amrici  dollar se zayed ki raqam Dubai  le kar ja rahi theen .
Pakistan  ke qanoon mein das hazaar Amrici  dollar se ziyada ki raqam beron malik le kar jane ki ijazat nahi hai
chain ka rukni wafad Gwadar  ke doray par
chain ke soobay سنکیانگ ka aik rukni wafad communist party ke secretary general zang چوانگ ki sarbarahi mein paiir ke roz soobah Balochistan  ke sahili shehar Gwadar  ke doray par pahonch gaya .
governor Balochistan  Mohammad  Khan  achakzai wifaqi secretary port and shipping Khalid  Parvez  sobai secretary dakhla akbar Hussain  Durani  samait deegar wifaqi o sobai hakkaam ne un ka istaqbaal kya .
aik sarkari aalamia ke mutabiq cheeni wafad ke sarbarah ne Gwadar  port area mein free zone ka iftitah karte hue kaha ke Gwadar  mein sarmaya kaari ke wasee mwaqae mojood hain .
un ka kehna tha ke chain Gwadar  mein sarmaya kaari samait mukhtalif shobo mein dilchaspi rakhti hai .
darin Isna  awaami jamhooria chain ke wafad ne behtareen taleem aur sehat aama se mutaliq aik taqreeb mein shirkat kar te hue kaha ke chain Gwadar  ki taraqqi aur khushhali ke liye bhar پوراقدامات kar rahi hai .
un ka kehna tha ke Gwadar  aur کرامے city ke darmiyan jurwan shehar qarar diye jane ke tehat social sector mein bhi muawnat faraham kere gi .
is ke ilawa chain Gwadar  ke primaray ke tlba o talbat ko aala taleem faraham karne ke liye har saal chain bheja jaye ga .
is mauqa par chairman Gwadar  port authority دوستین Khan  jmaldini ne kaha ke Gwadar  bandargaah ki takmeel ke baad aalmi karobari o tijarti hawalay se golden gate way saabit hoga jahan bain al aqwami tijarti sar garmion ko farogh miley ga .

ki is fehrist mein hindostan sab se ziyada asleha daraamad karne walay malik ke tor par samnay aaya tha. report mein kaha gaya hai ke Pakistan  ne mein million dollars ka asleha daraamad kya jabkay hindostan ka yeh hajam hazaar million dollars raha .

mila Yaqoob  aur mila abdalmnan rahbari shoora mein shaamil
khabar rasan idaray روئٹرز ne Afghan  taliban ke tarjuman ke hawalay se bataya hai ke mila Umar  ke barray betay mila Mohammad  Yaqoob  aur bhai mila abdalmnan ko faisla saazi ki ahem committee rahbari shoora mein shaamil kar liya gaya hai. qaari Yousuf  Ahmedi  ke mutabiq Yaqoob  ko taliban ke military commission ka sarbarah bhi bana diya gaya hai .
naqideen ke mutabiq mila Umar  ke do intehai qareebi sathiyon ko is baaghi tehreek mein ahem maqamat dainay ka maqsad taliban ke mojooda rehnuma mila Akhtar  mansoor ki position ko mustahkam karna hai kyunkay taliban ke mukhtalif dharon mein qayadat ke muamlay par ikhtilafat ab bhi mojood hain .
mila Umar  ki halakat ki khabar aam honay ke baad mila Akhtar  mansoor ko Afghan  taliban ka sarbarah muqarrar kar diya gaya tha jis ke baad mila Umar  ke ghar walon ke ilawa kayi deegar dharon ne bhi is par aitrazaat kiye thay .
kaha jata hai ke mila Mohammad  Yaqoob  taliban jungjuon mein aik intehai mooatbar naam hai. bataya gaya hai ke Yaqoob  ko taliban baaghi tehreek ke military commission ka sarbarah bana diya gaya hai aur ab woh Afghanistan  ke pandrah sobon mein jangju karwaiyon ki sarparasti kere ga .
Ahmedi  ke mutabiq mila Yaqoob  aur abdalmnan ne apni nai zimma darion ko nah sirf qubool kar liya hai balkay paiir se unhon ne –apne ohday sambhaal bhi liye hain .
taliban ke aik ahem rehnuma ne apna naam zahir nah karne ki shart par bataya hai ke mila mansoor ne aik taweel arsay se Yaqoob  aur abdalmnan ko shoora mein ahem maqam dainay ki dawat day rakhi thi. taham un ki baqaida tor par taqarruri paiir ke din amal mein aayi hai. is rehnuma ke bakol is pishrft se taliban mein ittehaad peda karne mein madad miley gi .
mila Umar  ki mout ki khabar aam honay ke baad is ke gharane ne qayadat sambhalay mein dlchpsi zahir ki thi. pehlay unhon ne –apne naye sarbarah ke tor par mila Yaqoob  ki himayat ki thi lekin baad azan unhon ne –apne mutalibaat manwane ke baad mila Umar  ke puranay aur qareebi saathi mila mansoor ko apna rehnuma qubool kar liya tha .
Afghan  taliban ke kuch dharon ka yeh ilzaam bhi hai ke mila mansoor Pakistan  ki kath patli hai. yeh dharay ab bhi taliban ki markazi rahbari shoora ki mukhalfat karte hain. guzashta baras aisi khabrain aam hui theen ke taliban ke mutharab dharon mein jharpon ke nateejay mein mila mansoor shadeed zakhmi ho gaya tha taham taliban ne un khabron ko mustard kar diya tha. is maqsad ke liye taliban ne mila mansoor ki aik audio rerecording bhi jari ki thi taakay logon ko ilm ho sakay ke woh bkhrit hai .
Sarfraz  Ahmed  T20 team ke captain muqarrar
sala Sarfraz  Ahmed  ne world T20 ke charon matchon mein Pakistan  ki numaindagi ki lekin T20 matchon mein ke behtar strike rate aur behtareen form ke bawajood inhen charon matchon mein batting ke liye nichale nambaron par bheja gaya .
Sarfraz  ne Pakistan  ki pehli domestic T20 league Pakistan  super league mein queta گلیڈی ایٹرز ki shandaar andaaz mein qayadat karte hue usay final tak rasai dilae lekin final mein Islamabad united ke khilaaf inhen nakami ka mun dekhna para. wazeh rahay ke roz qabal Shahid  afridi ne Pakistan  ki T20 cricket team ki captani chorney ka elaan kya tha .
Shahid  afridi ne is elaan ke liye samaji raabtey ki Website twitter ka sahara liya jahan aik press release mein un ka kehna tha ke woh bator khilari qaumi team aur league cricket ke liye dastyab rahen ge. guzashta roz dawn news se khusoosi guftagu mein chairman Shehryar  Khan  ka kehna tha ke Shahid  afridi ki janib se shikast ki zimma daari khud qubool karna aur qayadat se dastbardaar hona barray pann ki baat hai. unhon ne kaha yeh baat khush aaind hai ke Shahid  afridi T20 team ke liye dastyab hon ge lekin inhen team mein shaamil karne ka faisla selection committee kere gi .
chairman PCB ka kehna tha ke Shahid  afridi ke dastbardaar honay ke baad naib captain Sarfraz  Ahmed  T20 captain ke liye sab se mazboot umeed waar hain taham woh PCB hakkaam se mahswara kar ke jald captain ka hatmi elaan karen ge. wazeh rahay ke haliya world tea aur is se qabal asia cupp mein Pakistan  team ki nakami ke baad Shahid  afridi ko nah sirf shaiqeen ki janib se tanqeed ka saamna karna para balkay qaumi team ke coach aur manager ne bhi apni reports mein afridi ki qaidana salahiyaton par sawalaat uthaye thay .
guzashta roz Pakistan  cricket team ke head coach Waqar  Younis  ne PCB ki janib se tajaweez par amal-dar-aamad nah honay par –apne ohday se istifa day diya tha. Waqar  Younis  ke isteefay ke fori baad cricket board ne selection committee ko tahleel karte hue team ke qaleel aur taweel mudti faislon ka elaan kya tha .
mashriqi Afghanistan  mein khudkush hamla chay shehri halaak
mashriqi Afghanistan  mein aik motocycle sawaar khudkush bambaar ne aik school aur dwakhane ke qareeb khud ko dhamakay se ura diya. is waqeye mein kam az kam chay aam shehri halaak jab ke deegar zakhmi ho gaye hain. mangal ke roz yeh waqea dar-al-hakoomat kabul ke shumal maghrib mein waqay parwan soobay mein paish aaya. bataya gaya hai ke is khudkush hamla aawar ka mumkina hadaf aik police chocky thi taham jab usay maloom sun-hwa ke is ka taqub kya ja raha hai to is ne school ke qareeb hi khud ko ura diya. bataya gaya hai ke is waqeye mein aik police ahelkaar zakhmi bhi sun-hwa. muqami hakoomati tarjuman ne bataya ke zakhmion mein se baaz ki haalat naazuk hai is liye halakaton mein izafay ka khadsha mojood hai .
sukh zaireen ko halaak karne ka ilzaam Bharti  police ehalkaron ko Umar  qaid
sun mein sukh zaireen ke aik group ko halaak karne ke ilzaam mein Bharat  ki aik khusoosi adalat ne police ehalkaron ko Umar  qaid ki saza suna di hai. un police ehalkaron ne is waqt yeh daawa kya tha ke yeh tamam sukh askriat pasand thay. Bharti  khabar rasan idaray press trust of India  ke mutabiq utar pardesh riyasat mein paish anay walay is waqeye mein un police afsaron ka asal maqsad sukhnon ko halaak kar ke taraqqi haasil karna tha. bataya gaya hai ke is waqt sukh alehadgi pasand tehreek –apne urooj par thi aur isi tehreek ko bahana bana kar police ahkaron ne sukh zaireen ko qatal kya. paiir ke roz wakeel istighasa ne adalti faislay ke hawalay ke baad bataya ke un police afsaraan ne aik bas ko rokkk kar is mein mojood sukh zaireen ko aik qareebi jung mein le ja kar golion ka nishana banaya tha .
Khalda  zia ki zamanat ki darkhwast Manzoor
Bangladesh ki aik adalat ne oppostion rehnuma Khalda  zia ki zamanat ki darkhwast Manzoor  kar li hai. aik adalat ne hukoomat mukhalif tehreek ke douran par tashadud waqeat ko sun-hwa dainay ke ilzaam mein Khalda  zia ki giraftari ke warrant jari kiye thay. mangal ke roz sala Khalda  zia zamanat ki darkhwast Manzoor  honay ke baad adalat se nikleen to un ki jamaat Bangladesh نیشنسلٹ party ke qareeb paanch hazaar haami wahan mojood thay. is mauqa par muzahireen ki janib se hukoomat mukhalif naaray baazi bhi ki gayi. un ki jamaat Bangladesh nishnlst party ne hukoomat ko mutnabba kya tha ke agar Khalda  zia ko girftar kya gaya to poooray malik mein muzahirey shuru kar diye jayen ge .
panama papers mutadid mumalik mein tafteesh shuru

Shami  media ne taham yeh nahi bataya ke is waqeye mein kitni halakatain huien. is hawai adday ke qareebi ilaqon par shiddat pasandon ka qabza hai taham ab tak hakoomati forces is fouji adday par apna control qaim rakhay hue hain. hakoomati media ke mutabiq dehshat gardon ki janib se mstrd gas ke haamil rocket داغے gaye. fi al haal azad zaraye se un hakoomati dawoon ki tasdeeq nahi ho saki .

muhajreen se mutaliq deal tarkin watan ki yunan se turkey muntaqili ka silsila jari
Europi  union aur turkey ke darmiyan tay panay walay muahiday ke tehat turkey se yunan pounchanay walay ghairqanooni tarkin watan ki dobarah turkey muntaqili ka silsila jari hai. paiir ke roz do so se zayed afraad ko yonani jazair se dobarah turkey muntaqil kya gaya. bataya gaya hai ke yunan badar kiye gaye un afraad mein se ziyada tar Pakistani  shehri thay. hakkaam ke mutabiq yonani jazair par hirasati marakaz mein mojood tarkin watan ko behri jahazoo par sawaar kar ke turkey bheja ja raha hai. hakkaam ke mutabiq guzashta roz turkey beje gaye afraad mein se Pakistani  Afghan  irani chaar Srilankan aur teen Bangladeshi shehri thi. is ke ilawa chand africi mumalik se talluq rakhnay walay afraad ko bhi wapas turkey bheja gaya hai. isi deal ke tehat turkey mein mojood Shami  muhajreen ko qanooni tor par Europi  mumalik mein basanay ka silsila bhi shuru ho gaya hai. guzashta roz Shami  muhajreen ko aik tayyaray ke zariye shumali german shehar ہینوور laya gaya .

Israel  ne bahera Ahmar  ke kinare waqay aik sayahati maqam par hotlon mein kaam karne ke liye paanch so ardni bashindon ko mulaazmaten dainay ki manzoori day di hai. ایلات Nami  is maqam par ardni bashindon ko mulaazmaten dainay ki wajah malik mein mazdooron ki kami batayi gayi hai. machar ya keeron ke katnay se honay wali jalan se nijaat
agar machar ya kisi keeray ke katnay se jalan aur kharish ho rahi hai to daar cheeni ke aik tukre ko aik chamach shehad mein mix kar ke aik paste tayyar kar len aur phir usay mutasirah jagah par lgalin .
daar cheeni keel mahason ke nishanaat taizi se khatam karti hai aur bacteria khatam karne un ke ubharnay ki rokkk thaam bhi karti hai. aik chaye ke chamach daar cheeni ko aik chaye ke chamach jaiphal aur aik chamach shehad mein mix karen. is mixture ko mutasirah jagah par lagayen aur bees minute ke baad name garam pani se dho len .
daar cheeni ke andar mojood ajza kaandhon aur gardan ki takleef mein kami laane mein madad dete hain. aik jurab ka teen chothai hissa safaid chaawlon do daar cheeni ke tukron aur aik chamach loving se بھرلیں. usay مائیکرو view mein do minute tak garam karen aur phir apni gardan ke gird پھیلادیں. aap jurab ko garam karne aur gardan par rakhnay ka amal is waqt tak jari rakhen jab tak msalhon ki mehak khatam nah ho jaye .
daar cheeni dafaa reah masalha hai yani is ki keemiyai khoobiyan pait mein gas aur aphaar ko kam karti hai. usay apni ghiza ke zariye istemaal karen ya khanay ke baad is ka tukda choosnay se nizaam haazma behtar hota hai .
daar cheeni ka tukda kisi ساشے mein daal kar kitcehn kibnt mein rakh den taakay chyontyan wahan nah jayen ya is ka sufoof chyontyon ke dakhli maqamat par chidak den. kitcehn ke shelf mein daar cheeni ko chore dena jagah ko khushbodar banata hai jabkay keeron ko daur rakhta hai .
کبی kabhar khana kharab honay se poooray ghar mein bo phail jati hai aur agar aisa ho jaye to pareshan honay ki bajaye daar cheeni ke sufoof ko kisi bartan mein daal kar aik ghantay tak cholhe par bhonay masla hal ho jaye ga .
agar to aap ko saans ki bo ki shikayat hai jo bacteria ki wajah se hoti hai to daar cheeni is ke ilaaj ke liye mufeed hai. saans mein bo peda ho rahi ho to aik tukre daar cheeni ko چوسیں jis se is maslay ka jarr se khtama hojaye ga
Shah  rukh aur rnoyr film mein aik sath

Shah  rukh hadaayat car شیمت ke sath is se qabal ki film chak day mein kaam kar chuke hain jo saal ki kamyaab film saabit hui thi .

wazeh rahay ke yeh ranking ke baad se har saal jari ki jati hai
rawan saal behtareen passport ki fehrist mein Germany  pehlay number par hai jis ke passport par musafir mein se mumalik aur khitton mein baghair visay ke safar kar satke hain
soyidn dosray number hai jis ke passport par mulkon ka safar kya ja sakta hai
fun land France  italy spain aur yoke ka number teesra hai
jabkay America  jo aur mein sar-e fehrist tha rawan baras chouthay number par hai Belguim  Denmark  aur Netherlands  bhi America  ke sath chothi position par mojood hain
aur ki fehrist mein taap three mein shumaar kiye jane walay Japan  aur janoobi Korea  ab rawan saal bal tarteeb panchwin aur chhatay number par aagaye hain
bad tareen passport ki fehrist mein Afghanistan  sab se aakhri yani number par mojood hain is se oopar Pakistan  Iraq  somalia aur shaam mojood hain
ہینلے and partnrz ke mutabiq visa ki sharait kisi bhi malik ke dosray mumalik se taluqaat ki akkaasi karti hain
company ke aik numainday ne si an an se baat karte hue bataya ke kisi bhi malik ke shehrion ko visa free rasai is malik ke sath safarti taluqaat security khatraat aur visa sharait ki khilaaf wazion par munhasir hoti hai .
