f am products ke tehat banai gayi is film ki kahani Afghan  jung se mutasirah logon ke gird ghhoomti hai. film mein mohabbat ka aik masalas bhi dkhayagya hai جوترکی ke shehar istanbul mein muqeem aik nojawan morad istanbul ki aik Pakistani  dr mahi aur Afghan  muhajreen camp mein kaam karne wali aik hindustani dr jiya ke darmiyan hai .
mahi morad se be intahaa pyar karti hai jabkay morad kadl pehli nazar mein honay wali mohabbat jiya ke liye hi dhadakataa hai jis ke liye woh mahi ka rishta bhi ٹھکرادیتا hai. ittafaq se jab morad apni maa ki an jee o ke kaam ke silsilay mein Pakistan  mein qaim Afghan  مہاجرکیمپ pohanchana to wahan is ki talaash khatam ho jati hai aur is ki mulaqaat jiya se ho jati hai jo hindostan se Afghan  muhajreen ki raza karana madad ke liye Pakistan  aayi hui hai .
yahan morad jiya ko apni taraf mael karne ki koshish karta hai to usay maloom hota hai ke jiya abhi tak –apne mangetar se pyar karti hai jo kuch arsa qabal aik haadsay mein intqaal kar chuka hai aur is hi ke mission ko zindah rakhnay ke liye جیانے apni zindagi Afghan  muhajreen ki madad ke liye waqf kar rakhi hai .
jiya –apne sasur dr sameer aur dost sarah ke ehsas dilanay ke baad aakhir morad ke pyar ko qubool kar layte hai .
kahani agay barhti hai aur morad jiya se wapas anay ka ke kar turkey chala aata hai aur jab woh –apne walidain ko is rishte ke liye mananay ke baad wapas Pakistan  aata hai to halaat kuch is terhan tabdeel ho chuke hotay hain ke woh jiya se dobarah nahi mil paata hai .
film ki markazi cast no warid hai jinhen adakari ke shobay mein maqam bananay ke liye mazeed mehnat karne ki zaroorat hai. film ke deegar اداکارں mein Nadim  bag ayub khoso Zaib  chohadry jamal Shah  azraa aftaab aur mah jabeen shaamil hain jabkay film star Sana  fakhr bhi aik item number mein khusoosi tor par mojood hain .

salam alaikum ورحمہ Allah  wabarakatuho graami nama morkh_h decemeber mujhe kal mila. shaam hi ko sharn poor rawana ho gaya. aaj dosray roz sharn poor hi se yeh areeza Arsaal khidmat kar raha hon .
inayat naame ne be payaan musarrat bakhsh. aap ne jis baradarana mohabbat o talluq ka izhaar farmaya hai woh mere liye barri doulat hai. aap yaqeen farmaen hum log aap se jis terhan miley is mein bilkul tasnaa nah tha qalbi taqaza tha aur tabiyat ki kashish is ke bohat se wajoh ho satke hain. mujhe خوداندازہ nah tha ke aap se itna qurb o munasbat hai. dil ra badal راہیست. mere khayaal mein aksar doston ka yahi haal tha. sab aap se itni mohabbat o ehtram se miley ke arsay se is ka tajurbah nahi sun-hwa tha .
mujhe is ka qlq aur nedamat hai ke mein station par rukhsat karne ke liye haazir nah sun-hwa. is roz khaas tor par meri tabiyat muzamahil thi aur mujhe darul uloom hi rehna tha. dosray roz is ka qlq sun-hwa. Allah  aap ko baar baar laaye aur yeh mawaqay baar baar haasil hon .
Allah  taala darul uloom ki aur is ke zariye deen ki khidmat ki tofeq ataa farmaiye. yeh zamane ka inhitat aur qeht alrjal hai ke hum jaisay ناتوانوں par is ki khidmat ki zimma daari aagai hai. is ki taraqqi ke baray mein bohat se hauslay aur dil ke armaan hain. Allah  taala mehez –apne fazl se un ki takmeel farmaiye. aap ne apni mohabbat se jo tajarbay ki baat likhi hai woh barri qeemti hai. mein to –apne رفقاے car ka taawun chahta hon aur is lehaaz se bara khush qismat hon ke aghraaz ke is daur mein is doulat se mahroom nahi hon. agar dar-ul-alom ke paas koi qeemti sarmaya hai to yahi ke is ke usaatzaa aik khandan aur knbe ki terhan rehtay hain. kkhuda is khasusiyat ko baqi rakhay .
aap ke besh qeemat mazameen ka zaroor intzaar o Ishtiaq  rahay ga .
umeed hai ke aap عبقریت Ali ke tarjumay ko nah bhoolay hon ge. yeh kaam bhi zaroor ho jana chahiye aur is ke liye aap ka qalam bhmdallh mozoon hai ke aqeedat o mohabbat se bhi behra mand hai .
mein decemeber ko لکھنؤ se رنگون ke liye rawana ho raha hon. yeh safar darul uloom hi ke liye hai. wast January  tak un sha Allah  wapsi ho gi. is arsay mein agar yaad farmaen to pata hasbey zail ho ga

aik sawal par un ka kehna tha ke woh England  mein pehli martaba test match khailnay ke liye pareshan nahi hain balkay team ki kamyabi ke liye apna kirdaar ada karne ke liye pur josh hain .

un ka mazeed kehna tha ke Abbotabad mein munaqidah camp ke baad khiladion ki fitness behtar hui jo England  mein behtar karkardagi ke liye mufeed hogi .

unhon ne one day matchon mein ki ost se aik hazaar runs banaye hain .

sarkari takhminay ke mutabiq malik bhar mein qaim honay wali nai universition azlaa ki satah par un ke کیمپسز aur sab کیمپسز aur mojooda idaron ke liye aindah no saal mein taqreeban das hazaar pi each d afraad darkaar hon ge taham doctriat ki degree ke liye yeh bhi zaroori qarar diya gaya hai ke yeh kisi mayaari idaray se haasil ki jaye. chunkay duniya bhrki universition ke darmiyan ki jane wali darja bandi mein America  ki drsgahin sab se بہترہیں is liye wifaqi hukoomat ki koshish hai ke Pakistan  se aala taleem ke liye beron mumalik bhijvaaye jane walay afraad aala tareen degree bhi unhi behtareen Amrici  idaron se haasil karen. vision ke khaaliq champion minister ne tamam sobon aur دیگرفریقین ki mushawarat se tayyar ki jane wali is dastaweez mein jo saat ahdaaf muqarrar kiye hain un mein awleen tarjeeh insani taraqqi ko hi di hai aur yeh bhi aitraaf kiya hai ke is arsay tak agar Pakistan  ko upper middle income kamanay walay mumalik ki saf mein shaamil karna hai to is ke liye zaroori hai ke taleem ke shobay mein sarmaya kaari ko badhaya jaye aur khusoosan aala taleem mein aisay afraad peda kiye jayen jo جددید daur ke taqazoon ke mutabiq knowledge akanomi mein bharpoor kirdaar ada kar saken .
vision ki dastaweez ke mutabiq guzashta aik ashray mein Pakistan  ki fi kis aamdani sirf teen feesad ki sharah se barhi jabkay Bangladesh Bharat  chain janoobi Korea  aur Srilanka jaisay mumalik mein fi kis aamdani ki sharah mein chay se no feesad izafah sun-hwa. yeh bhi bawar karaya gaya ke agar Pakistan  ne isi dagar par apna safar jari rakha to aindah tees saal mein Pakistan  ki fi kis aamdani Indonesia  ke masawi tees hazaar dollars tak puhanche gi to tab roos ki pandrah hazaar Portugal  ki ikees ہزاراور spain ki tees hazaar dollars tak pahonch chuki ho gi. sorat e haal ko –apne haq mein karne ke liye wifaqi hukoomat ne mansoobah bandi ki hai ke taleem ke shobay ke liye mukhtas kiye jane walay wasail ko qaumi aamdani ke chaar feesad tak badhaya jaye ga jabkay aala taleem ki satah par انرولمنٹ ki sharah ko batadreej saat feesad se barha kar baara feesad tak laya jaye ga. Pakistan  ki samaji اوراقتصادی taraqqi ko yakeeni bananay ke liye bulaa shuba knowledge karidor bhi aik game changer hi hai lekin yahan kuch haqayiq ka idraak karna bhi zaroori hai taakay is mansoobay ko kamyabi se humkenar karne ki raah mein haail rakawaten daur ki ja saken .
sab se ahem pehlu yeh hai ke das hazaar pi each d afraad peed akrne ke liye zaroori hai ke aala taleem ki satah par dakhlay ki sharah bhi isi tanasub se barhai jaye. mojooda sharah jo baa-mushkil saat feesad hai is mein itni barri tadaad mein afradko doctriat ki degree dalwana taqreeban na mumkin hai. Bharat  mein yeh sharah feesad aur malaysia mein feesad tak hai. khud sochen jab bunyaad hi mazboot nahi ho gi to is par aliiiii shaan imarat kaisay taamer ki ja sakti hai. jis malik mein arhhayi crore bachay school ke naam se na aashna hon primaray satah par dakhlay ki sharah feesad ho middle ki satah par yeh sharah feesad aur high school ki satah par sirf feesad ho feesad larkiyan is liye high school se taleem ko kher abad ke den kyun ke un ke walidain un ki taleem boojh uthany ki sakt nahi rakhtay .
secondary satah prsrf dakhla lainay wali khush naseeb larkiyon ki sharah sirf feesad ho jis malik ke primaray schoolon mein se aik tahai mein sirf aik ustaad ho aur jis mein sirf aik soobay mein ghoost school hazaron ki tadaad mein hon jahan feesad schoolon mein chaar deewari se baath room tak bunyadi sahuliyaat bhi muyassar nah hon jis malik ke grijwayshn karne walay bhi feesad aisay hon jo aalmi miyaar ke mutabiq mulazmat ke ahal nah hon jis ki majmoi sharah khawandgi apna naam likhnay aur parhnay ki ahliat rakhnay walon ko shumaar kar ke bhi feesad ho aur jo aqwam mutahidda ki taraf se sonpe gaye میلینئیم development گولز ko bhi haasil karne mein nakaam ho jaye wahan knowledge karidor ke tehat hazaar afraad ko pi each d karana din mein khawab dekhnay ke mutradif hi hai. waisay Pakistan  mein to baaz aisay pi each d afraad bhi paye jatay hain jin ke baray mein dr Hood  bhai ne kaha ke inhen koi reserch paper parhna par jaye to woh mazhaka khaiz had tak ghalat hota hai lekin naam Nihaad  aalmi journals mein tehqiqati maqalay shaya karanay walay aisay afraad nah sirf khud ko dr balkay professor ڈاکٹرکہلاتے hain. yahan wifaqi hukoomat se guzarish hai ke chain Pakistan  economic karidor ki terhan pak you s knowledge karidor ko bhi atharvin tarmeem ki aarr mein sirf wifaq aur Punjab  tak mehdood nah rakhay balkay is se istifada karne ke liye malik bhar ke tlbav talbat ko bulaa imtiaz yaksaa mawaqay faraham kiye jayen .
knowledge karidor ki tamam tar juzziyat ko hatmi shakal day kar is ki munasib tashheer ki jaye taakay matlooba ahliat ke afraad is se bharpoor faida utha saken. pi each d programme ke liye afraad ke intikhab ka tareeqa car waza karte waqt pasmandah ilaqon ke kota ko bhi malhooz khatir rakha jaye. umeedwaron ke intikhab ke liye jo bhi committee ya board tashkeel diya jaye is mein tamam sobon aur fata samait deegar tamam akayyon ko numaindagi di jaye. tamam sobon ki mushawarat ke sath primaray se post grijwayshn ki satah tak taleem ke farogh ke liye inqalabi iqdamaat uthaye jayen taakay barri tadaad mein aisay qabil afraad mil saken jo doctriat ki degree haasil kar ke malik ki taraqqi aur khushhali mein apna kirdaar ada kar saken. aakhir mein dua گوہوں ke chain Pakistan  economic karidor ki terhan pak you s knowledge karidor bhi kamyabi se humkenar ho .

dr tabassum kashmiri aik naqaad muhaqiq adbi morak aur ustaad ki hesiyat se jane jatay hain. un ki takhleeqi aur Ilmi  zindagi ka yeh safar kam o besh athawan baras par muheet hai. woh saath ki dahai mein shuru honay wali jadeed urdu shairi ki tehreek ke ibtidayi shura mein se hain. unhon ne bah tor shayar apni adbi zindagi ka aaghaz ke awail mein kar diya tha lekin un ka pehla sheri majmoa Tamsaal  mein manzar aam par aaya. un ka dosra sheri majmoa nohay takhat لہور ke mein shaya sun-hwa. sfrِ Japan  un ki zindagi minayak naye mourr ki hesiyat rakhta hai. unhon ne japani tahazeeb ki jamaliat ko –apne baseerat Afroz  mushahiday ke zariye mukhtalif sheri sanchon mein dhala hai aur unhon ne sheri ufaq par kaasni barish mein dhoop baz گشتوں ke pal par aur surkh khizaa mein phool jaisay vqia majmoay paish kiye hain. jadeed urdu nazam sunah saath ki dahai mein jis hsasit aur jiddat ko le aayi baad ki tamam sheri riwayat is se allag nahi hai. dr tabassum kashmiri ki شعریات mein sunah saath ke tamam tajarbaat aur mozuaat mlitay hain. un ki nazmein mehsosaat aur jamaliat ke mtnoa manazair se hum aahang hain. woh apni شعریات mein kaayenaat ki mojoodaat ko fikar vaml ki kasoti par parkhte hain. un ka lehja umooman dheema aur Roman  ke jazbay se bharpoor hai. un ki شعریات zaat ke karb zindagi ki uljhano fard ke ehsas zeist aur is ke masail par mushtamil hain. un ki soch ka zavia bohat mukhtalif hai jis mein hum dardi reham insaaniyat se mohabbat avrghir insani ashya se ans ka jazba mojzan nazar aatahe. un ki شعریات mein zindagi aur fard ke karb ko Anees  nage Tamsaal  ke paish lafz میںاس terhan bayan karte hain

Tamsaal  ki nazmein hon ya kisi aur majmoay ki nazmein tabassum kashmiri kisi bhi fard ki afsurdagi ko apni zaat se jor letay hain is ke ranj o alum ko apna gham bnalite hain un ka yeh rawayya insaan dosti ki alamat hai. zaat aur fard ke aitbaar se to yeh soorat e haal thi afraad aur muashray ki satah par is ehad ki kya soorat thi usay dekhe aur jacchay baghair is ehad ki manzar kashi mumkin nahi hai. yeh ehad darasal insaan ke wujood ki talaash ka عہدتھا jis میںمعاشرہ toot phoot ka shikaar ho chuka tha. is ke wujood ki ikai aur shanakht khatam ho rahi thi aur woh is kurrah arz par rezah rezah bikhar chuka tha. is ka yeh safar be suraagh aur be simt tha. goya is ehad ka fard hairaton aur Moheeb  junglon mein gum ho gaya tha. talaash ka yeh safar be ant masafat ke zariye tay nahi hota tha. tabassum kashmiri aur is ehad ke shura isi almie mein safar kar rahay thay. is karb naak ehad aur muashray ki manzar kashi jelani Kamraan  un alfaaz mein karte hain

sheri paiker ka istemaal mehez kamaal fun ki Daleel  nahi balkay haqeeqat ke Urfan  ka aik bohat hi lateef aur mo-asar waseela bhi hai is kaayenaat mein har shai aik dosray se mutaliq hi nahi aik dosray mein paivest bhi hai. ashya ke darmiyan talluq aur raabtey ki noiyat ya ashya aur jazbaat aur ehsasat ke darmiyan نقطۂ Itsaal  ko sheri paiker ke zariye taayun kya ja sakta hai .
dr tabassum un munfarid sheri پیکروں ko apni shairi mein is terhan bayan karte hain raat ka تیراندازی karna mein teer andazi khalis insani feal hai aur raat aik ghair mujassam shai hai aur waqt e zamaan hai is se insanon ki terhan teer andazi karana aur is ko itnay khoob soorat andaaz mein paish karna maienay Afreen  hai. phir ajraam falki aur Zamani  anasir se is terhan ke af-aal ki misalein un ki shairi mein din ka chori hona shaam ka Sooraj  ke labon par lab rakhna dhanak ki kalayi baadal ka jhonparey par dastak dena dhoop ka darwazay par zor se hansna shaam ko tawwan mein rakh lena din ke gilaay mein taveez bandh dena khawahishon ka –apne jism ko utha kar sheeshay ki khirki se jhankna jaisi misalein shaamil hain

tabassum kashmiri ki shairi mein imagery تشبیہات استعاروں aur alamaton ka munfarid tarz mojood hai. un ki شعریات ki mukhtalif tasaveer ko dekhen twan mein aik barray musawir ke khoob soorat naqsh nazar atay hain. un ki mehsosaat ki satah itni buland hai ke mamooli se mamooli khayaal bhi munfarid nazar aata hai. maslan jheel ka –apne button khol kar baadal ki taraf pyar se dekhna bohat hi khoob soorat jumla hai isi terhan darakhton mein chupay tarre ka apni lambi lambi unglio se ’alvidah’ kehna haal آنکہ tarre ki kon si ungelian hoti hain lekin shayar ne unglio ke sath lambi lambi ka izafah kar ke is ke husn aur manoyt mein mazeed izafah kar diya hai kyunkay lambi ungelian khoob soorti ki alamat hoti hain. tarre ki ungelian ho na to is se yeh gumaan bhi peda hota hai ke tarre ke haath bhi hon ge aur is nisbat se tamam jismani aaza bhi. tabassum kashmiri ki mehsosaat mein is qader fikar angazi aur tadabbur payajata hai ke woh bohat mamooli baat ko is qader achay aur par dard andaaz mein paish karte hain ke qaari bhi is soorat e haal se mutasir hue baghair nahi reh sakta hai. samandar ka rotay rotay be ikhtiyar hichikiyaan bharnay lagna aur shehar ke naram balon zard galoon se pyar karna sookhte pamaal jismon par wafa ke hont rakhna zakham khorda meharban boorhi faseelon se mohabbat karna sard makanon ka haanpna karaahna aur un ki mutwaram cheekhain. yeh sab aisay کلامیے jin mein tabassum kashmiri ne shehar ko aik intehai lagar aur maghmoom ke tor par paish kya hai ke jis se shehar ke mutaliq ehsas hamdardi mein izafah hota hai. maslan naram baal zard gaal se pyar karna bohat ma-ani afreen hai jaisay koi bachay se ya kisi –apne pyare ke bemaar honay ki soorat mein is se pyar sirf aur sirf is ki dil joi aur بڑھاوے ke liye karta hai. un ki شعریات mein se darj zail misalein paish karte hain
hum ne shulon ki paneeri boi thi
shehar ki dewaron ke liye un ke jumlay qabil ghhor hain jin ke parhnay se ehsas hamdardi peda ho jata hai. meharban boorhi fasilain jo ke zakham khorda bhi ہیںان jumlon ko ehad maazi ke tanazur mein dekhen to yeh fasilain jo Lahore  shehar aur is ke ba شندوں ki hifazat par mamoor theen ab waqt guzarnay ke sath sath woh purani khasta haal aur boseedah ho chuki hain. tabassum kashmiri ne un dewaron ke liye boseedah khasta haal ke alfaaz istemaal karna munasib nahi samjha hai. unhon ne un dewaron se mohabbat aur kher khawahi ke tor par zakham khorda ki tarkeeb paish kar ke is ki manoyt mein be baha izafah kar diya hai. un dewaron ne har daur mein hamari hifazat ke liye –apne jismon par zakham khaye hain. yeh meharban is liye hain ke jaisay maa ki shafqat aur mohabbat –apne bachon ko bachanay ke liye hama waqt msrofِ amal rehti hai tabassum kashmiri ne maa ki mamta ke isi tasawwur ko paish kya hai. isi nazam ke aakhri hissay mein woh puranay makanon ke liye ہانپنے karahnay aur mutwaram cheekhain nikaalte ke alfaaz istemaal kar ke unhein khalis insani af-aal injaam dete hue dikhata hain. mohabbat ka jazba aur ahsasِ hamdardi ke sath yeh jumlay inhiraf ki bhi achi misalein hain. taymr aik be jaan shai hai yeh aik aala hai jo میکینکلی –apne kaam injaam deta hai. tabassum kashmiri ne taymr ke liye be charah taymr khidmat gaar taymr ki trakib laga kar yeh ehsas dilatey hain ke ghair insani ashya ke liye bhi un ki mehsosaat kitni mohabbat amaiz hain. dosray lafzon mein un ke dil mein yeh ehsas baqi hai ke yeh saari cheeze kis terhan hamari khidmat mein lagi rehti hain. be charah taymr aur khidmat gaar ٹائمربہت umdah kalme hain jin mein fikri geherai aur nai manoyt payi jati hai. yeh tamam pehlu un ki shairi ke lasani aur اسلوبیاتی tanawu ko bayan karte hain .
tabassum kashmiri aik suljhay hue shayar hain woh apni شعریات mein jahan sooti nahwi o رمعنیاتی jdton ko istemaal mein laatay hain woh apni naazon mein doosri zabanon ke alfaaz ke istemaal se bharpoor istifada bhi karte hain. woh zabaan ke is jadeed tasawwur se waaqif hain. un ki shairi mein ke namoonay bhi mlitay hain lekin un ki khoobi yeh hai ke woh doosri zabaan mein achanak daakhil hotay hue bhi itnay ajnabi mehsoos nahi hotay hain. woh apni nazam میپلز پشکلاوتی موئن jo dero mein muqami zabaan yani punjabi o رغیر mulki zabaan sansikrat balkay qadeem zabaan ke zariye ablaagh ki koshish karte hain .
un ka yeh tarz is liye bhi munfarid hai ke woh budh se is daur ke mutabiq paanch hazaar saal purani zabaan mein guftagu kerwatay hain. jo un ki Lisan  par mahaarat aur moqay ki munasbat se is ehad ki baat ko isi ehad ki zabaan mein bayan karna aik mustahsan amal bhi hai. tabassum kashmiri Tafheem  ki mushkilaat o رقاری ki mushkil ko hal bhi kar dete hain. woh Qosain  mein is zabaan ka tarjuma bhi paish kar dete hain jo aam qaari aur zabaan se Adam  waqfiyat rakhnay walay naqaad ke liye bhi bohat mufeed saabit hota hai. un ka yeh tarz zabaan ki jiddat aur is ki معنیاتی wusat ka sabab bantaa hai. tabassum kashmiri ki شعریات ke fikri aur لسانیاتی tajziye mein yeh baat wazeh hoti hai ke un ki fikar jiddat pasand hai. woh aalmi masail ka nah sirf idraak rakhtay hain balkay apni شعریات mein un masail ko bhar poor andaaz mein bayan karne mein kamyaab bhi hue hain. unhon ne yeh sheri safar zaat se shuru kar ke usay afraad aur muashray par muntabiq karte hue aalam geer hesiyat di hai. woh hassas hamdard aur insanon se mohabbat ke ilm bardaar hain. woh zaat ke karb ko zindagi ke karb mein dhaal kar usay apni zaat ka hissa bana letay hain. un ki naazon ke sotyati لفظیاتی نحویاتی معنیاتی aur جدلیاتی badlaav ki satah par kiye gaye tajziye un ki شعریات ke لسانیاتی pehluon ko ujagar karte hain. un ki شعریات میںاصوات ka munfarid bayan lafzon ka naya pan jumlon ki دروبست ka jiddat pasand اندازاور munfarid کلامیوں mein fikar o maienay ka naya tasawwur un ke kalaam ko اسلوبیاتی satah par mazboot banatay hain. dr ibadat briloy kalaam ki aafaqiat ke baray mein is terhan azharkhyal karte hain
aik zamane mein be shumaar likhnay walay pidahote hain. un ke hathon be shumaar cheezon ki takhleeq hoti hai lekin waqt un mein se sirf chand ko baqi rakhta hai. baqi –apne hi zamane mein fanaa ho jati hain. un ke baad un ka koi naam lainay والاباقی nahi rehta jo takhleeqat baqi reh jati hain aur jin ko hamesha hamesha kisi qoum ke afraad apni tahazeeb o tamaddun ka besh baha sarmaya tasawwur karte hain un ki aafaqiat hi un ko is darjay tak pohanchati hai .
tabassum kashmiri ki nazam jo ke fard ke zaati karb aur muashray ke Asri  masail se shuru hoti hai aur aahista aahista is ka daira aalam گیرمعاشرے ke masail tak phail jata hai. Tamsaal  ki ziyada tar nazmein zaat ke karb aur fard ki be basi ka manzar paish karti hain. nohay takhat لہور ke mein woh zaat ke karb aur zaat se nikal kar ijtimaiyat ki taraf safar karte nazar atay hain jis mein zindagi ki andoh naak soorat ka ijtimai tasawwur milta hai. is majmoay ki nazmein sufi adab aur lok punjabi adab ki la zawaal dastanoon aur asateer ko paish karti hain. un ki chand nazmein jo un ke شعریات ko har lehaaz se aafaqi aur aalam geer satah par mamoor karti ہیںان mein chup ki barish karvae talkh kaseelay zaiqay zamaan taa zamaan aik safar namaloom ki taraf shehron ke liye aik nazam میپلز پشکلاوتی موئن جوڈیرو africa africa aaj miradl africa africa mein mout aur مولائسس ke khoon ki subah shaamil hain jaisa ke insani zindagi aik irtiqai soorat mein rawan dawaan hai un ka sheri safar bhi isi terhan soorat پذیرہے. shayar muashray ke liye likhta hai aur is ki zindah eqdaar ko har soorat agli nasal mein dekhna chahta hai. woh is amal mein apni poori zaat ko samo deta hai aur is mein kamyabi se shayar ko aalam geer Riffat  muyassar aati hai yahi sift tabassum kashmiri aur muashray ke darmiyan rabt o talluq ko thos bunyaad faraham karti hai .
Pakistan  waqai ashrfih ka malik hai. aik zamana tha Pakistan  mein tax ki chhuut arab ke big bhag thi. jis se teen saal mein mojooda hukoomat ne fi sad tak khatam kar diya hai. abhi bhi is ka aik thai hissa baqi hai aur baqi rahay ga kyunkay jinhon ne tax laganay aur awam se wusool karana hai un par tax kaisay lag sakta hai .
ab tax islahat commission ne taxon ke husool mein behtari ke liye apni tajaweez f bi are ko بجھوائی hain jis mein commission ne sifarish ki hai ke saddar mumlikat Wazeer e Azam  pak fouj ke jrnilon aur judges wifaqi wuzra aur Pakistan  se bahar خدمامت injaam dainay walay afsaraan ko di gayi tax mara-aat khatam ki jayen. aisa pehli baar nahi jab bhi Pakistan  mein tax islahat ki baat hoti hai aur aalmi imdadi idaray karzzzz faraham karte hain to tax islahat ko hi awleen qarar dete hain. lekin policy saaz un tajaweez ko aik kaan se suntay hain aur dosray se nikaal bhi dete hain .
saal mein Wazeer e Azam  Yousuf  Raza  gilani musheer khazana aur Maroof  banker Shaukat  tareen ne bhi –apne daur mein arab se zayed ke tax gunjaish ka baton baton mein zikar kya tha aur is par media bhi bara وایلالہ sun-hwa. . phir isi douran aik nai istilaah rifam jee s tea bhi aayi. jisay are jee s tea kaha gaya. is par seminar hue aalmi imdadi idaron ne maeeshat ko dastaweez bananay aur ashrafi se tax wusool karne ke liye is متعاراف karne ki tajaweez den. . mojooda wazeer khazana Ishaq  daar un ki team cheekh cheekh kar is ki mukhalfat qarar karte hain aur mojooda hakoomati arakeen ka Sarina  mein honay walay seminar mein tareekhi jumla are jee s tea ghareeb se mun se niwala cheennay ke mutradif hai. .
tareekh ke ourak media ki archive aur Website ka hissa hai. is mein aik barray mazay ki baat hai jo mujhe aaj bhi yaad hai. chunkay hum sahafi sab ke liye masawi tax ke haami hai is liye hum sab par tax laganay ki khabron par khaas tawajah dete hain. is rifarm jee s tea mein bataya gaya tha ke tamam cheezon par jee s tea hoga aur koi khaam maal doodh adwiyah tax se bach nahi sakay gi sath sath koi shakhs bhi tax se bach nahi saka hai. jinhein tax ki chhuut dena hogi inhen tax ree fund kar diya jaye ga taham aik fi sad tax har kisi par hrshe par lagey ga taakay maeeshat dastaweez ho sakay .
is mein khushi ki khabar yeh thi ke is waqt malik mein sales tax ki sharah fi sad thi jisay teen saal mein marhala waar aik feesad kam kar ke fi sad par lana tha. ab dekhen qoum ke sath sun-hwa kya ke fi sad tax ki chhuut jo ke awam se wabasta theen woh khatam ho gayeen aur jee s tea kam bikhat jisay fi sad par aana tha ke fi sad par hai aur diesel par to fi sad se bhi ziyada hai. is maazi ka hawala dena is liye zaroori hai ke jinhein hum policy saaz banatay hain woh maeeshat ko behtar karne ke naam par kya kya Gul  khelati hain. ab tax islahat commission ki sifarshaat tayyar hain .
muqaddas gaaye saddar mumlikat Wazeer e Azam  Muaziz  wifaqi aur sobai wazeer gornrz aala adalaton ke judges aur jrnilon ke liye tax chhuut khatam karne ki tajweez hai. jo budget ke waqt kahin faailun mein dab jaye gi aur arab se zayed ka tax haasil honay ka khawab bikhar rahay ga. tax masawi ho sab ke liye sab barabar hain shareef aur ghareeb tax mein aik hain nahi hoga. malik mein koi muqaddas gaaye nahi. hoga nahi. .
Wazeer e Azam  ke Muawin  khusoosi dr Asif  karmaney ne نکیال mein PPP aur Muslim League (N) ke kaarkunon mein tassadum ka zimma daar Azad Kashmir  ke Wazeer e Azam  chohadry abdalmjid ko qarar dete hue un ke isteefay ka mutalba kiya hai .
Islamabad mein news conference mein dr Asif  karmaney ne ka kehna hai ke na ahal aur bad unwan wazeer e azam ke kehnay پرہمارے kaarkunon ko girftar kya ja raha hai. unhon ne ilzaam lagaya ke نکیال mein peoples party youth really ke shrka ne Wazeer e Azam  Azad Kashmir  ki sheh aur Hadayat  par Muslim League (N) se talluq rakhnay walay karobari hazraat par hamla kya .
Asif  karmaney ka kehna hai ke tassadum ke waqt woh wahan mojood thay aur soorat e haal ko sheh day rahay thay Muslim League (N) ke kaarkunon ne apna difaa kya jis ke nateejay mein tassadum sun-hwa Azad Kashmir  police khamosh tamashaayi bani rahi police ne nah sirf hamla awaron ki hosla afzai ki balkay un ki sahoolat car bhi bani .
Asif  karmaney ne ilzaam lagaya ke Wazeer e Azam  aaza daal Kashmir  ke ehkamaat par ae jay ke police Azad Kashmir  mein Muslim League (N) ke kaarkunon aur votoron ke gharon mein ghis kar grftaryan kar rahi hai. is گھناؤنے jurm mein Wazeer e Azam  Azad Kashmir  kakar kirdaar hai unhon ne khauf aur ghabrahat mein bayanaat dainay shuru kar diye hain .
woh mujrim hai is ne گھناؤنے jurm ka irtikaab kya hai woh waqeye ki tehqiqaat nahi chahtay aur is waqeye ko zabardasti hamaray gilaay mein daal rahay hain chohadry abdalmjid Asif  Ali  Zardari  se musalsal jhoot bol rahay hain Zardari  sahib party ke kisi Dana  aadmi ko Azad Kashmir  bhejen aur waqeye ki tehqiqaat karayen
قلو پطرہ misar ki malka aur iskandriya ke hukmaran yonani khandan btlemoos mein se thi woh btlemoos says dhamg ke haan qabal maseeh peda hui .
is ka baap aqtdarse mahroom honay ke بعدروم ki himayat se bahaal huwa tha is ke sath misar par room ki ghulami کاسایہ parna shuru ھوگیاتھا .
badshah ahel room ka maqrooz tha is ne room ki majlis amra se wada kya tha ke is ke marnay ke baad misar par room ka qabza ho ga qabal maseeh mein is ka intqaal ho gaya is ki aulaad mein sab se barri قلوپطرہ thi jis ki Umar  is waqt saal aur doosri larki آرھینو thi is se chhota larka jo baad mein btlemoos چہاردھم aur sab se chhota larka btlemoos پانزدھم kehlaya .
Shah  msrki wasiyat ke mutabiq is ka bara larka aur barri larki mushtarqa tor par taaj وتخت ke waris qarar paye aur mil kar hukoomat karne lagey lekin qasr Shahi  do groupon mein taqseem ho gaya .
قلوپطرہ ka haami giroh kamzor nikla aur قلو پطرہ ko jalaa-watan hona para lekin thoray hi dinon baad jawaa saal قلوپطرہ shaam ke ilaqay se aik fouj le kar misar mein daakhil ho gayi .
unhi dinon room mein shenshah پومپئی aur is ke hareef جولئیس sezar mein rassa kashi shuru ho gayi پومپئی shikast ke baad panah ki talaash mein misar aaya lekin saahil par hi munharif drbaryon ke hathon qatal ho gaya .
جولئیس sezar پومپئی ke taqub mein misar pouncha aur malka قلوپطرہ ke daam husn mein girftar ho gaya
قلوپطرہ ne sezar ki madad se –apne dushmanon کاصفایا kya jin mein is ka bhai aur choti behan shaamil thay. idhar room mein sezar ka qabil aetmaad naib anthony room ke mamlaat ki nigrani karne laga .
ab sezar aur malka قلوپطرہ dono –apne dushmanon ke khauf se azad zindagi ke mazay lotney lagey. قلوپطرہ ke batan se sezar ka aik beta سیزارین peda sun-hwa. betay ki paidaiesh ke kuch arsa baad sezar ko wapas room jana para .
misar se aakar sezar ftohat mein masroof raha
jashnn ftohat ke mauqa par قلوپطرہ bhi room pahonch gayi aur room ki malka ban'nay ke khawab dekhnay lagi lekin پومپئی ke hamion ne phir sir utha liya aur sezar ko qatal kar diya .
ab قلوپطرہ ne –apne betay سیزارین ko takhat par bithanay ka khawab dekha is ne sezar ke naib anthony ko –apne daam fraib mein girftar kar liya. anthony ne usay skndrih lout jane aur munasib waqt ka intzaar karne ko kaha .
room mein آکٹوین ne ghalba pa liya to anthony bhi iskandriya agaya. is ke taluqaat bhi sezar ki terhan قلوپطرہ se agay berhay. malka haamla ho chuki thi anthony qabal maseeh mein room wapas chala gaya .
chay mah baad قلو پطرہ ke haan jurwan bachay peda hue .
anthony misar aur shaam mein nakami ke baad misar agaya. آکٹوین ne anthony ka khatrah hmish_h ke liye khatam karne ke liye misar par yalghaar kar di. anthony mara gaya aur قلوپطرہ qaid kar di gayi. woh janti thi ke agar woh zindah rahi to آکٹوین usay aur is ke bachon ko misar ki sarkon par zaleel ruswa kere ga .
قلوپطرہ ne آکٹوین se anthony ki qabar par jane ki ijazat mangi. qabar par phoolon ki chadar charhai. doli mein baith kar wapas aayi aur hamaam tayyar karne ka hukum diya .

aik zamana tha ke akhbar bektay thay tab nazriaat ke naam par jung hoti thi ab mafadaat ki jung ho ti hai. Iraq  par hamlay se pehlay New York times ki خبرقارئین ke liye saheefay ki hesiyat rakhti thi. Iraq  mein barray pemanay par tabahi phelanay walay hathyaaron ki khabar ne tabal jung baja diya. America  ne khrbon dollar is jung mein jhonk diye. wahan se atomi hathyaar to nahi niklay Albata  داعش Bar  aamad ho gayi. faida sirf sarmaya daaron ko sun-hwa jin ka farmolh hai ke har barbadi mein mawaqay chupay ho te hain .
ab New York times simat gaya is ki circulation mehdood ho gayi. magar is ke malkaan ko is se gharz nahi kyunkay unhon ne das saal mein itna maal bana liya jitna New York times aik sadi mein nah bana paata .
duniya ki terhan Pakistan  mein bhi ab media aik bara business ban chuka hai magar yahan bhi ab khalis media groupon ki jagah woh group le rahay hain jin ke deegar karobaron ko media ki chhatri darkaar hai. barray barray sarmaya car vn ne media hao سزکھول liye hain. jo is maidan mein utre un ke karobaron ne din dogni aur raat چونگنی taraqqi ki a seen ko dekhte hue kuch دیگرگروپ bhi maidan mein koodnay walay hain. un groupon mein editor naam ki post ab media manager mein tabdeel ho chuki hai .
aik barray akhbaari group ke editor ko guzashta dinon is liye nokari se nikaal diya gaya ke maalik ne aisay waqt akhbar ki lead tabdeel karne ki farmaaish ki jab akhbar aadha choup chuka tha. un media groupon mein rportron ke faraiz glandorf mansabi mein malkaan ki mukhtalif mehakmon mein ruki hui faailun ko harkat mein rakhna hota hai. unhein nokari dete waqt yeh bta diya jata hai ke kin idaron aur shaksiaat ke khilaaf khabar nahi di ja sakti. aik daur tha jab is list mein sirf hassas idaray hi atay thay magar ab yeh list itni phail chuki hai ke is mein f bi are se le kar madrasay tak sab atay hain .
aik media group jo barray tumturaq se warid ho raha tha is ki bolti is ke bolnay se pehlay hi bndkr di gayi. karporishnin safaid hathi ban kar qaumi khazanay ko chaat rahi hain magar un ki njkari is liye nahi ki jati ke lakhoon log berozgaar ho jayen ge. magar bol ka huqqa pani phir bhi band kar diya gaya aur is se wabasta kam az kam aik laakh log be روزگارہو gaye. magar chunkay sab مراثیوں hijrhon aur bhikariyon ne aika kar liya tha is liye pind ke chohdryon ke pa seen avrkoyi rasta nahi tha. bol ke baad suna hai Karachi  ke aik barray brokr ke sath bhi yahi sun-hwa. is ke baad se stak market hichkolay kha rahi hai .
بانئ Pakistan  ne kaha tha ke
pind ke chaudhry ne tamam مراثیوں ko aagah kar diya hai مراثیوں ko is baat par aitraaz nahi woh to sirf –apne daam barhana chahtay hain aur –apne najaaiz karobaron ka tahaffuz chahtay hain. mujhe is waqt barri herat hoti hai jab mere saathi azadi sahaafat ke naaray lagatay hain. azadi sahaafat naam ki cheez malkaan ne –apne mafadaat ke aiwz girwi rakh di. ab Sirf sahafion ki jaan bachi hai jo داعش jaisay garohoon ke nishanay par hai. malkaan maal bachanay ki fikar mein hain aur sahafi jaan bachanay ki. . .
المورد mein khutoot aur e mil ke zariye se deeni mozuaat par sawalaat masool hotay hain. janab Javed  Ahmed  ghamdi ke تلامذہ un salawon ke jawab dete hain. yahan un mein se muntakhib sawal o jawab ko Afadah  aam ke liye shaya kya ja raha hai .
sawal duniya mein jurm ki saza panay ke hawalay se Ameer  aur ghareeb mein aur sahib Iqtidaar  aur majboor o be kis mein farq kyun hai
jawab kkhuda ne yeh duniya aazmaysh ke liye banai hai. chunancha is ne is mein yeh gnjaysh rakhi hai ke yahan agar koi –apne daira ikhtiyar mein Adal  karna chahay to woh Adal  kar sakay aur zulm karna chahay to zulm kar sakay neki karna chahay to neki kar sakay aur badi karna chahay to badi kar sakay .
yahi wajah hai ke yahan sahib Iqtidaar  afraad aam tor par –apne متعلقین ko juraim ki saza panay se bacha letay hain lekin isi duniya mein yeh bhi dekhnay mein aata hai ke baaz sahib Iqtidaar  afraad kkhuda se dartay hain aur woh aisa nahi karte. kkhuda ke nazdeek yeh afraad itnay qeemti hotay hain ke woh unhein apni jannat ke liye muntakhib kar laita hai. is ne isi maqsad ki khatir yeh aazmaysh gaah banai hai .
chunancha aadmi ko pareshan honay ke bajaye yeh dekhna chahiye ke hum khud –apne daira ikhtiyar mein kkhuda khofi se kaam le rahay hain ya nahi kyunkay bas abhi adalat lagnay wali hai aur abhi faisla honay wala hai. waqt taizi se guzarta chala ja raha hai. har aadmi musalsal apna aamaal nama likh raha hai woh aik lamhay ke liye bhi nahi ruk raha phir jab mout ka farishta aata hai to woh apna aamaal nama likhna band kar deta hai baghair kisi se baat kiye chup chaap is ke sath chal deta hai aur phir woh kabhi wapas nahi aata phir woh kisi se koi rabita nahi rakhta. har aadmi aisay hi kar raha hai. duniya ki yeh kahani kitni ajeeb hai. bas lazim hai ke har aadmi apni fikar kere .
sawal is shakhs ke baray mein deen kya kehta hai jo panj وقتہ namaz ada karta hai lekin is ke sath woh rishwat bhi laita aur dhoka bhi deta hai
jawab haraam rizaq ke sath jo namaz parhi jati hai woh Allah  ke haan qabuliat nahi paati. lekin baat sirf itni hi nahi hai. insaan ka maamla yeh hota hai ke woh –apne jis amal ke sath bhi dil ki geherai ke sath chipka ho wohi amal bil akhir dosray aamaal par ghalba pa laita hai .
yeh baat to zahir hai ke is waqt is shakhs ki namaz sachey abid ki namaz nahi hai kyunkay kkhuda ka sacha bandah –apne dil se kkhuda ka farmaa bardaar bhi hota hai. lekin agar yeh shakhs –apne juraim ko dil se nagawaar jaanta khud ko ghalat qarar deta aur Allah  ke samnay sharminda hota rehta hai to yeh tawaqqa ki ja sakti hai ke is ki namaz is ki bad aamalyon par ghalba pa le yeh tauba kar le aur achay injaam ko puhanche. Albata  agar maamla bar aks sun-hwa to phir tawaqqa bhi bar aks hi ki hai kyunkay irshad baari hai
Albata  jis ne kamaai koi badi aur is ke gunah ne is ko –apne ghairay mein le لیاتو wohi log dozakh walay hain woh is mein hamesha rahen ge .
yani insaan khuwa kaisa hi namazi ya rozay rakhnay aur hajj karne wala kyun nah ho agar is ne kisi aik buraiee ko is terhan ikhtiyar kar liya ke woh buraiee is par chhaa gayi aur is ke gunah ne is ko –apne ghairay mein le liya to ab is ki sab naikian barbaad ho jayen gi aur woh jahannum mein jaye ga .
sawal naffa o nuqsaan mein shiraakat ke tasawwur se ki gayi sarmaya kaari par milnay wala munafe agar sood nahi to bank mein jama shuda raqam par milnay walay munafe ko sood kaisay kaha ja sakta hai jabkay bank ke dewalia ho jane ka imkaan hota hai aur aisi soorat mein raqum jama karanay walon ko bank ke sath nuqsaan mein shareek hona parta hai. isi terhan agar bank ke
jawab bank –apne account holdrz ko –apne kaarobar mein naffa o nuqsaan ki sharait par shareek nahi karta balkay woh unhein un ki jama shuda raqum par mutayyan muddat mein mutayyan izafah ki yaqeen dehani karata hai. isi ko sood aur rubaa kehte hain .
bank ke dewalia ho jane par account holdrz ki raqmon ka toot jana ya un ko nuqsaan ho jana ya is terhan ki baaz doosri sooraton mein unhein ghata parna kaarobar ka naffa o nuqsaan nahi hai balkay yeh bank se mutaliq afraad par afaat o hawadis ki soorat mein honay walay asraat hain. bank behar haal soodi nizaam par mabni idaara hai. usay maloom hai ke naffa o nuqsaan mein shiraakat kya hoti hai. woh naffa o nuqsaan ki sharait par logon ko –apne sath shareek nahi karta balkay sood ke usool par un se raqum laita aur unhein deta hai. chunancha is terhan ki baton se khud ko dhoka nahi دیناچاہیے .
isi terhan woh sab national saving askimin jo mutayyan raqam par mutayyan muddat mein mutayyan izafah deti hain woh bhi zahir hai ke sood hi deti hain. islam ke nazdeek aisi askimon se faida uthana haraam hai. raha kisi ka infiradi masla ke is ke paas is haraam se faida uthany ka izr mojood hai to be shak mazoor aur majboor aadmi apni zaroorat ki had tak dil ke guraiz aur na pasandeedgi ke sath is se faida utha sakta hai .
sawal sunnat ki tareef mein is qader ikhtilaaf kyun hai logon ki aksariyat kyun sunnat ki classical tareef hi ki qaail hai jabkay ghamdi sahib ke nazdeek sunnat ki tareef is se mukhtalif hai
jawab poori ummat is par mutfiq hai ke hamein nabi sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ne kkhuda ki taraf se deen ke tor par ilm bhi diya hai aur amal bhi yahi ilm o amal sahaba se tabayn ne liya aur phir un se agay yeh poori ummat mein phela hai. chunancha is pehlu se ulma mein koi ikhtilaaf nahi hai .
jab ulma ne is deen ko Madoon  karna shuru kya to is waqt mukhtalif eslehaath ka masla peda sun-hwa sunnat ka lafz bhi unheen eslehaath mein se aik hai. baaz ulma ne aap sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ke Uswah  aur aap ke aamaal ko sunnat ka naam diya baaz ne aap ki ahadees ko sunnat ka naam diya. ghamdi sahib ke nazdeek bator istilaah sunnat ke lafz ko amli tawatar se milnay walay un deeni aamaal ke liye bola jana chahiye jinhen nabi sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ne is ummat mein jari kya tha. chuna nacha woh اصطلاحا unheen کوسنت qarar dete hain .
sunnat ka yahi lafz aik doosri istilaah ke tor par bhi bola gaya hai yani baaz ulma ne un nawafil ko bhi sunnat kaha hai jinhen nabi sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ne faraiz ke baad ya un se pehlay تطوعا parha hai. اصطلاحا sunnat ka lafz kis cheez par bolna chahiye is mein mohqiqeen ki aara mukhtalif ho sakti hain aur woh mukhtalif hain. rahi yeh baat ke insanon ki aksariyat sunnat ki classical tareef hi ki qaail kyun hai to is ka jawab yeh hai ke sunnat ka lafz –apne jin istilahi maeno mein aik lambay arsay se bola jata raha hai zahir hai ke log isi ke qaail hon ge. ghamdi sahib ne sunnat ko jin istilahi maeno mein bola hai agar ummat ke nazdeek yeh ziyada mozoon hui to un sha Allah  woh usay qubool kar le gi .
sawal iddat se kya morad hai is mein aurat par kya pabandiyan hoti hain baaz log barri Umar  ki khawateen ko is se mustasna qarar dete hain kya yeh durust hai
jawab iddat ka hukum surah baqra ki darj zail ayaat mein bayan sun-hwa hai
aur tum mein se jo log wafaat pa jayen aur –apne peechay biwiyan choden to woh –apne aap ko chaar mahinay das din intzaar karayen. phir jab unn ki iddat poori ho jaye to –apne baray mein jo kuch dastoor ke mutabiq woh karen uss ka tum par koi gunah nahi hai. aur jo kuch tum karte ho Allah  ussay khoob jaanta hai .
iddat ka lafz istilaah mein is muddat ke liye istemaal hota hai jis mein biwi shohar ki taraf se Talaq  ya is ki wafaat ke baad kisi dosray shakhs se nikah nahi kar sakti. yeh muddat aslan is liye muqarrar ki gayi hai ke aurat ke pait ki soorat e haal poori terhan wazeh ho jaye. shohar ki wafaat ki soorat mein yeh iddat chaar mah das din hai. agar koi aurat –apne marhoom shohar ke ghar mein yeh iddat gzarti hai to phir is ke liye yeh bhi zaroori hai ke woh yeh sara arsa sog hi ki kefiyat mein guzaray. nabi sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ne farmaya hai
bewa aurat rangeen kapray nahi pehnay gi nah zard nah گیروسے rangay hue. woh zewraat istemaal nahi kere gi aur nah mehndi aur surma lagaye gi .
yeh iddat barri Umar  ki khawateen ko bhi guzaarni ho gi. haamla aurat ki iddat waza hamal tak hai aur bewa ghair madkhola ke liye koi iddat nahi hai .
sawal hamaray malik mein jo kaarobar bhi kya jaye is ke liye bank se sood par karzzzz lena parta hai. kya sood dena bhi islam mein isi terhan mamnoo hai jaisay ke sood lena
jawab bank waghera se sood par karzzzz lena jaaiz hai. is mein sharean koi qabahat nahi hai. Shariat  ne sood khanay yani sood lainay se mana kya hai sood dainay se nahi .
hadees mein sood khilanay walay ko bhi sood lainay walay hi ki terhan mujrim qarar diya gaya hai. yeh sood khilanay wala kon hai. baaz ulma ne sood dainay walay hi ko sood khilanay wala qarar diya hai. lekin yeh baat durust nahi hai. sood khilanay wala darasal woh agent hai jo sood Khor  ke liye gahak lata is ki numaindagi karta aur is ke soodi nizaam ko chalata hai .

jawab bank aik aisa idaara hai jo aslan soodi kaarobar karta hai yani woh kuch logon se sood ki kam sharah par raqam laita aur dosray logon ko wohi rqmin sood ki ziyada sharah par deta hai. yahi is ka asal kaarobar hai aur isi se woh apna munafe kamata hai. lehaza is ki kamaai bhi haraam hai aur is mein hissa daar ban-na bhi haraam hai .
jab aap kisi bank ke share holdar bantay hain to zahir hai ke aap is ke malkaan mein se aik fard hotay hain. chunancha ab is se koi farq nahi پڑتاکہ market mein bank ke shiyrz ki qeemat kabhi kam hoti hai aur kabhi ziyada aur un shiyrz par jo munafe hota hai woh bhi yaksaa nahi rehta. behar haal yeh share holdar bank ke malkaan mein se hai aur woh –apne soodi idaray se apna naffa haasil karta hai. lehaza hamaray khayaal mein bank ke shiyrz lainay se zaroor bachna chahiye .

jawab quran Majeed  mein yeh baat un alfaaz mein kahi gayi hai
ae imaan walo tumhari biwion aur tumhari aulaad mein se baaz tumhare liye dushman hain to un se bach kar raho aur agar tum unhein maaf karo ge dar guzar karo ge aur bakhsho ge to Allah  ghafoor o Raheem  hai. tumhare maal aur tumhari aulaad tumhare liye imthehaan hain aur Allah  ke paas bohat bara ajar hai .

Baltistan  ke zila shgr mein october ko jalsay se khitaab mein kaha ke hukoomat Pakistan  krgl ladah ke tareekhi road ko kholnay ke liye tayyar hai lekin Bharat  is mein rukawat bana sun-hwa hai .

isi terhan Baltistan  ke head quarter skrdo mein میںمہاجرین krgl ne is road ke kholnay ke haq mein mein muzahira kiya aur krgl ki taraf March  ka elaan kya jis ki himayat Maroof  qoum parast rehnuma Manzoor  Hussain  parwana ki aur is ki Padaash  mein un par riyasat mukhalif honay ka muqadma qaim kya gaya jo aaj bhi zair samaat hai .

Mosoof  ne october ko bayan mein wazeer aala Gilgit  Baltistan  Hafiz  Hafeez  Al Rehman  ko tareekh ka na ahal tareen wazeer aala qarar diya hai ab yeh maloom nahi ke woh kis tareekh ki baat kar rahay hain kyunkay khittay ki tareekh mein pehlay muntakhib wazeer aala woh khud aur dosray Hafiz  Hafeez  Al Rehman  hain aur dono hi Kashmir  al-nasal hain. darasal aisa lagta hai ke syed mehdi Shah  ko wizarat se mehroomi ke baad party ki sobai sadarat ke jane ka gham khaye ja raha hai kyunkay it-tila-aat hain peoples party ki sobai qayadat ne June  ke intikhabaat mein party ki bad tareen shikast ki zimma daari syed mehdi Shah  par aed ki hai jis ke baad party ki sobai qayadat inhen sadarat ke ohday se hataane ke liye sargaram hai .

peoples party ke zaraye ka kehna hai ke dono rehnuma sobai qayadat ke mabain ikhtilaaf ke khatmay aur tanzeem saazi ke liye Gilgit  mein mojood hain bzahir koshish yahi ho rahi hai ke syed mehdi Shah  aur syed Jaffer  Shah  ke darmiyan ikhtilafat ka khtama kar ke dono mein se kisi aik kaantkhab kya jaye lekin party ke andar aisay log mojood hain jo is se shadeed ikhtilaaf rakhtay hain. peoples party ke zaraye ka daawa hai ke do sidon ki larai میںصوبائی sadarat ka quraa amjad Hussain  advocate ya sabiq dapti speaker Jameel  Ahmed  ke naam nikal sakta hai taham peoples party ke sanjeeda halqon ko un dono ki ghair سجیدگی par shikayat hai. zaraye ke mutabiq dono rehnuma mutharrak aur sargaram zaroor hain lekin un ki jazbatiat aur jald baazi party ke liye mazeed nuqsaan ka baais banay gi mojooda sorat e haal mein syed Jaffer  Shah  hi mazboot umeed waar hain taham intikhabaat ke douran Gilgit  regain ki zimma daari un ke paas thi lekin inhen kamyabi nah mil saki yahi nakami un ke naqideen kasb se bara hathyaar hai .
doosri janib qmralzman kairah ne elaan kya hai peoples party dobarah Iqtidaar  پرآئی to khittay ko sobai status day gi dilchasp baat yeh hai mein jab peoples party ne khittay ke liye intizami package ka elaan kya Mosoof  bator wifaqi wazeer umoor وگلگت Baltistan  aur Gilgit  Baltistan  ke pehlay governor ke yeh daawa karte rahay ke peoples party ne Gilgit  Baltistan  ko Pakistan  ka panchawan soobah bnayahe jis ne bhi un bayanaat ya elanaat ki tareekhi haqayiq ke khilaaf qarar diya is ko ghaddar samait ajab alqabaat se nawaza gaya. kya Mosoof  qoum ko bta satke hain ke se tak sobai set up ke hawalay se un ke elanaat aur bayanaat durust thay ya aaj ka elaan bhar haal har do soorat mein aik baat to ghalat bayani aur dhoka hai. yeh aik tareekhi haqeeqat hai ke tanaza kshmirki wajah se hukoomat Pakistan  Gilgit  Baltistan  ko ziyada se ziyada ikhtiyarat to day sakti hai lekin aaeni soobah نہیںبنا sakti .
isi bunyaad par yeh sawal uthaya ja raha hai ke Gilgit  Baltistan  mein insidaad e dehshat gardi ki adalat ke judge Raja  Shahbaz  Khan  ki janib se aktobrko idaron ke khilaaf bayan dainay par MQM ke quied Altaf  Hussain  ko saal qaid jaedad ki zabtghi aur laakh jrmane ki saza qabil amal hai ya nahi kya aeen ke mutabiq judge sahib is terhan ka faisla dainay ka ikhtiyar rakhtay hain Mosoof  ne aik niji channel ke hawalay se bhi kuch arsa qabal isi terhan ka faisla diya tha un dono فیصلوںکا bareek beeni se jaiza liya jaye to aisa lagta hai ke yeh ikhtiyarat se tajawaz hai aur is terhan ke faislon se malik ke mukhtalif hisson mein khittay ki عدالیہ ke hawalay se misbet asraat muratab nahi ho rahay hain MQM ke quied Altaf  Hussain  ke mobayyana juraim apni jagah lekin Gilgit  Baltistan  ki adalat ka yeh faisla bhi apni jagah khud aik sawalia nishaan hai .
nuqta nazar ka yeh column mukhtalif ashaab fikar ki nigarshaat ke liye mukhtas hai. is mein shaya honay walay mazameen se idaray ka mutfiq hona zaroori nahi hai .
molana hamid Aldeen  frahi ne aik risala fi ملکوت Allah  ke naam se likha hai jo darasal un ki Tafseer  nizaam al quran ke muqadma ka aik hissa hai. yeh risala jo barri taqtee ke safhaat par mushtamil hai daira حمیدیہ madarsa alaslah saraye Meer  Azam  garh se hjri mein shaya ho chuka hai. zair-e nazar mazmoon mein isi risalay ka taaruf karaya gaya hai .
is risalay mein jaisa ke is ke naam se zahir hai ملکوت Allah  yani Allah  ki badshahat aur is ki yaktai se mutaliq umoor o masail se behas ki gayi hai. is mein baaz maqamat par nuqtay lagey hue hain jin se saaf maloom hota hai ke molana agay kuch mazeed likhna chahtay thay jisay woh nahi likh sakay. is ke ilawa is risalay ke baaz mubahis mujmal hain. taaruf mein un sab umoor ka lehaaz rakha gaya hai taakay koi baat ghair wazeh ya namukammal nah reh jaye .
molana frahi se pehlay kisi aalmِ deen ne is mauzo se tarruz nahi kya halaank توحیدی nuqta nazar se yeh aik ahem mozo ain hai. is ke feham ke baghair Muarif  quran tak rasai mushkil hai. molana frahi ne risalay ka taaruf un lafzon mein karaya hai
is kitaab ka talluq muqadma nizaam al quran se hai. is mein ملکوت Allah  ke masla se behas ki gayi hai jo aloom quran ke ahem Muarif  ka jame hai. un Muarif  se is ka taalib is waqt tak aagahi haasil nahi kar sakta hai jab tak ke is ki nigah is markazi nuqta yani ilm ملکوت Allah  par barabar murtakiz nah rahay jis se aloom ki nehrein is terhan jari hain goya kisi labraiz chashma se phoot niklee hon. chunkay hamaray ulma mein se kisi ne is ilm se tarruz nahi kya hai is liye sab se pehlay zaroori hai ke hum is ka taaruf karayen aur deen mein is ki ahmiyat ke wajoh ko tafseel se bayan karen .
molana frahi ke nazdeek is ilm ka maqam bohat ouncha hai. jumla deeni aloom ki bunyaad aur un ki haqeeqi gharz o Ghayat  kkhuda ki sifaat kamila ki sahih Maarfat  hai. yahan yeh baat malhooz rahay ke ilm sifaat ka maamla ilm zaat se bilkul mukhtalif hai. kkhuda ki sifaat ka ilm insaan ke liye baqadar zarf o haajat mumkin hai lekin zaat-e khuda wandi ka Urfan  namumkin hai. insani aqal behar haal mehdood hai aur is par har daur ke arbab_e_ aqal ka ittafaq raha hai. ehad haazir ke Ashaab ilm o nazar ka bhi yahi khayaal hai ke insani aqal apni محدودیت ki wajah se hasti mutlaq ke idraak se aajiz hai. haqeeqat yeh hai ke khuday-e buzurag o bartar nah tasawwur ki girift mein aa sakta hai aur nah takhayyul ka prِ parwaaz wahan tak pahonch sakta hai. Burhan  o istadlaal ki naarasai bhi maloom ke woh aqal hi ke saaz o barg hain .
lekin kaayenaat mryi jo Allah  ki sifaat ilm o qudrat ka aaina hai insani aqal o shaoor ke daira car ilm o feham se Mawra  nahi hai. insaan is aaina ke andar khaaliq aalam ka manwi deedar kar sakta hai. is silsilay mein hasti mutlaq ki jo sift sab se ziyada Laiq  tawajah hai woh is ki hama geer aur khalis badshahi hai yani yeh ke is kaayenaat mein is ke siwa koi dosra Ali  الاطلاق haakim o mutsarif nahi hai. is bana par insaan ka haqeeqi mabood o مطاع is ke siwa koi dosra nahi ho sakta hai .
quran Majeed  mein hazrat ibrahim alaihi salam ke mushahida fitrat ka zikar un lafzon mein aaya hai
aur hum ne بایں tor ibrahim ko asmano aur zameen ke Iqtidaar  ka mushahida karaya taakay woh yaqeen karne walon mein se ho .
is aayat ke mutabiq hazrat ibrahim alaihi salam ko Allah  ke Iqtidaar  aala ki Maarfat  nazam kaayenaat ke mushahida se haasil hui. is mushahida se un par yeh raaz khula ke is aalmِ rang o bo par aik hi zaat-e be nihayat ki hukum rani hai. is ke ilawa koi dosra wujood kaayenaat ke kisi gooshay par kisi noo ka hukum o tasarruf nahi rakhta aur is خاکداں ki har choti barri cheez is ke hukum ke agay surangoon hai .
is se maloom sun-hwa ke jo shakhs toheed ke asasi pehlu yani kkhuda ki badshahi ki yaktai se na aashna hai woh duniya ke waqeat o hawadis bilkhushoos qomon ke urooj o zawaal ke haqeeqi asbaab ke feham se qassar ho ga. ashkhaas ke sath hadaayat o ضلالت aur izzat o zillat ke jo mamlaat paish atay hain un ki tojeeh bhi is ke liye mushkil ho gi. woh har waqea aur har haadsa ko zahiri asbaab o all se marboot kar ke dekhe ga aur nateejatan ghalat nataij tak puhanche ga aur بایں tor fikar o amal ki musalsal jadah پیمائیوں ke bawajood nah to is ko zindagi ki seedhi shahrah mil sakay gi aur nah hi takhleeq hayaat ki haqeeqi Ghayat  se woh waaqif ho sakay ga .
molana frahi ne ilm ملکوت Allah  ke fawaid par اجمالا guftagu ki hai. hum yahan un ki tafseel karte hain taakay is ilm ki ahmiyat aur is ke fawaid poooray tor par wazeh ho jayen .
is ilm se duniya ki tareekh ka feham haasil hota hai aur qalb ko itminan milta hai aur is haqeeqat se insaan bakhabar hota hai ke bohat se dunewi ahwaal o waqeat jo bzahir shar maloom hotay hain باعتبار injaam kher hotay hain. yeh aik falsfiyana masla hai .
is mein shak nahi ke is duniya mein kher ke sath shrka bhi wujood hai. lekin yeh aik izafi wujood hai is ko mustaqil bil zaat wujood ki hesiyat haasil nahi hai. is liye ke jo kkhuda is kaayenaat ka khaaliq hai is se shrka Sadoor  mumkin nahi hai ke woh kher mehez hai .
yahan hum shar ke wujood ko baaz misalon se wazeh karte hain. har shakhs ki nazar mein bahaduri aik umdah sift hai aur aik maienay mein yeh kher hi ka aik pehlu hai lekin is se dushman ko jo nuqsaan pohanchana hai woh is ki nazar mein shar hai. isi terhan aag bzatِ khud kher hai aur insani zindagi ke liye is ka wujood na guzeer hai lekin isi aag se tabahi o barbadi ke waqeat bhi paish atay hain khait khalyaan aur makaan jal kar khakstar ho jatay hain. kya hum aag ke is amal ko shar kahin ge kon hai jo shab ko shar kahe ga woh to gehwaara raahat hai. lekin dekhen ke duniya ke aksar gunah aur juraim tareqi ke parday hi mein injaam paate hain. un misalon se maloom sun-hwa ke shar darasal aik salbi haalat hai is ko ijabi hesiyat haasil nahi hai. yeh hesiyat sirf kher ko haasil hai .
baaz mojoodaat aalam ki shakal mein hum ko jo shar nazar aata hai woh bhi izafi wujood hai aur tarkeeb maadi ke nateejay mein peda hota hai. yeh baat maloom hai ke aalam khaki ki har shai ki tarkeeb o taamer mein mukhtalif alnoa anasir shaamil hain lekin woh anasir bajaye khud kher o shar ki sifaat se khaali hain. is ke bawajood hum dekhte hain ke unheen anasir ki tarkeeb se aisi bhi cheeze banti hain jin se shrka Sadoor  hota hai. is se maloom sun-hwa ke shrka talluq tarkeeb se hai nah ke Johar takhleeq se .
wujood shar par aik dosray pehlu se ghhor karen. har cheez ki takhleeq mein usool azdaad ki karfrmayi hai yani har wujood misbet aur manfi do akayyon par mushtamil hai. is kaayenaat maadi ka sab se chhota juz atom hai aur yeh usool azdaad ki sab se umdah misaal hai. is ke ajzaye tarkeebi mein aliktran manfi aur پروٹان misbet sift rakhta hai lekin atom ka wujood aur is ki saari qowat isi misbet aur manfi sift ki mrhonِ minnat hai .
is pehlu se kaayenaat ka مطالہ kijiyej to maloom ho ga ke woh tamam ashya jo bzahir shar dikhayi deti hain darasal hsolِ kher ka zareya hain. agar un cheezon mein shar mojood nah hota to kher ki Maarfat  mumkin nah thi .
haqeeqat yeh hai ke insaan ki saari tamadduni trqyan is mukhalif mahol ki deen hain jo darasal shar ki aik soorat hai aur jis se woh aaghaz آفرینش se barabar do chaar raha hai. agar khaaliq aalam ki taraf se yeh mukhalif mahol muhayya nah kya jata to insaan ke nafsi kamalaat ka izhaar mumkin nah tha. gharz jis pehlu se bhi dekhieye yahi maloom hota hai ke shar insaan ki Rohani  aur maadi dono terhan ki taraqqi ke liye aik na guzeer Amel  hai .
is masla ko aik aur zavia nigah se dekhen. quran Majeed  ke bayan ke mutabiq insaan ki ghayat takhleeq imthehaan hai
is ne mout aur zindagi peda ki taakay tumhara imthehaan le ke tum mein kon باعتبار amal acha hai .
agar kher ke sath shar ki takhleeq nah hoti to phir imthehaan ke koi maienay nah hotay. insaan ko iradah o ikhtiyar isi liye diya gaya hai ke woh apni marzi se khuwa kher ki pairwi kere ya shar ki dosray lafzon mein kkhuda ka Mutee  banay ya nafs amarh ka jo insaan ko barabar buraiee ke liye اکستاتا rehta hai .
is imthehaan ka talluq afraad ke sath aqwam se bhi hai. un ke sath shar ke jo mamlaat paish atay hain woh darasal is imthehaan ke nataij hain jin ko Allah  taala kabhi kabhi is duniya mein is liye zahir kar deta hai taakay buray logon ko tanbeeh ho aur achay logon ko tasalii ke Allah  ka qanonِ mukafaat barhaq hai .
ملکوت Allah  se hum ko tareekh deen ka ilm haasil hota hai jis ka talluq aqwam ke urooj o zawaal se hai. yeh aik tareekhi masla hai .
aik tareekh to woh hai jis ka daira maadi asbaab o all ke gird ghoomta hai aur is mein siyasi samaji aur iqtisadi awamil ko ahmiyat haasil hai aur khayaal kya jata hai ke yahi awamil tareekh ki soorat giri karte hain. lekin aik deeni tareekh bhi hai jis mein tareekh ki tabeer ikhlaqi qadron ki bunyaad par ki jati hai yani ikhlaq ki bulandi aik qoum ko baam urooj tak le jati hai aur isi ki pasti is ko zillat ke khud mein gira deti hai. bilashuba qomon ke urooj o zawaal mein samaji aur iqtisadi awamil bhi kaam karte hain lekin is maamla mein faisla kin cheez Aamaal ikhlaq hain jin ka talluq tamam tar batin se hai. quran Majeed  ki do ayatain is ikhlaqi usool ki taraf hamari rehnuma yi karti hain aur woh darj zail hain
be shak Allah  kisi qoum ki haalat ko is waqt tak nahi badalta jab tak ke woh apni androoni haalat ko tabdeel nah kar le .
yeh is bana par sun-hwa ke Allah  is Nemat  ko jo kisi qoum ko ataa kar chuka ho is waqt tak nahi badalta jab tak ke woh apni androoni haalat ko tabdeel nah kar le .
un dono ayaton se jo usool مستنبط hota hai woh ikhlaqi usool hai. Allah  taala jab kisi qoum ko koi Nemat  maslan maal o doulat aur malik o Iqtidaar  waghera ataa karta hai to is Nemat  ki baqa aur is ka zawaal dono is qoum ki androoni haalat par munhasir hotay hain. jab tak is ki nafsi haalat Nemat  ke taqazoon se hum aahang hoti hai is waqt tak woh Nemat  is ke paas baqi rehti hai. lekin jis waqt is ki nafsi haalat tabdeel ho kar Nemat  ke taqazoon ke barkhilaf ho jati hai to woh Nemat  is se chean li jati hai. is ka wazeh matlab yeh hai ke aqwam ka urooj o zawaal un ki nafsi yani ikhlaqi haalat ke tabay hai kharji halaat ka is se bohat kam talluq hai. kharji halaat darasal qomon ke baatini ahwaal ka aks hotay hain. woh aik aisa aaina hai jis mein kisi qoum ki ikhlaqi haalat ke tamam marahil o Manazil  saaf tor par dekhe ja satke hain .
is zavia nigah se agar tareekh aalam ka mutalea kya jaye to woh nihayat mufeed aur nateeja khaiz saabit ho ga bilkhushoos un logon ke liye jo ehley taqwa hain. yeh mutalea unhein is Haqeeqat nafs الامری se aagah kere ga ke is duniya mein urooj o sar bulandi sirf متقین yani Allah  taala ke sachey farmaa bardaroon ke liye makhsoos hai. agar is ke barkhilaf soorat miley to yaqeen kar len ke متقین mojood nahi hain. ghair متقین ko hukoomat millti hi is waqt hai jab kkhuda ki zameen ahal taqwa se khaali ho jati hai. aik Ajal muayyan tak kaarobar duniya ko behar haal chalna hai is liye mushiyat Ellahi is kaam ke liye is qoum ka intikhab karti hai jo makhlooq kkhuda ki kifalat aur is ke mamlaat ke nazam o insaram ki behtar salahiyat rakhti ho. lekin yeh intizam bilkul earzi hota hai. mushiyat Ellahi barabar is baat ki muntazir rehti hai ke ehley taqwa ka koi munazzam giroh utthay aur ghair متقین se Iqtidaar  le kar un ke hawalay kar day .
is se شریعتوں ke ikhtilaaf ki haqeeqat maloom hoti hai. hum dekhte hain ke duniya ke barray mazahab bilkhushoos islam yahoodiyat aur esaiyat ki شریعتوں mein wazeh farq o ikhtilaaf hai. lekin agar ghhor se dekhen to maloom ho ga ke yeh farq o ikhtilaaf bilkul zahiri hai un ki rooh وکنہ mein koi ikhtilaaf nahi hai aur nah ho sakta tha. tamam شریعتوں ka johar asli aik hai yani kher o taqwa aur is mein koi ikhtilaaf nahi hai .
agar is johar asli par barabar nazar rehti to شرائع ke zahiri ikhtilaaf ke bawajood deen ke naam par nah to firqay bantay aur nah hi mukhtalif qomon ke darmiyan mazhabi jhagray peda hotay. lekin aisa nahi sun-hwa. شرائع ke zahiri ikhtilaaf ko bunyaad qarar day kar har mazhab ke پیروؤں ne dosray mazhab ke پیروؤں ko gum raah be deen aur کشتنی qarar diya. yahood o nasari ne is maamla mein ziyada ghallo kya. unheen ke mutaliq quran Majeed  mein aik jagah farmaya hai
yahood kehte hain keh isaai be asal hain aur isaai kehte hain ke yahood be asal hain halaank yeh kitaab ki tilawat karte hain .
aur is se barh kar zalim kon ho ga jo Allah  ki ibadat gaahon mein is ke zikar se rokay aur un ki weerani ke darpay ho .
musalmanoon ki rawish bhi yahood o nasari se mukhtalif nahi hai. unhon ne bhi zahir Shariat  ko dekha is ke batin yani taqwa ko nah dekha. is tarz ka laazmi nateeja wohi nikla jo is se pehlay nikal chuka tha. chunancha musalmanoon mein bhi yahood o nasari ki terhan firqay banay saf bndyan huien masajid o madaris allag hue aur aik firqay ne dosray firqay ko kafir o be deen kaha hatta ke masajid ki be hurmati aur masoom namazion ke qatal ke waqeat se bhi is qoum ki tareekh khaali nahi hai. aur hanooz yeh afsos naak silsila jari hai .
wahdat e ala ka laazmi taqaza wahdat e Shariat  hai. agar hum yeh tasleem karte hain ke is kaayenaat ka aik hi haakim o Amir  hai to aslan is ki Shariat  bhi aik ho gi. quran Majeed  ki yeh aayat is haqeeqat ki tarjuman hai
kya woh deen khuda wandi ke siwa koi aur deen chahtay hain halaank asmano aur zameen mein jo bhi hai sab charonachar isi ke agay sir itaat jukaye hue hain aur sab ko isi ki taraf lout kar jana hai .
nazam kalaam se bilkul wazeh hai ke deen Allah  se jo aalam تکوینی aur aalam تشریعی dono ke liye yaksaa hai kkhuda ka aeen itaat morad hai. farq sirf yeh hai ke aalmِ تکوینی mein yeh jabran nafiz hai aur aalam تشریعی mein طوعا matloob hai. agar aap aalam تکوینی ke qawaneen ka mutalea karen to maloom ho ga ke woh mukhtalif alnoa hain. jo qawaneen aalam samawi ke liye hain woh aalam khaki ke qawaneen se mukhtalif hain hatta ke un dono عوالم ke –apne qawaneen bhi mukhtalif hain. lekin un sab qawaneen ko jo cheez aik rishta wahdat mein proti hai woh qanoon itaat hai yani khaaliq kaayenaat ki kaamil farmaa bardari .
aalam تشریعی ke qawaneen ka bhi yahi haal hai. Allah  taala ki taraf se har daur mein mukhtalif Anabia  o Rasal  ke zareya jo Shariat  bhi aayi is ki rooh aik thi yani dil ki poori Raza  o raghbat ke sath kkhuda ki itaat o bandagi. isi ka islahi naam taqwa hai. شرائع mein jo zahiri farq o ikhtilaaf nazar aata hai woh aitbaari hai nah ke haqeeqi. شرائع ki rooh jaisa ke pehlay zikar sun-hwa taqwa hai aur is mein koi ikhtilaaf nahi. quran Majeed  mein aik jagah is ko khairaat ke lafz se tabeer kya gaya hai
hum ne tum mein se har aik ke liye aik Shariat  aur tareeqa muqarrar kar diya hai aur agar Allah  ko Manzoor  hota to tum sab ko aik hi Ummat bana deta. jo Shariat  tum ko di hai is mein tumhara imthehaan le. pas neki mein musabqat karo. tum sab ko Allah  hi ki taraf lout kar jana hai. phir jis cheez mein tum ikhtilaaf kya karte thay is se tum ko bakhabar kere ga .
is aayat ke mutabiq duniya ki har qoum ko allag allag Shariat  di gayi hai. Allah  taala is amar par Qadir  tha ke jumla aqwam ko aik hi Shariat  deta jis mein koi farq nah hota lekin is ne aisa nahi kya aur is ki wajah bhi bta di yani imthehaan. kis baat ka imthehaan is baat ka imthehaan ke log Ashkaal Shariat  ko ziyada ahmiyat dete hain ya rohِ Shariat  yani kher o taqwa ko jo tamam شرائع ki asal o asaas hai aur jis par roz akhirat Foze  o Falah  ka husool munhasir hai .
quran mein aik jagah qurbani ke zikar mein farmaya gaya hai
Allah  tak janwar ka gosht aur is ka khoon nahi pohanchana balkay jo cheez is tak pahunchti hai woh tumhara taqwa hai .
haqeeqat namaz ke bayan mein irshad sun-hwa hai
woh momin kamyaab hain jo apni namazon mein Khashoo  ikhtiyar karte hain .
un dono ayaton se maloom sun-hwa ke Allah  ke nazdeek asal cheez jo qabil lehaaz hai woh rohِ Shariat  yani taqwa hai. agar kisi ne qurbani ki aur is ka dil taqwa se khaali hai to zahir Shariat  ke aitbaar se is ki qurbani ki aur is ka dil taqwa se khaali hai to zahir Shariat  ke aitbaar se is ki qurbani ho gayi lekin Allah  ki nazar mein yeh qurbani mooatbar nahi hai. isi terhan agar kisi ne namaz parhi aur is ke vajbat o faraiz mein koi kami o Beshi  nahi ki magar dil mein Khashoo  ki kefiyat nah thi to Shariat  ke nuqta nazar se is ki namaz ho gayi lekin kon keh sakta hai ke yeh namaz roz-e- akhirat is ke liye kamyabi ka zareya ban sakay gi .
aayat mazkoorah mein aik aur ahem baat kahi gayi hai ke شریعتوں ke zahir y farq ki bana par mazhabi nazaa ghalat hai. quran ke bayan ke mutabiq is duniya mein mazhabi ikhtilafat ka faisla mumkin nahi hai. is gharz ke liye Allah  ne akhirat ka din muqarrar kya hai. is liye zahir Shariat  mein ikhtilaaf par jhagra karne ke bajaye rohِ Shariat  yani neki o taqwa ki taraf تیزگامی ho ke tanha yahi cheez falah akhirat ki zamin hai .
is se kkhuda ke usool siyasat ka ilm haasil hota hai aur woh Adal  aur hikmat ka usool hai. kaayenaat ki har cheez is usool ke mutabiq –apne fitri wazaif injaam di rahi hai. is ilm ka laazmi taqaza hai ke insani muashra bhi is usool par qaim ho. is se inhiraf kar ke kisi achay samaaj ka qiyam o baqa mumkin nahi hai. is ki aik Ibrat  naak misaal ehad jadeed mein roos ki hai. is malik mein ishtirakiat ki nakami ki sab se barri wajah usool hikmat se inhiraf tha. ishtirakiat nwazon ne jo samaji muashi aur siyasi qawaneen waza kiye is mein samaaj ke tamam tabqaat ke liye insaaf nahi tha. is ke ilawa woh insani fitrat ke khilaaf thay .
lekin Adal  aur hikmat par mabni qanoon saazi aik mushkil kaam hai. qanoon saazi karne walon ka talluq laazmi tor par samaaj hi se ho ga is liye jo bhi qanoon is mein is ke ghalib tabqa ke mafadaat dosray tabqaat par laziman haawi hon ge. agar hukoomat ghair jamhoori ho to phir Adal  ka qiyam aur bhi mushkil hai .
insani maashron ki tareekh mein zulm o istehsal ke jo andoh naak waqeat mlitay hain is ki wajah wohi hai jis ka oopar zikar sun-hwa. shakhsi aur jamati khud ghrzyon ke ilawa insaan ki fitrat mein intahaa pasandi ke rujhanaat bhi paye jatay hain. woh hamesha aik intahaa se doosri intahaa tak gaya hai. is intahaa pasandi ka wahid ilaaj yeh hai ke wahi ko jo Adal  o hikmat par mabni khudai qanoon hai aqal ke sath makhloot kya jaye. is wahi ka dosra naam quran hakeem hai. yeh kitaab batati hai ke Allah  ki saltanat kis terhan hikmat Adal  aur rehmat ke usoolon par qaim hai. rehmat ka matlab qanoon shikni nahi balkay hudood aeen ke andar zaroori had tak Afoo  o dar guzar hai. is ka matlab yeh sun-hwa ke aik misali insani muashra ka qiyam unheen usool salasa ki pairwi ke zareya mumkin hai .
is ilm se aqal ki ahmiyat zahir hoti hai. kkhuda jis hasti ka naam hai is ko hkma ki zabaan mein aqlِ mujarad aur Shaoor mutlaq kaha gaya hai aur isi ki aik adna tajallii insani shaoor bhi hai. is liye zaroori hai ke hamara koi amal aqal o shaoor ke manafi nah ho. aqal ki tauheen o tardeed ka matlab darasal kkhuda ki aik sift ki تنقیص o tardeed hai .
ahal ilm jantay hain ke kisi daur mein bhi Allah  ki taraf se qawaneen ki tafseeli soorten nazil nahi huien balkay ziyada tar usool yani kuliyat qanoon diye gaye taakay insaan apni aqlِ khudadad ki madad se halaat o zaroof ki riayat karte hue zeli qawaneen bana sakay. kkhuda ki aakhri kitaab yani quran Majeed  mein bhi yahi tareeqa ikhtiyar kya gaya hai. is ke ziyada tar qawaneen kalie noiyat ke hain. aur is ki gharz wohi hai jis ka oopar zikar sun-hwa .
lekin yeh aik ajeeb baat hai ke ahal mazhab ne taqreeban har daur mein aqal ki tauheen ki hai aur deen o mazhab ke mamlaat mein is ke istemaal ko acha samjha hai. musalman bhi is se mustasna nahi hain. molana room ne aqal ko shetan aur un ke shagird manwi allama iqbal ne is ayyar kaha hai halaank quran Majeed  mein aqal ki tauseef warid hai aur bakasrat maqamat par anfs o Afaq  ke assaar o Mazahir  mein ghhor o fikar ki dawat di gayi hai. quran ne un logon ko janwar kaha hai jo aqal se kaam nahi letay .
quran ki is wazeh taleem ke bawajood aakhir kya wajah hai ke bohat se ulma islam ne aqal ki buraiee bayan ki hai jaisa ke oopar zikar sun-hwa. is ki wajah ghaliban yeh hai ke unhon ne aqal ke jo amli Mazahir  dekhe un se yeh qiyaas kar liya ke aqal imaan ki dushman hai. is ke ilawa insaan jazbaat aur khwahisaat bhi rakhta hai. is liye jin logon ki aqal khaam hoti hai woh basa auqaat jazbaat se maghloob ho jati hai. dosray lafzon mein Makhdum  se khadim ban jati hai. lekin jo aqal pukhta hoti hai woh jazbaat se maghloob nahi hoti aur –apne wazifa asli yani istadlaal
is ilm se hamaray liye aasaan ho jata hai ke hum Allah  ki taraf mansoob baaz mutazaad af-aal maslan hadaayat o ضلالت aur rehmat o azaab ki sahih tojeeh kar saken. bzahir yeh baat pareshan kin hai ke jo Allah  hadaayat deta hai woh gum raah bhi karta hai. isi terhan jo zaat Rehman  o Raheem  hai is darja Raheem  ke kal aasman o zameen ki پہنائیاں bhi is ka ihata karne se qassar hain is ki taraf azaab ki nisbat kis terhan ki ja sakti hai. har daur ke Ashaab ilm ne jin mein mazhabi aur ghair mazhabi dono terhan ke log shaamil hain is mushkil sawal ka jawab dainay ki koshish ki hai .
aik taraf hum dekhte hain ke is aalam maadi ki har cheez itaat o انقیاد ki raah mein gaam zan hai mamooli hukum aduli ka tasawwur bhi un ke liye mahaal hai. lekin insaan ka maamla is se mukhtalif hai. woh agar itaat karta hai to nafarmani bhi karta hai. is se bilkul wazeh hai ke woh iradah o ikhtiyar rakhta hai jis se doosri makhloqaat mahroom hain. quran Majeed  ki mutadid ayaat se is khayaal ki taied hoti hai. maslan aik jagah farmaya hai
hum ne is ko rasta dikha diya hai ab woh shukar karne wala banay ya kufar karne wala .
kya hum ne is ke liye do ankhen aur aik zabaan aur do lab nahi banaye aur hum ne is ko dono rastay nahi dukhaay
jo shakhs buraiee kamata hai to is ke ksb ka wabaal khud is ke oopar hai .
hum ne luqman ko hikmat ataa ki ke tum Allah  ka shukar baja lao. aur jo shakhs shukar karta hai woh –apne liye karta hai aur jo kufar karta hai yani na shukri to Allah  be niaz aur sazawar hamd hai .
lekin insani iradah o ikhtiyar mutlaq nahi balkay mehdood aur mushiyat Ellahi ke tabay hai jaisa ke quran mein aik jagah farmaya gaya hai
aur tum nahi chahtay magar yeh ke dono jahan ka rab bhi chahay .
insani iradah o ikhtiyar ko tasleem kar lainay ke baad hadaayat o ضلالت ka masla hal ho jata hai. is silsilay mein qanoon qudrat yeh hai ke jo bandah apni marzi se hadaayat ki raah par chalna chahta hai kkhuda ki Mushiyat  is ki hum nawai karti hai aur isi ka naam khudai hadaayat hai jaisa ke farmaya hai
aur woh log jo hamari raah mein intehai koshish karte hain hum un ko apni raah zaroor deikhein ge aur Allah  naiko karon ke sath hai .
aur jo bandah apni khushi se ضلالت ka rasta ikhtiyar karta hai to Mushiyat  khuda wandi is mein muzahim nahi hoti aur ضلالت ki raah mein chalna is ke liye aasaan ho jata hai. Allah  ke gum raah karne ka yahi matlab hai. farmaya hai
ae logo Allah  ka wada bilkul sacha hai. to aisa nah ho ke dunewi zindagi tum ko dhoka mein daal day aur nah aisa ho ke dhokay baz Allah  ke baray mein tum ko kisi dhokay mein mubtala kar day. be shak shetan tumhara dushman hai is liye tum bhi is ko apna dushman samjhoo. woh –apne giroh ko bulaataa hai taakay woh دوزخیوں mein shaamil ho jayen. jin logon ne kufar kya un ke liye sakht azaab hai aur jo log imaan laaye aur unhon ne achay kaam kiye un ke liye bakhshish aur ajar azeem hai. to kya aisa shakhs jis ko is ka Amal bad acha kar ke dekhaya gaya phir woh is ko acha samajhney laga Allah  jis ko chahta hai gum raah karta hai aur jis ko chahta ہیہدایت deta hai. pas tum un ke haal par afsos kar ke –apne aap ko halkaan nah karo. be shak Allah  ko un ke tamam kamon ki khabar hai .
un ayaat se maloom sun-hwa ke imaan aur kufar bande ke ikhtiyaari aamaal hain aur yeh ikhtiyar is ko is liye diya gaya hai taakay is ki azmaish ho ke kon acha amal karta hai aur kon ikhtiyar ka ghalat istemaal kar ke buray kaam karta hai
kkhuda ka azaab is ki rehmat ke manafi nahi balkay is ka ain iqtiza hai. Allah  ne insaan ko iradah o ikhtiyar ki Nemat  se nawaza kher o shar mein imtiaz ki salahiyat ataa ki aur lutaf mazeed ke tor par Anabia  o Rasal  ke zareya achhai aur buraiee dono ki rahein bilkul wazeh kar den. ab yeh faisla karna insaan ka kaam hai ke woh hadaayat ki raah par chalay ya kufar ki raah ikhtiyar kere lekin is haq intikhab ke nataij se woh nahi bach sakta hai. duniya mein Amal bad ke nataij ko kabhi kabhar sirf is liye zahir kar diya jata hai ke ghaafil log khabar daar ho jayen aur buray log tauba ki taraf mael hon taakay akhirat ke ziyada barray azaab se bach saken. farmaya hai
insaan ke –apne hathon ki kamaai ki wajah se khushki aur tri mein fasaad barpaa ho gaya hai taakay un ke baaz aamaal ka un ko maza چکھائے taakay baz aa jayen .
pas Allah  ne is ko akhirat aur duniya ke azaab mein pakar liya. be shak is mein Ibrat  hai har is shakhs ke liye jo Allah  se daray .
aur hum barray azaab se pehlay un ko qareeb ke azaab ka maza chkhayin ge taakay woh baz aa jayen .
ملکوت Allah  ka bunyadi mafhuum jaisa ke is ke naam se zahir hai Allah  ki hakmiyat mutalqa hai jo tamam aasmani mazahab mein aik mutfiq alaihi usool raha hai. yeh doosri baat hai ke امتداد zamana ke sath har mazhab ke maan-ne walay is bunyadi usool se munharif ho kar shirk ki mukhtalif raahon mein Butt  gaye. is mutfiq alaihi usool ka zikar quran Majeed  mein un lafzon mein sun-hwa hai
ke do ke ae ehley kitaab aao aik aisi baat ki taraf jo hamaray aur tumahray darmiyan yaksaa hai. hum Allah  ke siwa kisi dosray ki bandagi nah karen aur kisi ko is ka shareek nah th_hrayin aur hum mein se aik dosray ko kkhuda ke siwa rab qarar nah day .
is hakmiyat mutalqa ke do pehlu hain aik ka talluq aalmِ تکوینی se aur dosray ka aalam تشریعی se hai. molana frahi ne hakmiyat mutalqa ke un dono pehluo se behas ki hai اوراثبات mein aqli o naqli dono terhan ke dalail diye hain. مؤخرالذکر ki tashreeh mein tareekh bilkhushoos mazhabi tareekh ko bator Daleel  paish kya hai .
aalam تکوینی mein Allah  ki hakmiyat ke mutaliq shuru se mukhtalif nuqta haae nazar rahay hain. baaz logon ne duniya mein معاصی aur alaam ko dekha aur yeh bhi dekha ke jo log jor o zulm ke zimma daar hain unheen ko ghalba haasil hai aur Saleh  log maghloob hain is se unhon ne yeh nateeja akhaz kar liya ke is duniya ka koi haakim o Amir  nahi hai. agar koi kkhuda hai jo ilm o Adal  ki sifaat bhi rakhta ho to un معاصی o masaaib ki kya tojeeh ki jaye gi yeh ملاحدہ ka giroh hai .
مجوسیوں ne is mushkil ko is terhan haal kya ke diwaala bana liye aik mabood kher aur dosra mabood shar. nasari un se bhi do qadam agay nikal gaye. unhon ne saaf keh diya ke duniya par shetan ki hukoomat hai. matzlh ne yeh tojeeh paish ki ke شرور o ذنوب ka talluq bundon ke af-aal se hai. lekin sawal yeh hai ke bachon ki takaleef ki wajah kya hai kon keh sakta hai ke is ki wajah un ke af-aal hain. aur mushriqeen ne farz kar liya ke is kaayenaat par aik ke bajaye mutadid khudaon ki hukoomat hai. yunan ke mushriqeen ka yahi aqeedah tha .
molana frahi ne kkhuda ke wujood aur is ki hakmiyat ke mutaliq mukhtalif mkatb fikar ka tanqeedi jaiza liya hai aur yeh baat wazeh kar di hai ke insaan ki aqal aur is ke aloom har cheez ki rooh o quna ke idraak se qassar hain. insaan ke liye yeh mumkin nahi ke woh Allah  taala ke tamam af-aal ki haqeeqat o Ghayat  ko mukammal tor par jaan sakay. is silsilay mein molana ne رواقیین ka qoul naqal karte hue likha hai ke duniya ka har waqea –apne andar kher o hikmat ke pehlu rakhta hai khuwa woh kher o hikmat zahir ho ya posheeda. hamari aqal mehdood hai is liye har cheez ki haqeeqat ka idraak is ke liye mushkil hai. aqal ke liye is ke siwa koi charah nahi ke khuday-e wahid par imaan laaye .
jin logon ne wujood kkhuda ka inkaar kya hai un ke inkaar ki bunyaad ilm ke bajaye sara sar zan o تخمین par hai. agar woh ghhor o tadabbur se kaam letay to duniya mein shar ke wujood aur zulm o istehsal ke waqeat ki haqeeqi allt maloom kar satke thay. un ka inkaar kkhuda khud un ke qoul ke khilaaf hai. un ka inkaar saabit karta hai ke woh khud ko is kaayenaat ke bil-muqabil aik bartar wujood khayaal karte hain. aur yahi cheez is baat ki Daleel  hai ke koi is se bhi bartar wuju diye jis ne un ke nafoos ko kaayenaat par bartari ataa ki hai. nafs ki yeh bartari iradah o ikhtiyar ki Mazhar  hai. insani nafoos mein iradah o ikhtiyar ki qowat tasleem kar lainay ke baad duniya mein zulm o istehsal ke waqeat aur khud nafs insani mein shar ki mojoodgi ka mafhuum bilkul wazeh ho jata hai ke yeh iradah o ikhtiyar ke laazmi smrat hain .

gaal … Pakistan  ne Srilanka ko gaal test mein wicketon se shikast day kar teen matchon ki series mein aik sifar ki bartari haasil karli .
gaal international stadium mein khailay gaye match mein Srilanka ne Pakistan  ko jeet ke liye runs ka hadaf diya jo is baghair koi wicket gawaion haasil kar liya .
Mohammad  Hafeez  aur Ahmed  Shahzad  runs بناکرناٹ out rahay. umdah batting par Sarfraz  Ahmed  ko mean of di match qarar diya gaya .
test ke aakhri din Srilanka ne doosri namukammal ining runs do khilari out se shuru pehli hi gaind par home team ki pehli wicket girgaee yasir Shah  ne night watch mean ko sifar par chalta kya .
is ke baad krwna rantay aur three manay ne achi batting ki lekin Wahab  Riaz  ne Younis  Khan  ki madad se تھریمانے ko ke infiradi score par out kar diya .
doosri janib krwna rantay ne apni nisf century mukammal ki. khanay ke waqfay par krwna rantay aur mathews runs ke sath craze par mojood thay .
khail ke dosray session mein bhi maizban team ki wickten waqfay waqfay se girty rahen captain mathews runs bana kar یاسرشاہ ki gaind par azhar Ali  ko catch day baithy .
krwna rantay bhi runs bana kar yasir Shah  ka shikaar banay. وتھا nageh sirf aik run bana sakay un ki wicket bhi yasir Shah  ke hissay mein aayi. prasad ko runs par Zulfiqar  Babar  ne pavellion ki raah dikhayi. ہیراتھ bhi aik run bana kar yasir Shah  ko wicket day baithy. چندیمل runs bana kar yasir Shah  ki gaind par out hue yun Srilanka ki poori team apni doosri ining mein runs bana saki aur Pakistan  ko gaal test mein kamyabi ke liye runs ka hadaf mila hai .
yasir Shah  ne doosri ining mein khiladion ka shikaar kya test ki dono ining mein yasir Shah  ne wickten haasil kee. Wahab  Riaz  ne do jabkay Zulfiqar  Babar  ne aik wicket haasil ki. Pakistan  ko jeet ke liye runs ka nisbatan aasaan hadaf mila jo is ne baghair kisi nuqsaan ke haasil kar liya .
