pichlle dinon insaaf nah milnay par aik aala adalat mein aik khatoon Sundas  Farooq  ne khodsozi karne ki koshish ki. isi terhan Lahore  high court ne aik mafroor mulzim ke rishte daaron ko be ja pareshan karne ke khilaaf aik darkhwast ka notice letay hue –apne remarks mein kaha hai ke kisi mulzim ko girftar karna police ki zimma daari hai. is ke rishte daaron par dabao nahi dala ja sakta kyunkay kisi bhi shakhs ke jurm ki saza dosray ko nahi di ja sakti .
is mein shuba nahi ke aala adaltin aisay mamlaat mein is noiyat ke remarks pehlay bhi kayi martaba day chuki hain magar police ki zayadtio ka silsila jon ka ton qaim hai. is Soorat haal par aik Danish  war ne likha hai
agar saarhay teen laakh ehalkaron ki police force aur senkron hazaron wakeelon aur jajon ki juditional force mil kar Sundas  Farooq  jaisay muzloomon ko insaaf nahi day sakti to kam az kam yeh idaray mil kar un muzloomon ko aik aik pistol aur matti ke tail ki aik aik bottle hi day den ke jo mazloom agay barh kar apna haq wusool kar satke hain woh kar len aur jo is ki ahliat nahi rakhtay woh kisi konay kisi gooshay mein baith kar –apne oopar tail chhrhkin aur chup chaap jal mrin agar aap kisi haq daar ko haq nahi day satke to aap is ko marnay ka haq to den .
is se inkaar nahi ke hamaray haan adalaton mein hsolِ insaaf ke naaqis intizam aur police ke zulm ke masail bohat sangeen soorat ikhtiyar kar chuke hain magar zaroori hai ke is surat_e_ haal ki hikmat aur danai ke sath islaah karne ki koshish ki jaye aur is muamlay mein jazbatiat se guraiz kya jaye. logon ko asleha pakarney qanoon –apne haath mein lainay ki targheeb dena maslay ka hal nahi balkay mazeed aur sangeen tar masail peda karne ki ghair shaori koshish hai .
isi terhan hum ne dekha hai ke halaat ki sakhti se tang aa kar khudkushi karne walon ke baray mein hamaray Danish  war jab likhte hain to khudkushi karne walon ki himayat karte un se hamdardi ka izhaar karte mulki nizaam ko kostay aur hukoomat ko bura bhala kehte hain. hum samajte hain ke yeh aik ghair mutawazan rawayya hai. zaroori hai ke aisay moqaon par khudkushi karne aur aisi koshish karne walon par bhi tanqeed ki jaye un ki buzdilana rawish ki malamat ki jaye aur halaat ka mardana waar muqaabla nah karne par muzammat ki jaye .
agar nabiyo ki zindagi ka mutalea kya jaye to maloom ho ga ke un ke oopar be panah zulm dhaaye gaye un ke sathiyon ki zindagi ajeeran kar di gayi magar unhon ne sabr kya aur –apne sathiyon ko bhi sabr karne ki Talqeen  ki halaat ka datt kar muqaabla karne ki naseehat ki zindah reh kar zindagi ke masail se nabard aazma honay ki taleem di aur akhirat ki jaza o saza ki Tazkeer  ki .
yeh baat barray wusooq ke sath kahi ja sakti hai ke jo log khudkushi karte hain woh laazmi tor par deeni shaoor se aari hotay hain. agar woh is shaoor se behra yab hon to kabhi khudkushi jaisi buzdilana harkat nah karen. kyunkay agar woh deeni shaoor se behra yab hotay to un par yeh haqeeqat bilkul wazeh hoti ke yeh duniya aik aazmaysh gaah hai. is duniya mein museebatein aur takleifein aani hi hain. yeh kkhuda ki scheme ka laazmi hissa hain. isi terhan unhein yeh bhi maloom hota ke yeh duniya jaza aur saza ke usool par nahi chal rahi. is waqt kkhuda ne sab ko dheel day rakhi hai is liye yahan kabhi kaamil Adal  wujood mein nahi aana. kabhi har zalim ko saza nahi milni. kabhi har mazloom ki mukammal talaafi nahi honi. yeh sab masail akhirat mein hal hon ge. kaamil Adal  roz-e- Adal  hi mein wujood mein aaye ga. zalim ko is ke har zulm ki saza qayamat hi mein miley gi. mazloom ki mukammal talaafi kkhuda hi ke hathon se ho gi .
chunancha deeni shaoor ke haamil log deen aur mulki qanoon ke hudood mein reh kar zalim ko saza dainay ki koshish karte hain apna haq haasil karne ki sae karte hain magar is koshish mein nakaam honay ki soorat mein depration ka shikaar nahi hotay. himmat nahi hartay. buzdali ka muzahira nahi karte. woh roz-e- Adal  par –apne imaan par qaim rehtay hain aur zindah reh kar zindagi ke masail hal karne ki koshish karte rehtay hain .
kash hamaray Danish  war hazraat masail ke hal ke liye aalam ke parvar-digaar ki utari hui hadaayat se istifada karna shuru kar den. kash un logon ki samajh mein yeh baat aa jaye ke khaaliq ko nazar andaaz kar ke makhlooq ke masail hal nahi kiye ja satke. kash masail o masaaib mein payghambaroon ne jo tareeqa ikhtiyar kya woh usay aam karne ka silsila shuru kar den to hamaray masail mein kuch kami ho sakti hai. bsortِ deegar imkaan hai ke un logon ke tajziyon ke baais masail ki tadaad mein bhi izafah ho ga aur un ki sngini mein bhi .
italy ke dar-al-hakoomat room mein aik cheisat sala buzurag shehri ki wajah se chay so ke qareeb tarkin watan samandar mein doobnay se bach gaye. yeh afraad kashtiyon ke zariye libya se atalwi sahilon ki taraf safar par thay .
atalwi dar-al-hakoomat room se milnay walay khabar rasan idaray ae f pi ki jumaraat ikatees March  ko milnay reporton ke mutabiq aik buzurag atalwi shehri ko aaj hi satellite phone se aik cal masool hui thi. ibtida mein is ne samjha ke yeh koi raang cal thi lekin darasal yeh bahera room mein safar karte hue tarkin watan ki janib se ki gayi aik cal thi jis mein woh madad talabb kar rahay thay .
aik muqami akhbar ke sath guftagu mein italy ke is buzurag shehri ne bataya mujhe aik lafz bhi samajh nahi aa raha tha phone karne wala shakhs angrezi aur francesi zabanon mein baat kar raha tha. mujhe samajh hi nahi aa rahi thi ke woh Ali  alsubah mujh se kya chaah raha hai
bahera room ke rastay libya se italy ki janib mehv safar yeh tarkin watan khulay paanion mein thay aur woh apni jaanen bachanay ke liye madad ke tallab-gaar thay isi liye woh baar baar phone kar rahay thay. buzurag shakhs ko pehlay to yeh baat samajh nahi aayi lekin jab usay baar baar phone aata raha to is ne aakhir-kaar police ko shikayat kar di .
police ahelkaar jab is atalwi bashinday ke ghar puhanche to is douran usay dobarah phone aaya. un ehalkaron ne bataya ke inhen phone par samandar ke pani taiz sun-hwa aur kashti ke engine ki aawazian sunai day rahi theen is liye inhen فورإ andaza ho gaya ke yeh darasal
is par police ne فورإ mulki coastguards ko ittila di jinhon ne satellite phone ka maqam ka taayun kar ke madadgaar kashtiyan wahan bhaij den. coastguards jab khulay samandar mein is maqam tak puhanche to inhen tarkin watan ki paanch kashtiyan dikhayi den jin mein chay so ke qareeb panah Guzeen  sawaar thay .
phone karne walay tarik watan ne bataya ke woh log libya se italy ke safar par niklay thay lekin bahera room ke paanion mein gum ho gaye. is shakhs ne mukhtalif atalwi nambaron par phone karna shuru kar diya lekin kisi ne jawab nah diya. aakhir is buzurag shakhs ne aisi hi aik cal wusool kar li thi .
atalwi sahili muhafizon ke mutabiq unhon ne haliya dinon ke douran pandrah so se zayed panah gzinon ko samandar mein doobnay se bachaya hai. turkey se yunan aur phir wahan se maghribi Europe  pounchanay ke rastay band ho jane ke baad bahera room ke rastay shumali africi mumalik bilkhushoos libya se italy ki janib ghairqanooni safar ke rujhan mein izafah sun-hwa hai .

mein roznama Pakistan  Islamabad ke mudeer aala banay aur Pakistani  sahaafat ke sab se kam Umar  mudeer honay ka aizaz haasil kya. mein aik baar phir inhen Pakistani  Wazeer e Azam  par bad unwani par roznama Pakistan  par mukalama likhnay par –apne mansab se subukdosh hona para. mein roznama Awsaf  Islamabad ke baani mudeer banay .

unhon ne kaha aaj kal kayi shadian ghalat wajohaat ke baais toot rahi hain aur logon ke paas aik dosray ko dainay ke liye waqt nahi hota isi liye Priyanka  is waqt shadi karen gi jab un ke paas –apne rishte ko nibhanay aur samajhney ke liye waqt ho ga un ka mazeed kehna tha ke shadi ka faisla Priyanka  khud hi karen gi
aik sawal ke jawab mein un ka kehna tha ke Priyanka  ki bohat barri madah hon mein khud is ka kayi martaba aatograf le chuki hon lekin is ke sath sath mein is ke kaam ki aik bohat barri naqaad bhi hon .
mein ne is mazmoon ka unwan matan hadees mein ulma ke تصرفات baandha tha. lafz tasarruf ke maienay maamla karna ultana palatna istemaal mein lana waghera ke atay hain. dour tadween se aaj tak hadees ke sath hum ne jo kuch kya hai tasarruf hi is ke bayan ke liye aik acha lafz hai lekin baaz logon ne mera pehla mazmoon parh kar yeh ta-assur bayan kya hai ke is lafz mein aik sakhti hai woh yeh ke is se yeh ta-assur peda hota hai ke شایدعلما ne jantay بوجھتے aisa kya hai. lughwi aitbaar se yeh lafz nah manfi hai aur nah misbet. un mazameen mein mera maqsad ulma ki تنقیص nahi hai nah mein ne usay is qisam ke kisi manfi maqsad ke liye likha hai. is liye mein ne is mazmoon ka unwan tabdeel kar diya hai aur unwan mein se ulma ka lafz nikaal diya hai .
mein ne –apne mazmoon ki pehli qist aur is qist mein bhi yahi baat arz ki hai ke yeh تصرفات bayan o hekiyaat ka fitri taqaza hain راویوں aur ulma ne yeh jaan boojh kar nahi kiye. ulma ka lafz is liye istemaal kya gaya tha ke is mein rawah hadees ke sath sath Sufia  محدثین فقہا شارحین mfsrin aur musanifeen sab shaamil thay un ke liye ulma hi ki tabeer sab se ziyada mozoon thi. behar haal kisi bhi qisam ki ghalat fehmi ko zael karne ke liye yeh zaroori tha ke mein is ke unwan mein tabdeeli kardoon. ab yeh mazmoon isi unwan se chupay ga taaank_h is mein kisi qisam ki koi khata samnay aajay .
is silsilay ke mazameen ke do hissay hain aik تصرفات ke bayan ka aur dosra maslay ki tojeeh ka. wazeh rahay ke yeh dosra hissa mere un mazameen ka laazmi hissa nahi hai. is dosray hissay yani tojeeh o tozeeh ke liye un mazameen mein mera usool yeh hai ke agar mein mukhtalif darjay ki ahadees se akhaz o istifada karoon ga to is mein koi bhi hadees husn ya husn لغیرہ ke darjay se neechay ki nah ho yani yeh ke un ahadees ko mein is usool par lon ke kam azkam sahih tar ahadees mein un mazameen ki taied aur bunyaad mojood ho aur yeh bhi meri koshish hogi ke isi hadees se استشہاد karoon jisay kisi nah kisi Muhaddas  ne qabil e ehtijaj qarar diya ho mein apni raye par is ko munhasir nahi karoon ga. Albata  تصرفات ke bayan mein sahih o zaeef ka imtiaz mere khayaal mein zaroori nahi hai is liye ke yeh bhi tasarruf hi ki aik soorat hai. aur is liye bhi ke un zaeef حدیثوں ko hadees ki hesiyat nah bhi den aik tareekhi dastawizi hesiyat to unhein haasil hai hi is liye tasarruf ke tehat to usay laya ja sakta hai. mazeed yeh ke zaeef riwayaat ka wujood aur un ko kitabon mein likhna bazat khud aik tasarruf hai yani bawajood zeaf sanad ke usay kisi majmoa hadees mein darj کرناوغیرہ aqval rasool par aik tasarruf hi to hai. isi terhan is mein bhi shuba nahi hai ke ummat ka aik bara tabqa zaeef ahadees se اخذو istifada karta hai. jis mazmoon par ishraaq ke adarie mein tabsarah sun-hwa is mein بحمد Allah  aik bhi riwayat is usool se hati hui nahi hai jisay mein ne oopar bayan kya hai .
isi terhan baaz ahbaab ne kaha ke tumahra mazmoon jadeed taleem Yafta  logon ke liye khasa mushkil tha un ki aasani ke liye mein ne hasb zaroorat mushkil alfaaz ke angrezi mutradif day diye hain .

ابوسعید خدری razi Allah  anho se riwayat hai ke nabi akram sale Allah  alaihi wasallam eid al-adha ya eid fittar parhanay ke liye aydgah ki taraf niklay to aap aurton ke parao se guzray aap ne farmaya ae عورتو Allah  ki raah mein kharch kya karo kyunkay mein ne dekha hai ke tum aurtain ziyada dozakh mein jao gi. aurton ne poocha ya rasool Allah  aisa kyun hai aap ne farmaya is liye ke tum laan ta'an ziyada karti ho aur shohar aur azeezon ka kufran Nemat  karti ho. mein ne naaqis aqal Wadin  cheezon mein se tum aurton se ziyada taiz koi cheez nahi dekhi jo sahib Hazam  mardon ki aqal maoof kar deti ho. to unhon ne kaha ae rasool Allah  aurat ke is deen o aqal ke nuqs se kya morad hai توفرمایا kya aurat ki gawahi mard ki gawahi se aadhi nahi hai to aurton ne kaha haan aisa hi hai to aap ne farmaya yeh aurat ki kam aqli hai. kya aisa nahi hai ke jab woh haiz se hoti hai to nah namaz parh sakti hai aur nah rozay rakh sakti hai aurton ne kaha haan aisa hi hai. aap ne farmaya to yeh un ke deen ki kami hui .

. masnad الحمیدی mein yeh hadees yun naqal hui hai jis mein aurton ke is sawal ka mukhatib bhi hazrat Abdul  Allah  hi ko banaya gaya hai. jis se mazeed wazeh ho jata hai ke yeh alfaaz nabi akram ke nahi hain
Abdul  Allah  ban masood razi Allah  anho se riwayat hai ke nabi akram sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ne aurton ke giroh se farmaya ae عورتو Allah  ki raah mein kharch kya karo khuwa –apne zewraat hi dena parrin kyunkay tum aurtain ziyada dozakh mein jao gi. aik kam hesiyat aurat khari hui aur boli ya rasool Allah  aisa kyun hai aap ne farmaya is liye ke tum laan ta'an ziyada karti ho aur shohar aur azeezon ka kufran Nemat  karti ho .
phir hazrat Abdul  Allah  ne kaha naaqis aqal Wadin  cheezon mein se duniya mein aurton se ziyada تیزکوئی cheez nahi hai jo sahib aqal o raye mardon par ghalba pa kar un ke kamon se unhein ghaafil kar sakti ho. to kaha gaya ae ابوعبد al-rehman aurat ke is deen o aqal ke nuqs se kya morad hai to hazrat Abdul  Allah  ne kaha aqal ke nuqs se morad aik mard ki gawahi ke barabar do aurton ki gawahi hai. aur aurat ke deen ke nuqs se morad yeh hai ke woh baaz dinon mein namaz ka aik sajda bhi nahi kar sakti .
abbu Huraira  razi Allah  anho se riwayat hai ke nabi akram sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ne logon ko khutba diya unhein nsihtin kee phir farmaya ae عورتو tum Allah  ki raah mein kharch kya karo kyunkay tum dozakh mein ziyada jao gi. aurton mein se aik boli aisa kyun hai ya rasool Allah  aap ne farmaya tumhari laan ta'an ki kasrat ki wajah se yani shohar aur aazh ki na shukri ki wajah se. farmaya mein ne naaqis aqal o deen cheezon mein se tum se ziyada sahib raye o Danish  mardon ki aqal par chaane wali koi cheez nahi dekhi. un mein se aik aurat ne kaha deen aur aqal ke nuqs se kya morad hai unhon ne kaha yeh ke do aurtain gawahi mein aik mard ke barabar hain aur deen ki kami yeh hai ke haiz tum sab ko kam az kam teen chaar dinon tak namaz se rokay rakhta hai .
chunancha pehlay aur dosray nuktay ko mila krbat bohat mazboot ho jati hai ke yeh izafah darasal Ibn  masood razi Allah  anho ki baat hai jisay baad ke راویوں ne ghalat tor par nabi akram se mansoob kar diya tha .
. bohat si kutub mein yeh riwayat bohat mukhtasir hai. yani unhon ne Abdul  Allah  ban masood ke kalaam wala hissa naqal nahi kya hai. yeh bhi aik taedi ishara hai ke yeh jumla nabi akram sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ka nahi hai balkay abdullah Ibn  masood ka hai jo asal riwayat ka hissa hi nahi tha. koi yeh keh sakta hai ke yeh Daleel  nahi hai lekin oopar ki Sarih  riwayaat ke baad yeh bilashuba aik Qawi  qareena ban jata hai. isi terhan yeh bhi maloom hota hai ke is jawab ke tum khawand ki na shukri karti ho ke baad mazeed sawalaat bhi nahi kiye gaye bas aurton ne khairaat mein zewraat dainay shuru kar diye
jabir ban Abdul  Allah  razi Allah  anho se riwayat hai ke mein aik eid par nabi akram sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ke sath tha aap ne namaz khtbe se pehlay parhai jis ke liye nah azaan di gayi aur nah Iqamat  kahi gayi. phir aap bilal razi Allah  anho ka sahara le kar kharray hue aap ne Allah  se darnay ka hukum diya Allah  ki itaat par ubhara logon ko naseehat ki achi baton ki yaddehani ki phir aap wahan se chal diye aur aurton ki jagah par aaye aap ne unhein bhi waaz o naseehat ki aur farmaya Allah  ki raah mein kharch kya karo kyunkay tum mein se aksar dozakh ka eendhan ban'nay wali ho. aik siyah galoon wali ghareeb tabqa ki aurat khari hui اوربولی kyun ya rasool Allah  aap ne farmaya is liye ke tum shikayaat bohat karti ho aur shoharon aur aazh ki na shukri karti ho. hazrat jabir kehte hain ke phir aurtain –apne zewraat raah e kkhuda mein dainay lagen aur woh hazrat bilal ki chadar mein apni balian aur anghutiyaan daalnay lagen .
. mere aik sarsari استقصا se yeh baat samnay aayi hai ke hjri se pehlay wafaat panay walay محدثین ki kutub mein un riwayaat mein yeh alfaaz mojood nahi hain is ka matlab yeh hai ke yeh baad mein kahin izafah hue hain. maslan abbu dawod طیالسی ki masnad hamidi ki masnad Ibn  الجعد ki masnad Ibn  abi شیبہ ki musannif waghera mein yeh alfaaz mojood nahi hain. lagta hai ke Ibn  masood razi Allah  anho ka yeh jumla aahista aahista nabi akram se nisbat pa gaya. nabi sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ki nisbat se sab se pehlay yeh alfaaz salmi ki kitaab adab Alnisa  mein mlitay hain
mere استقصا ki had tak hazrat zainab yani zoja Abdul  Allah  Ibn  masood ne ناقصات aqal wala jumla naqal hi nahi kya jo barah e raast is waqea ki Shahid  theen. sahih bukhari ومسلم ki mazkoorah baala riwayaato se yeh bhi maloom hota hai ke شایدنبی akram sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ne sadqa o khairaat par ubhaarne ki yeh baat hazrat zainab hi ko dekh kar shuru ki thi kyunkay aap sahib sarwat khatoon theen. is liye agar woh ناقصات aqal wali baat kisi riwayat mein nahi btatin to is ke maienay yeh hain ke yeh baat nabi pak ne ki hi nahi .
. ناقصات aqal o deen ki tozeeh wala jumla sayaq o Sabaq  se mil nahi khata. jab aurat ki takhleeq hi is terhan se hui hai ke woh aqal mein naaqis hai. woh is پیدایشی nuqs ke sabab se mard ki aqal par asar andaaz hoti hai to is ka to qasoor hi nah sun-hwa is liye ke is ka yeh پیدایشی nuqs is ke liye izr hai. usay aik cheez ki samajh hi nahi hai to woh mujrim kis terhan se hui. jurm to tab tha ke woh mukammal aqal o shaoor ki maalik honay ke baad aisa karti. is liye dozakh mein aurton ke ziyada honay ki wajah na qabil feham hai .
yeh baat deen ke Musalmah  usoolon aur quran o sunnat ke qatee نصوص
wazeh rahay ke ghulam aurat ko zina ki aadhi saza di gayi hai is liye ke muashray mein is ke maqam ki wajah se usay is darja ka احصان vthfz haasil nahi tha jo azad aurat ko haasil tha. lehaza is ki saza to kam ho gayi lekin aik aurat jo kkhuda ki taraf se thi hi naaqis aqal usay baaz cheeze samajh hi nahi aasktin to is ki saza kam kyun nah hui had yeh hai ke tamam juraim mein aurat ko mard ke barabar saza di gayi hai. maslan chori ki saza mein aap sale Allah  alaihi wasallam hi ne fatima Nami  aurat ke haath bhi katay hain. kyun yeh baat is waqt paish e nazar nah rahi ke woh naaqis al-aqal hai
deen ke tamam ehkaam se saabit hai ke aurat mard hi ki terhan deen ki poori poori mklf hai. مثلادونوں irtikaab shirk par dozakh mein jayen ge agar aurat kam aqal hai to usay to samajh hi nahi aaye gi ke shirk kya hai aur kya nahi hai phir saza kis baat ki waghera. lehaza hadees ke matan par yeh izafah deen ki baqi tamam talemaat ki nifi karta hai. jin ka مدارقطعی نصوص par hai. lehaza ادرست baat yeh hai ke un ke ziyada dozakh mein jane ka sabab yahi hona chahiye ke un ko aqal o shaoor to poora poora hai lekin is ke hotay hue woh mardon ke muqablay mein ziyada gunah karti hain aur un ki aqal par haawi ho kar un ko gunaaho par abharti hain .
. jis nuqs deen o aqal ki baat is riwayat mein ki gayi hai woh nuqs kehlanay ka mojab nahi hai. haiz ke dinon mein namaz nah parhna aur gawahi ka aadha hona kisi terhan nuqs bemani khata nahi hai. khud Sanie  fitrat ne jis cheez ko jaisa takhleeq kya ho woh nah nuqs hai aur nah dosh diye jane ka sabab .
khud Shariat  ya sanie fitrat ne jis cheez ko muqar riya takhleeq kya ho woh nuqs mojab saza nahi ho sakta. maslan aik gungay aadmi ko is baat par کافرنہیں kaha ja sakta ke woh tasdeeq باللسان nahi kar sakta. aurton ke liye deen hi yeh hai ke woh un dinon mein namaz nah parheen. un ka aisa karna hi kaamil itaat Ellahi hai. woh aurat to naaqis deen hai jo طہرکے dinon mein namaz nah parhay. lekin woh aurat naaqis deen kaisay ho sakti hai jo kkhuda ke hukum hi ki wajah se chand makhsoos dinon mein namaz nah parhay. lehaza yeh tabsarah bhi bar mehal nahi hai. aqal o deen mein naaqis hona riayat ki wajah to ho sakta hai dozakhi honay ki wajah nahi ho sakta .
. isi terhan jin naqais ka zikar sun-hwa hai woh kisi ki aqal ki kami par kaisay Dalalat  karta hai kya haiz mein namaz nah parhnay se aqal mutasir hoti hai ya gawahi aadhi honay se nabi akram sale Allah  alaihi wasallam ne –apne aik sahabi ki gawahi ko do admion ke barabar qarar diya tha to kya baqi tamam sahaba abbu baker o Umar  balkay خلفاے Rashida  samait sab sahaba navz billah un ke muqablay mein naaqis al-aqal thay abbu baker ki صدیقیت Umar  ki فاروقیت usmaan ki haya Ali  ki qaza Ibn  masood ki قرآنیت Ubaida  ban aljrah ki amana الأمہ — razi Allah  عنہم ورضوا anho — waghera un do gwahyon walay aik sahabi ke muqablay mein kya thareen ge gawahi ke kam ya ziyada honay ka koi talluq aqal o baseerat se nahi hai. saari ummat janti hai ke un do gwahyon walay sahabi hazrat Khuzaima  ke muqablay mein خلفاے Rashida  — rizwan Allah  allahum اجمعین — ka maqam o martaba ziyada hai halan ke un sab ki gawahi Khuzaima  ke muqablay mein aadhi thi. haqeeqat yeh hai ke quran Majeed  ne bhi gawahi ki bunyaad aqal ki kami Beshi  par nahi rakhi balkay adalat aur bhool chowk se mubara honay par rakhi hai taakay gawahi mein shubhat nah rahen. yeh dono umoor aisay hain ke mard o aurat barabar hain .

Pakistan  ne roos ke khilaaf be sar o samani ke bawajood Afghanistan ki madad ki .

Imran  Khan  ko yeh parwah bhi nahe hoti thi ke woh bahar jatay hue kaisay lag rahay hain jab mere ghar walay bahar jatay hain to mujhe har waqt un ki fikar lagi rehti hai. Imran  Khan  ka frige khoola to woh bhi khaali thi un ka ziyada guzara daal daliya par tha aik larka kitcehn mein kaam karta tha aur woh bhi ziada waqt TV hi daikhta rehta tha .
Imran  bachon ko –apne paas ziyada pasand nahe karte thay is liye mein ne –apne bachon ko aik kamray tak mahsor kar liya tha woh kitcehn tak bhi nahe jatay thay. hamaray bed room mein to har waqt kuttay ghse rehtay thay balkay aik kuttay ko to mujh se pyar bhi ho gaya tha .

Sindh  mein Nawaz  shareef ke ittihadi kaafi arsay se naraaz hain magar unhon ne abhi tak khil kar Nawaz  shareef se allag honay ka elaan bhi nahi kya hai naraaz rehnumao mein muslim league national peoples party ki qayadat muslim league ke baaghi rehnuma aur sabiq wazraye aala Sindh  dr arbab ghulam Raheem  syed Ghaus  Ali  Shah  sardar mumtaz bhutto Liaqat  Ali  jtoyi aur deegar shaamil hain. agar yeh sab Nawaz  shareef se ittehaad ke khatmay ka elaan kar ke oppostion ke sath shaamil hotay hain to phir Nawaz  shareef ke liye aik aur mushkil khari ho sakti hai. isi terhan dehi Sindh  mein peoples party ke liye bhi mushkilaat ka sabab ban satke hain. agarchay abhi tak Sindh  democratic alayns ka nishana peoples party rahi hai magar is mein wifaqi hukoomat ki janib se koi madad nah milnay par alayns ke log kaafi naraaz hain. mubasireen ke mutabiq mojooda halaat mein Wazeer e Azam  miyan Mohammad  Nawaz  shareef dohri mushkil mein phas gaye hain. peoples party ki qayadat agarchay bilawal bhutto Zardari  ko siyasi tor par samnay le aayi hai magar qanooni tor par parlimani jamaat ki qayadat aur party ke andar aaj bhi faisla kin hesiyat Asif  Ali  Zardari  ko haasil hai yahi wajah hai ke baaz mawaqay par dono baap betay ki policion mein tazaad bhi nazar aata hai. dar asal peoples party ke beshtar rehnumao ki koshish hai ke bilawal be nazeer bhutto ka Farzand  honay ke sath sath fi al haal siyasi ilzamaat se pak hai aur awaami satah par un ko maidan mein utaar kar awaami himayat haasil ki jaye aur kaarkunon ki خوائش bhi yahi hai taham back dor aur haqeeqi فیصلو n ka ikhtiyar sabiq saddar Zardari  ke paas honay ki wajah se aik bara tabqa nakhush bhi hai. mubasireen ke mutabiq yeh silsila ziyada der nahi chal sakay ga kyunkay bilawal bhutto Zardari  bhi is ko mehsoos kar rahay hain aur agar unhon ne kalie tor par party ko control karne ka faisla kya to sabiq saddar Asif  Ali  Zardari  ke liye kaafi mushkil hogi. Sindh  mein is ke kuch assaar nazar آنابھی shuru bhi hue hain. peoples party ke chairman bilawal bhutto Zardari  ne soobay mein tanzeem no ke liye senior sobai wazeer Nisar  Ahmed  کھوڑوکی sarbarahi mein Sindh  کوارڈینیشن committee tashkeel di hai jis mein Wazeer e Aala Sindh  ke musheer baraye siyasi umoor rashid Hussain  Rabbani  Wazeer e Aala Sindh  ke musheer baraye mehakma it-tila-aat Sindh  maula bakhash chandio senior sobai وزیرسید morad Ali  Shah  aur rukan qaumi assembly Nafisa  Shah  hain committee ne mah ke andar mushawarat ka amal mukammal karna hai. it-tila-aat ke mutabiq committee ko soobay mein kaafi sakht radd amal ka saamna hai. is zimn mein Haider  abad mein nakhushgawaar waqea bhi paish aaya jab tanzeem no ke mamlaat par senior sobai wazeer syed morad Ali  Shah  aur Wazeer e Aala Sindh  ke Muawin  khusoosi عبدالجبارخان mein nah sirf talkh kalami hui balkay maamla garibanoo tak pahonch gaya isi terhan deegar azlaa mein bhi kaafi mushkilaat paish aa rahi hain ghaliban yahi wajah hai ke committee ne apna kaam fi al haal moakhar kar diya hai. zaraye ke mutabiq bilawal bhutto Zardari  ka hukum hai ke nazar ‫at‬ logon ko zimma daari di jaye magar nazriati aur puranay kaarkunon ko shikayat hai ke committee baar baar partiyan badalny walon ko aik martaba phir musallat karna charhi hai agar kaarkunon ka yeh ilzaam durust hai to phir sawal yeh peda hota hai ke kya committee yeh sab kuch apni marzi se kar rahi hai ya kisi aur ka hukum hai
isi terhan peoples party ke rehnumao aur kaarkunon ki aik barri tadaad baldeati idaron ke intikhabi amal mein takhirki bhi party ke hkmran group ko samjhti hai. jin ka muaqqaf hai ke hukoomat danista tor par takheeri harbe istemaal kar rahi hai. majmoi tor par peoples party ki qayadat ne Pakistan  peoples party پارلمینٹرینز aur Pakistan  peoples party aik sath chalanay ki koshish kar rahi hai مگرتو uge chal kar is se masail peda ho satke hain aur baeed ne nahi ke siyasat ki be rehmi baap aur betay ko siyasi rastay judda karne par majboor kar day waisay bhi musalmanoon ki tareekh mein Iqtidaar  ki jung mein baap betay ke کردارکچھ ziyada misali nahi rahay hain is liye peoples party ko yeh faisla kar ke Pakistani  awam ko yeh batana hoga ke asal party kon si hai aur ba ikhtiyar quied bilawal بھٹوزرداری ya Asif  Ali  Zardari  hain
haier education commission ne haal hi mein apni Website par ghair ilhaaq shuda idaron ki list jari ki hai jis mein sargodha university se munsalik sab کیمپسز ko bhi bogus qarar diya gaya hai .
jari kardah list ke serial number par sargodha university ke mandarja zail کیمپسز ko ghair ilhaaq shuda bataya gaya hai
each e si ki Website pay yeh list is link par dekhi ja sakti hai
zaraye ke mutabiq un کیمپسز mein taleem ka miyaar bilkul nahi tha public private policy ke tehat yeh کیپمسز ka maqsad sirf aur sirf پیسہبن chuka tha jis ki bana pay each e si ne yeh ahem qadam uthaya taham jo talba o talbat zair-e taleem hain un ke liye koi bhi hikmat glandorf amli ka tarteeb nah diya jana aik sangeen masla hai. jis ka fori hal zaroori hai .

awaami samaji halqon aur walidain ne wazeer aala Punjab  cheif secretary secretary education chairman haier education commission aur cheif justice Supreme Court of Pakistan  se maamla ki nazakat ka notice letay hue talba vtalbat ke qeemti saal aur un ke walidain ke rupoo ke zeyaa ko roknay ke liye iqdamaat karnay ki appeal ki hai .
is waqt duniya mein aik taraqqi Yafta  fard ke muqablay mein chay pas mandah afraad mojood hain. mojooda sarmaya daarana nizaam is terhan se tarteeb diya gaya hai ke yeh chay pas mandah afraad musalsal mehnat karen aur –apne aap ko pas mandah rakhen to tab yeh aik fard taraqqi Yafta  bhi rahay aur muashi aitbaar se mutmaen aur khush haal bhi. yeh chay afraad khaam maal bhi peda karte hain aur taraqqi Yafta  duniya ki banai hui cheeze mehangay damon khareed kar inhen istemaal bhi karte hain aur –apne difaa ke liye bhi inhen maghrib hi par takiya karna parta hai lehaza aik aitbaar se yeh sab maghrib ke halqa ghulami mein shaamil hain. ab agar kisi wajah se technology ki muntaqili amal mein aaye aur science aur industry par maghrib ki ajarah daari khatam ho to maghrib ko dar hai ke is ka azeem miyaar zindagi barqarar nahi reh sakay ga lehaza woh chahta hai ke yahan stits ko
isi maqsad ko haasil karne ke liye maghrib ne aik aur hikmat e amli se bhi kaam liya hai. woh yeh ke maghrib ne tamam pas mandah mumalik mein apna aik mamnon ahsaan mara-aat Yafta  tabqa peda kar diya hai jis ki wajah se maghrib ko ab yahan –apne mafadaat par nazar rakhnay ki bhi zaroorat nahi balkay yeh mara-aat Yafta  tabqa is ke tamam maqasid poooray kar raha hai. is maqsad ko haasil karne ke liye maghrib ne teesri duniya ke hukmraanon ko dil khol kar qarzay diye .
yeh qarzay jaan boojh kar aisi mdon ke liye diye gaye ke is ka sara faida brsraqtdar tabqay ko puhanche aur is ke zariye sarmaya daaron ki aik class wujood mein aajay aur awam ko is ka faida nah honay ke barabar ho. un qarzon ke sath rishwat aur maghribi mumalik ke doroon ka aik programme bhi tarteeb diya gaya taakay yeh tabqa maghrib se mashooor o maroob ho kar hamesha is ke gun gaaye aur har muamlay mein rahnumai ke liye un ki taraf dekhe. is wajah se is naye tabqay ka miyaar zindagi –apne hi malik ke awam ke muqablay mein itna ouncha ho gaya ke ab woh is mein kisi kami ka tasawwur bhi nahi kar satke aur woh is nateejay tak puhanche hain ke ab agar un ko ba-hasiat tabqa apna miyaar zindagi barqarar رکھناہے to is ke liye yeh zaroori hai ke woh –apne awam ko taraqqi ke smrat nah pounchanay den un ko hamesha mahroom aur apna dast nagar rakhen. chunancha maghrib ka agent pas mandah mumalik ka srbraavrd_h tabqa –apne tareekhi farz ko bah tareeq Ahsen  poora kar raha hai. yahi wajah hai ke sarmaya daarana nizaam jis ki kookh se maghrib mein falahi mmlkton ke behtareen nizaam ne janam liya hamaray yahan falahi mmlkton ki pidaaish
maghrib ne –apne is jaal ko mazeed phelaya aur is srbraavrd_h tabqay ko mustaqil tor par hukmaran rakhnay ke liye yahan aik aisay andaaz jamhoriat ko rivaaj diya jis mein hizab e ikhtilaaf aur hizab Iqtidaar  dono atraaf se yahi tabqay samnay ayen. –apne liye to unhon ne aam tor par mutanasib numaindagi ka nizaam pasand kya magar yahan halqa bandion par mabni aik aisa nizaam banaya gaya jis mein election larnay ke akhrajaat itnay ziyada ho jatay hain ke bohat barray barray sarmaya daaron aur jageerdaroon ke ilawa koi fard is ka soch bhi nahi sakta. zahir hai ke yeh afraad jis taraf se bhi ayen ge –apne hi tabqay ke mafadaat ka tahaffuz karen ge. baaz auqaat Mutwast  tabqay se talluq rakhnay walay kuch afraad bhi assembly mein pahonch jatay hain magar un ke peechay sarmaya daaron ki labyan kaam karti hain lehaza yeh afraad parliment mein pahonch kar wohi kuch karne par majboor hotay hain jo un ko agay laane wali labyan chahti hain .
halqa bandion ke is tareeq car se saaray malik mein senkron chhootey chhootey kkhuda ban jatay hain jin ke saaray mafadaat is poooray nizaam se wabasta hotay hain. chunancha yeh tamam kkhuda logon ke mamooli mamooli masail hal karte hue inhen nizaam ki tabdeeli ki baat se ghaafil rakhtay hain lehaza dhancha aur nizaam tabdeel hue baghair jamhoriat ka aik dhong jari rehta hai aur do barri partiyon mein kisi ke bhi brsraqtdar anay ki soorat mein un ke maghribi aaqaon ko koi khatrah darpaish nahi hota. bakol Iqbal
chunancha maghrib ki is hikmat e amli ke aitbaar se pas mandah mumalik mein teen group ban jatay hain. aik mustaqil hukmraanon
maghrib ki is hikmat e amli ka nateeja yeh nikla hai ke aaj pas mandah aqwam ki hakoomaten yahan ki siyasat yahan ki maeeshat aur yahan ka difaa sab kuch maghrib ke hathon girwi hai. yeh bhi zaroori nahi ke un tamam tabqaat ko maghribi mafadaat poooray karne ke –apne kirdaar ka shaoor ho balkay mehez yeh khauf ke kahin tabdeeli aakar sab kuch jala kar bhasam nah kar day aur un ka miyaar zindagi gir nah jaye un ko is poooray nizaam ko barqarar rakhnay par amaada karta hai. is terhan mashriq mein falahi jamhoori aur mazboot mmlkton ka khawab sharminda tabeer nahi honay paata .

nabi kareem? ne irshad farmaya ke jung ka maqsad dushman ka jismani tor par khtama karna nahi hai jadeed bain al aqwami insani falahi qawaneen bhi yeh keh kar ke jung ka maqsad dushman ki jungi taaqat aur jungi istedad ko kamzor karna hona chahiye isi nateejay par puhanche hain ke jo naahi dushman ki jungi istedad kamzor ho jaye hamlon ko rokkk dena chahiye .
jung ke usool وقوانین mein islam ne jo bunyadi islahat ki hain woh yeh hai ke taaqat ke istemaal ko sirf shareek jung tak mehdood kya jaye .
islam ke qanoon jung ka dosra bunyadi usool yeh hai ke qanooni tor par tasleem shuda siyasi hukoomat ki ijazat ke baghair taaqat ke istemaal ki ijazat nahi hai .
islam ke qanoon jung ka taisar usool amli tor par jung mein hissa nah lainay walay afraad se mutaliq hai tibbi imdaad dainay walay aur isi qabeel ke dosray afraad hatta ke agroh jungjuon aur hamla awaron ko madad bhi faraham kar rahay hon inhen jung mein shareek afraad ka hissa nahi samjha jata riayat nah sirf tib se mutaliqa logon ko di gayi hai balkay dosra imdadi amlah jin mein nrsin khidmat gaar khana pakka ne walay shehri zaroriat ki farahmi karne walay bohat Umar  Raseedah  sipahi aur woh boorhay afraad jo jung mein hissa nah le rahay hon bhi is riayat mein shaamil hain un sab afraad ko qatal se mustasna qarar diya gaya hai .
choutha usool yeh hai ke koi aisa kaam nah kya jaye jis mein dhoka dahi ka Ansar  shaamil ho quran pak ki bohat si ayaat hain jin mein dhoka dahi aur kisi cheez ko hatta ke dushman ke samnay bhi ghalat andaaz mein paish karne se mana kya gaya hai .
بنونظیرنے Ayyaam sulah mein moahida aman ke bawajood پیغمبراسلامﷺ? ko shaheed kar ne ki napak koshish ki jis ke ro se un ko madinah mein rehne ki gunjaish khatam hui to inhen sirf jala watan kya gaya. بنوقریظہ ne haalat jung mein is terhan ka ghadar kya aur tamam musalmanoon ko naist vnabod karne ki saz-baaz ki چانچہ un ke sirf mardon ko un ke muqarrar kardah hukum Saad  ban Maaz  ke kehnay پرتہ tegh kya gaya. garam taqub ki istilaah mein agar dekha jaye to yeh ain insaaf hai is shareer qoum se tang aakar hitler ne kya kya tha woh aap ke samnay hai .
hazrat abbu Baseer  aur hazrat abbu Jandal  ke waqeat mashhoor ومعروف hain aap? ne Herbi  maahdat ki pasdari ki aik azeem al shan misaal qaim kar ke un dono wapas kya .
hazrat Ali ? ka mashhoor waqea hai ke Ghazwah  khandaq mein aik mauqa prjb woh –apne mad maqabil intehai طاقتوردشمن ko pachhar chuke to unhon ne hazrat Ali ? par neechay se thook diya to woh un se yakdam paray hatt gaye kisi ne poocha hazrat is waqt to aap un ka kaam barri se tamam kar satke thay farmaya meri un se zaati koi dushman nahi hai nah hi hum apni zaat ke liye kisi se intiqam letay hain. isi waqea ke zail mein baaz moar-kheen ne hazrat Ali  ka is jung mein aik aur ajeeb vghrib waqea bhi naqal kya hai ke unhon ne –apne aik Mubarez  ko injaam tak pohanchaya avranki talwar dhaal aur zarah liye baghair khaali haath lautay nabi kareem? ya hazrat umar ke poochnay par bataya un ki sharamgah khil gayi thi mein sharam ke maaray sab kuch chore kar wapas chala aaya. یقینادنیا ki tareekh kisi bhi ghmsan ki jung mein husn ikhlaq ke is kirdaar ka namona paish karne se qassar hai .
dosray khalifa rashid ke zamane mein musalmanoon aur iranio ke mabain jung ho rahi thi aik irani darakht par charh gaya aur is ki chouti par panah le li aik musalman sipahi ne usay pa liya aur farsi mein usay kehnay laga مترس yani mat daro irani fouji yeh samjha ke shayad usay panah aur tahaffuz day dyagyahe chunancha woh neechay اترآیا taham musalman fouji ne usay qatal kar dala hazrat umar ko is muamlay ki khabar di gayi unhon ne aik policy bayan jari kya jis mein unhon ne yahi farsi istilaah istemaal karte hue elaan kya ke agar koi shakhs dushman fouji ko مترس aur baad mein usay qatal karte paaya gaya to is par qatal ka muqadma chalaya jaye ga aur woh sazae mout kahq daar hoga aisay amal ko dosray khalifa rashid ne qatal ke barabar grdana sirf is wajah se ke iraday ko ghalat andaaz mein paish kya gaya yahan dhoka dahi ko is ke lughwi maeno se kahin ziyada wasee kar ke mana kar diya gaya .
musalman hukoomat ne jadeed turkey aur misar ki sarhadoon ke qareeb kahin abad ghair muslim logon se moahida kar liya yeh log musalmanoon ke liye mushkilaat peda kya karte thay khaas tor par woh tijarti qaafley jo arab aur Europe  ke darmiyan safar karte thay yeh inhen lout liya karte Hazr  t- Ameer  muawiya? ne un ke khilaaf qadam uthany ka faisla kya taham musalmanoon ne un se jo moahida کررکھاتھا is mein waqt ki pasdari zaroori thi aur is muahiday mein har saal tosee kar di jati thi un ke khilaaf qadam uthany ke liye khalifa ne intzaar kya yahan tak ke yeh moahida khatam honay ko agaya is muahiday ke khatam honay se aik mah qabal unhon ne tayari ki aur apni kamaan mein fouj ko hukum diya ke woh is ilaqay ki janib paish qadmi karen jahan yeh mushkilaat peda karne walay log rahaish Pazeer  thay un ka khayaal tha ke woh muahiday ki aakhri tareekh tak intzaar karen ge aur phir muahiday mein tosee karne ke bajaye agli hi subah un logon ko saza den ge takneeki lehaaz se qanooni aaeni aur aaj ki zabaan mein bain al aqwami qanoon ki ro say un ka yeh qadam jaaiz hota woh –apne hi ilaqay mein naqal o harkat kar rahay thay aur muahiday ke arsay mein un ke khilaaf koi qadam bhi nahi atharhe thay lekin yeh khalifa ki zaati raye thi aur is par doosron se mushawarat nahi ki gayi thi aik sahabi rasool? عمربن انباسہ? ghoray par sawaar ho kar taizi se is janib barhay jis simt musalman fouj paish qadmi kar rahi thi khalifa ko khabar di gayi ke koi shakhs nazdeek aarhahe jab woh qareeb aaye to dekha gaya ke woh sahabi رسولﷺ Umar  ban ابناسہ? hain jab hazrat عمرنے musalman fouj ko jalya woh zor vshor se chlarhe thay wafa لاغدر apna wada poora karo dhoka dahi ke murtakib nah ho .
khalifa tak pounchanay ke baad unhon ne muahiday ke mutaliq –apne feham aur tabeer ko wazeh kya aur yeh ke khalifa ka yeh qadam kaisay dhoka dahi mein shaamil hai hazrat Umar ? ne kaha ke jab aik musalman riyasat kuch afraad ke sath koi muahiday kar bithti hai to is ka taqaza hai ke bawajood is ke ke un ke iraday dushmani ki janib mael hon par aman رہاجائے trfin ko jazbati tor par par aman rehna chahiye yeh haqeeqat ke aik musalman hukmaran ne maahd qoum ke khilaaf fouji karwai ka socha aur is iraday ke sath apni foujon ko harkat bhi di is ka matlab yeh sun-hwa ke woh muahiday ki asal rooh yani muahiday ke arsay mein par aman rehne ke azm ke khilaaf aik harkat ke murtakib hue .
chunancha musalmanoon ko yeh hukum dyagyahe ke agroh muahiday ko khatam karna chahain to inhen –apne iraday ka elania izhaar karna chahiye taakay dushman mojooda haalat ke baray mein aagah ho jaye aur usay pata chal jaye ke musalman un ke khilaaf koi qadam utha satke hain chunancha woh bhi isi terhan tayyar rahen sirf isi soorat mein musalman un ke khilaaf koi qadam utha satke hain jin ke sath un ka aman ka moahida tha hazrat muawiya? samait musalman fouj ne is tashreeh ko qubool kya aur foran hi –apne iqdamaat ko khatam kar ke Dimashq  wapas rawana hogaye .
